   "source": [
    "# ECSoC Temazepam Within-Subject Analysis\n",
    "## Sleep-EDF Expanded — Sleep Telemetry コホート (N=22, 44夜)\n",
    "\n",
    "### 研究設計\n",
    "- **データ**: ST群44ファイル (22被験者 × 2夜: Temazepam夜 + Placebo夜)\n",
    "- **比較**: Within-subject (同一被験者のT夜 vs P夜)\n",
    "- **主要検定**: Wilcoxon符号順位検定 (n=22, 対応あり)\n",
    "- **根拠**: ST-subjects.xlsに各被験者のTemazepam/Placebo夜割り当てが記載\n",
    "\n",
    "### ECSoC指標\n",
    "- **CHI** = 2(α₁ − α₂): スケール非対称性\n",
    "- **α₁**: 短スケールDFA指数 (0.1–0.4s)\n",
    "- **α₂**: 長スケールDFA指数 (0.8–4.0s)\n",
    "- **R²**: DFAスケーリング適合度\n",
    "- **Phase V**: R² < 0.93 (スケーリング崩壊)\n",
    "- **D_eff_rel**: 相対実効次元 (Fpz-Cz + Pz-Oz, n_ch=2)\n",
    "\n",
    "### ファイル命名規則\n",
    "ST7**ss**N**J0-PSG.edf\n",
    "- ss = 被験者番号 (2桁)\n",
    "- N = 夜番号 (1 or 2)\n",
    "- どちらがT夜/P夜かはST-subjects.xlsで決まる"
   ]
  },

    "ST_SUBJECTS_XLS = os.path.join(SLEEP_EDF_ROOT, 'ST-subjects.xls')\n",
    "OUTPUT_DIR      = os.path.join(DRIVE_ROOT, 'ECSoC_Temazepam_results')\n",
    "os.makedirs(OUTPUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n",
    "\n",
    "# ECSoCパラメータ (100Hz, 30s epoch)\n",
    "FS              = 100\n",
    "WIN_SEC         = 30\n",
    "DFA_S_LO, DFA_S_HI   = 10, 40    # 短スケール: 0.1–0.4s\n",
    "DFA_L_LO, DFA_L_HI   = 80, 400   # 長スケール: 0.8–4.0s\n",
    "DFA_N_SCALES    = 12\n",
    "PHASE_V_THR     = 0.93\n",
    "EEG_CHANNELS    = ['EEG Fpz-Cz', 'EEG Pz-Oz']\n",
    "PRIMARY_CH      = 'EEG Fpz-Cz'\n",
    "\n",
    "STAGE_MAP = {\n",
    "    'Sleep stage W': 'W',\n",
    "    'Sleep stage 1': 'N1',\n",
    "    'Sleep stage 2': 'N2',\n",
    "    'Sleep stage 3': 'N3',\n",
    "    'Sleep stage 4': 'N3',\n",
    "    'Sleep stage R': 'REM',\n",
    "    'Movement time': 'MT',\n",
    "    'Sleep stage ?': 'UNK',\n",
    "}\n",
    "VALID_STAGES = ['W', 'N1', 'N2', 'N3', 'REM']\n",
    "STAGE_ORDER  = ['W', 'N1', 'N2', 'N3', 'REM']\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'ST_DIR   : {ST_DIR}')\n",
    "print(f'  存在: {os.path.exists(ST_DIR)}')\n",
    "print(f'XLS      : {ST_SUBJECTS_XLS}')\n",
    "print(f'  存在: {os.path.exists(ST_SUBJECTS_XLS)}')\n",
    "print(f'OUTPUT   : {OUTPUT_DIR}')"

    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 3: ST-subjects.xlsからTemazepam/Placebo夜割り当てを構築\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# ST-subjects.xlsの構造:\n",
    "#   列0: Subject Nr (1,2,4,5,...,22,24 ※3,23は欠番)\n",
    "#   列1: Age\n",
    "#   列2: Sex (1=M, 2=F)\n",
    "#   列3: Placebo night nr (1 or 2)\n",
    "#   列4: Placebo lights off time\n",
    "#   列5: Temazepam night nr (1 or 2)\n",
    "#   列6: Temazepam lights off time\n",
    "\n",
    "df_subj = pd.read_excel(ST_SUBJECTS_XLS, header=0)\n",
    "\n",
    "# ヘッダ行を除いてデータ部分のみ取得\n",
    "df_subj = df_subj.iloc[1:].reset_index(drop=True)  # 行0はサブヘッダ\n",
    "df_subj.columns = [\n",
    "    'subject_nr', 'age', 'sex',\n",
    "    'placebo_night', 'placebo_lights_off',\n",
    "    'temazepam_night', 'temazepam_lights_off'\n",
    "]\n",
    "df_subj = df_subj.dropna(subset=['subject_nr'])\n",
    "df_subj['subject_nr']      = df_subj['subject_nr'].astype(int)\n",
    "df_subj['placebo_night']   = df_subj['placebo_night'].astype(int)\n",
    "df_subj['temazepam_night'] = df_subj['temazepam_night'].astype(int)\n",
    "df_subj['age']             = df_subj['age'].astype(int)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'被験者数: {len(df_subj)}')\n",
    "print(df_subj[['subject_nr','age','sex','placebo_night','temazepam_night']].to_string(index=False))"
   ]

    "id": "step4_file_mapping"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 4: 被験者ごとのファイルペアを構築\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# ファイル名規則: ST7{ss}{N}J0-PSG.edf\n",
    "#   ss = 被験者番号 (2桁ゼロ埋め)\n",
    "#   N  = 夜番号 (1 or 2)\n",
    "\n",
    "def make_psg_path(st_dir, subject_nr, night_nr):\n",
    "    ss = str(subject_nr).zfill(2)\n",
    "    pattern = os.path.join(st_dir, f'ST7{ss}{night_nr}J0-PSG.edf')\n",
    "    # ハイフン有無・大文字小文字の揺れに対応\n",
    "    candidates = glob.glob(os.path.join(st_dir, f'ST7{ss}{night_nr}*PSG.edf'))\n",
    "    if candidates:\n",
    "        return candidates[0]\n",
    "    return None\n",
    "\n",
    "def make_hyp_path(st_dir, subject_nr, night_nr):\n",
    "    ss = str(subject_nr).zfill(2)\n",
    "    candidates = glob.glob(os.path.join(st_dir, f'ST7{ss}{night_nr}*Hypnogram*.edf'))\n",
    "    if candidates:\n",
    "        return candidates[0]\n",
    "    return None\n",
    "\n",
    "pairs = []  # list of dicts\n",
    "missing = []\n",
    "\n",
    "for _, row in df_subj.iterrows():\n",
    "    nr  = int(row['subject_nr'])\n",
    "    age = int(row['age'])\n",
    "    sex = 'M' if int(row['sex']) == 1 else 'F'\n",
    "    p_n = int(row['placebo_night'])\n",
    "    t_n = int(row['temazepam_night'])\n",
    "\n",
    "    p_psg = make_psg_path(ST_DIR, nr, p_n)\n",
    "    p_hyp = make_hyp_path(ST_DIR, nr, p_n)\n",
    "    t_psg = make_psg_path(ST_DIR, nr, t_n)\n",
    "    t_hyp = make_hyp_path(ST_DIR, nr, t_n)\n",
    "\n",
    "    entry = {\n",
    "        'subject_nr':    nr,\n",
    "        'age':           age,\n",
    "        'sex':           sex,\n",
    "        'placebo_psg':   p_psg,\n",
    "        'placebo_hyp':   p_hyp,\n",
    "        'placebo_night': p_n,\n",
    "        'temaz_psg':     t_psg,\n",
    "        'temaz_hyp':     t_hyp,\n",
    "        'temaz_night':   t_n,\n",
    "    }\n",
    "    pairs.append(entry)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # 欠損チェック\n",
    "    for label, path in [('Placebo PSG', p_psg), ('Placebo HYP', p_hyp),\n",
    "                         ('Temaz PSG',   t_psg), ('Temaz HYP',   t_hyp)]:\n",
    "        if path is None:\n",
    "            missing.append(f'Nr={nr:02d} [{label}]')\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'被験者ペア数: {len(pairs)}')\n",
    "print(f'ファイル欠損: {len(missing)}')\n",
    "if missing:\n",
    "    print('  欠損詳細:')\n",
    "    for m in missing:\n",
    "        print(f'    {m}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('ペアサンプル (最初の3件):')\n",
    "for p in pairs[:3]:\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={p['subject_nr']:02d} Age={p['age']} {p['sex']}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"    Placebo : {os.path.basename(p['placebo_psg']) if p['placebo_psg'] else '❌'} \"\n",
    "          f\"+ {os.path.basename(p['placebo_hyp']) if p['placebo_hyp'] else '❌'}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"    Temaz   : {os.path.basename(p['temaz_psg']) if p['temaz_psg'] else '❌'} \"\n",
    "          f\"+ {os.path.basename(p['temaz_hyp']) if p['temaz_hyp'] else '❌'}\")"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "step5_core_functions"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 5: ECSoCコア計算関数\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "def dfa_ecsoc(x, s_lo=DFA_S_LO, s_hi=DFA_S_HI,\n",
    "              l_lo=DFA_L_LO, l_hi=DFA_L_HI, n_scales=DFA_N_SCALES):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    高速版DFA (v2): ×33高速, オリジナルと数値的に等価 (CHI誤差 < 5e-8)\n",
    "\n",
    "    改善点:\n",
    "    1. fluct()のPythonループ → NumPyベクトル演算 (主要改善)\n",
    "    2. 入力をfloat32に変換してメモリ削減\n",
    "    3. cumsumはfloat64を維持 (float32だと桁落ちリスク)\n",
    "    4. fluct計算: sqrt(mean_k(MSE_k)) ← オリジナルと完全等価\n",
    "\n",
    "    提案版 (dfa_proposed) との違い:\n",
    "    - 提案版は cumsum を float32 のまま行う → CHI誤差 ~2e-5 (許容範囲内だが不要)\n",
    "    - 提案版の rms_per_seg.mean() は mean(sqrt(MSE)) であり sqrt(mean(MSE)) と異なる\n",
    "      → 本版は sqrt(mean(MSE)) でオリジナルと等価を保証\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    x = np.asarray(x, dtype=np.float32)\n",
    "    if len(x) < l_hi * 2:\n",
    "        return None\n",
    "\n",
    "    # cumsum は float64 で実行 (float32では長信号で桁落ちリスクあり)\n",
    "    y = np.cumsum(x.astype(np.float64) - x.mean())\n",
    "\n",
    "    scales_s   = np.unique(np.round(np.geomspace(s_lo, s_hi, n_scales)).astype(np.int32))\n",
    "    scales_l   = np.unique(np.round(np.geomspace(l_lo, l_hi, n_scales)).astype(np.int32))\n",
    "    scales_all = np.unique(np.concatenate([scales_s, scales_l]))\n",
    "\n",
    "    log_s_list, log_F_list = [], []\n",
    "    for s in scales_all:\n",
    "        s = int(s)\n",
    "        n_seg = len(y) // s\n",
    "        if n_seg < 4:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        # セグメントを2D配列に変換 (n_seg, s)\n",
    "        segs = y[:n_seg * s].reshape(n_seg, s)\n",
    "        # 解析的最小二乗: 傾き・切片をベクトル化\n",
    "        t     = np.arange(s, dtype=np.float64)\n",
    "        t_c   = t - t.mean()\n",
    "        t_var = (t_c ** 2).sum()\n",
    "        seg_c      = segs - segs.mean(axis=1, keepdims=True)\n",
    "        slopes     = (seg_c * t_c).sum(axis=1) / t_var\n",
    "        intercepts = segs.mean(axis=1) - slopes * t.mean()\n",
    "        trend      = slopes[:, None] * t + intercepts[:, None]\n",
    "        # ★ sqrt( mean_k( MSE_k ) ) ← オリジナルのfluct()と完全等価\n",
    "        rms = np.sqrt(((segs - trend) ** 2).mean(axis=1).mean())\n",
    "        if np.isfinite(rms) and rms > 0:\n",
    "            log_s_list.append(np.log2(s))\n",
    "            log_F_list.append(np.log2(rms))\n",
    "\n",
    "    log_s = np.array(log_s_list)\n",
    "    log_F = np.array(log_F_list)\n",
    "\n",
    "    if len(log_s) < 6:\n",
    "        return None\n",
    "\n",
    "    mask_s = (2**log_s >= s_lo) & (2**log_s <= s_hi)\n",
    "    mask_l = (2**log_s >= l_lo) & (2**log_s <= l_hi)\n",
    "\n",
    "    if mask_s.sum() < 3 or mask_l.sum() < 3:\n",
    "        return None\n",
    "\n",
    "    a1, _, r_s, _, _ = linregress(log_s[mask_s], log_F[mask_s])\n",
    "    a2, _, r_l, _, _ = linregress(log_s[mask_l], log_F[mask_l])\n",
    "    a_g, _, r_a, _, _ = linregress(log_s,          log_F)\n",
    "\n",
    "    alpha1 = abs(a1)\n",
    "    alpha2 = abs(a2)\n",
    "    alpha_global = abs(a_g)  # ★追加: conventional single-exponent DFA (全域フィット傾き)\n",
    "    return {\n",
    "        'alpha1':       alpha1,\n",
    "        'alpha2':       alpha2,\n",
    "        'alpha_global': alpha_global,  # ★追加\n",
    "        'CHI':          2 * (alpha1 - alpha2),\n",
    "        'R2':           r_a**2,\n",
    "        'R2_s':         r_s**2,\n",
    "        'R2_l':         r_l**2,\n",
    "    }\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_d_eff(X):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    D_eff = (Σλ)² / Σλ² , D_eff_rel = D_eff / n_ch\n",
    "    X: (n_ch, n_samples)\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    n_ch = X.shape[0]\n",
    "    if n_ch < 2:\n",
    "        return np.nan, np.nan\n",
    "    Xc = X - X.mean(axis=1, keepdims=True)\n",
    "    eigvals = np.linalg.eigvalsh(np.cov(Xc))\n",
    "    eigvals = eigvals[eigvals > 1e-12]\n",
    "    if len(eigvals) < 2:\n",
    "        return np.nan, np.nan\n",
    "    D = eigvals.sum()**2 / (eigvals**2).sum()\n",
    "    return D, D / n_ch\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def read_hypnogram(hyp_path):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    Hypnogram.edf → list of (onset_sec, duration_sec, stage_str)\n",
    "\n",
    "    Sleep-EDF STファイルはduration可変アノテーション形式:\n",
    "    同一ステージが連続する区間を1アノテーションにまとめて記録。\n",
    "    例: 'Sleep stage W' onset=0s duration=1560s (= 52エポック分)\n",
    "    mne.read_annotations() で正しく全アノテーションが読める。\n",
    "    mne.io.read_raw_edf().annotations では1件しか取れないため使用不可。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    epochs = []\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        annotations = mne.read_annotations(hyp_path)\n",
    "        for desc, onset, duration in zip(\n",
    "                annotations.description,\n",
    "                annotations.onset,\n",
    "                annotations.duration):\n",
    "            mapped = STAGE_MAP.get(desc, None)\n",
    "            if mapped:\n",
    "                epochs.append((float(onset), float(duration), mapped))\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f'    ⚠️ Hypnogram読み込みエラー: {e}')\n",
    "    return epochs\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t_start):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    duration可変アノテーション対応版。\n",
    "    onset <= t_start < onset + duration のアノテーションを返す。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    for onset, duration, stage in stage_epochs:\n",
    "        if onset <= t_start < onset + duration:\n",
    "            return stage\n",
    "    return 'UNK'\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def process_one_night(psg_path, hyp_path, subject_nr, condition):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    1夜分のPSGを処理してECSoC指標DataFrameを返す\n",
    "    condition: 'Placebo' or 'Temazepam'\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(psg_path, preload=False, verbose=False)\n",
    "        avail = raw.ch_names\n",
    "\n",
    "        # 主チャンネル選択\n",
    "        primary = None\n",
    "        for cand in [PRIMARY_CH] + [c for c in avail if 'EEG' in c.upper()]:\n",
    "            if cand in avail:\n",
    "                primary = cand\n",
    "                break\n",
    "        if primary is None:\n",
    "            print(f'  ⚠️ EEGチャンネルなし [Nr={subject_nr}]')\n",
    "            return None\n",
    "\n",
    "        # D_eff用マルチチャンネル\n",
    "        multi = [c for c in EEG_CHANNELS if c in avail]\n",
    "        if len(multi) < 2:\n",
    "            eeg_all = [c for c in avail if 'EEG' in c.upper()]\n",
    "            multi = eeg_all[:2] if len(eeg_all) >= 2 else eeg_all\n",
    "\n",
    "        picks = list(set(multi + ([primary] if primary not in multi else [])))\n",
    "        raw_loaded = mne.io.read_raw_edf(\n",
    "            psg_path, include=picks, preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "        actual_fs  = int(raw_loaded.info['sfreq'])\n",
    "        win_samp   = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f'  ⚠️ PSG読み込みエラー [Nr={subject_nr} {condition}]: {e}')\n",
    "        return None\n",
    "\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "\n",
    "    sig, times = raw_loaded.get_data(picks=[primary], return_times=True)\n",
    "    sig = sig[0] * 1e6  # V → μV\n",
    "\n",
    "    data_multi = None\n",
    "    if len(multi) >= 2:\n",
    "        data_multi = raw_loaded.get_data(picks=multi) * 1e6\n",
    "\n",
    "    results = []\n",
    "    n_ep = len(sig) // win_samp\n",
    "\n",
    "    for ep in range(n_ep):\n",
    "        t0    = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        i0    = ep * win_samp\n",
    "        i1    = i0 + win_samp\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        x     = sig[i0:i1].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "        # アーティファクト除外\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > 500:\n",
    "            stage = 'ART'\n",
    "\n",
    "        dfa = dfa_ecsoc(x)\n",
    "\n",
    "        d_eff, d_eff_rel = np.nan, np.nan\n",
    "        if data_multi is not None and stage != 'ART':\n",
    "            Xep = data_multi[:, i0:i1].copy()\n",
    "            if np.abs(Xep).max() <= 500:\n",
    "                d_eff, d_eff_rel = compute_d_eff(Xep)\n",
    "\n",
    "        row = {\n",
    "            'subject_nr': subject_nr,\n",
    "            'condition':  condition,\n",
    "            'epoch_idx':  ep,\n",
    "            't_start':    t0,\n",
    "            'stage':      stage,\n",
    "            'actual_fs':  actual_fs,\n",
    "            'D_eff':      d_eff,\n",
    "            'D_eff_rel':  d_eff_rel,\n",
    "        }\n",
    "        if dfa is not None:\n",
    "            row.update(dfa)\n",
    "            row['PhaseV'] = int(dfa['R2'] < PHASE_V_THR)\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            for k in ['alpha1','alpha2','alpha_global','CHI','R2','R2_s','R2_l','PhaseV']:  # ★alpha_global追加\n",
    "                row[k] = np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "        results.append(row)\n",
    "\n",
    "    del raw_loaded\n",
    "    return pd.DataFrame(results)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "print('コア関数定義完了')\n",
    "print(f'  DFA短スケール: {DFA_S_LO}–{DFA_S_HI} samples ({DFA_S_LO/FS:.2f}–{DFA_S_HI/FS:.2f}s)')\n",
    "print(f'  DFA長スケール: {DFA_L_LO}–{DFA_L_HI} samples ({DFA_L_LO/FS:.2f}–{DFA_L_HI/FS:.2f}s)')"
   ]

    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 7b: サンプリングレート整合性チェック\n",

    "#       前提としている。process_one_night() 内で actual_fs は win_samp\n",
    "#       (30秒エポック長) にのみ使われ、DFA窓のサンプル数自体には反映されない。\n",
    "#       そのため、もしどこかのファイルで actual_fs != 100 だった場合、\n",
    "#       DFA窓が意図した実時間 (0.1-0.4s, 0.8-4.0s) からズレたまま、\n",
    "#       警告なく処理されてしまう。ここでは全44夜について actual_fs の値が\n",
    "#       本当に一貫して100であったかを確認する。\n",
    "print('=' * 80)\n",
    "print('[ST群] actual_fs の値の分布')\n",

    "fs_counts = df_all['actual_fs'].value_counts()\n",
    "print(fs_counts)\n",
    "print()\n",

    "expected_fs = FS  # 100\n",
    "n_total = len(df_all)\n",
    "n_match = (df_all['actual_fs'] == expected_fs).sum()\n",
    "n_mismatch = n_total - n_match\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'期待値 FS = {expected_fs} Hz')\n",

    "\n",
    "if n_mismatch == 0:\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "    print('-> 全エポックで actual_fs == 100Hz を確認。')\n",
    "    print('   DFA窓のサンプル数固定 (10-40, 80-400) は実時間 (0.1-0.4s, 0.8-4.0s)')\n",
    "    print('   と正しく対応しており、ハードコードによる窓幅ズレは発生していない。')\n",
    "else:\n",

   "metadata": {
    "id": "step8_per_subject_stage_mean"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 8: 被験者 × 条件 × ステージ の平均値を計算\n",
    "# Within-subject比較の単位はこのレベル\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "valid = df_all[\n",
    "    df_all['stage'].isin(VALID_STAGES) &\n",
    "    df_all['CHI'].notna()\n",
    "].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'有効エポック数: {len(valid):,}')\n",
    "print(f'条件別:')\n",
    "print(valid.groupby('condition')['CHI'].count())\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "# 被験者 × 条件 × ステージ の平均\n",
    "subj_means = valid.groupby(\n",
    "    ['subject_nr', 'condition', 'stage', 'age', 'sex']\n",
    ").agg(\n",
    "    n_epochs     = ('CHI', 'count'),\n",
    "    CHI_mean          = ('CHI', 'mean'),\n",
    "    CHI_sd            = ('CHI', 'std'),\n",
    "    alpha1_mean       = ('alpha1', 'mean'),\n",
    "    alpha2_mean       = ('alpha2', 'mean'),\n",
    "    alpha_global_mean = ('alpha_global', 'mean'),  # ★追加: conventional single-exponent DFA\n",
    "    R2_mean           = ('R2', 'mean'),\n",
    "    PhaseV_rate  = ('PhaseV', 'mean'),\n",
    "    D_eff_rel_mean = ('D_eff_rel', 'mean'),\n",
    ").reset_index()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Placebo / Temazepam をワイド形式に変換 (Within-subject比較用)\n",
    "subj_P = subj_means[subj_means['condition'] == 'Placebo'].copy()\n",
    "subj_T = subj_means[subj_means['condition'] == 'Temazepam'].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "wide = pd.merge(\n",
    "    subj_P.rename(columns=lambda c: c+'_P' if c not in ['subject_nr','stage','age','sex'] else c),\n",
    "    subj_T.rename(columns=lambda c: c+'_T' if c not in ['subject_nr','stage','age','sex'] else c),\n",
    "    on=['subject_nr', 'stage', 'age', 'sex'],\n",
    "    how='inner'\n",
    ")\n",
    "wide['ΔCHI']          = wide['CHI_mean_T'] - wide['CHI_mean_P']\n",
    "wide['ΔD_eff_rel']    = wide['D_eff_rel_mean_T'] - wide['D_eff_rel_mean_P']\n",
    "wide['ΔPhaseV']       = wide['PhaseV_rate_T'] - wide['PhaseV_rate_P']\n",
    "wide['Δalpha_global'] = wide['alpha_global_mean_T'] - wide['alpha_global_mean_P']  # ★追加\n",
    "\n",
    "csv_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'within_subject_wide.csv')\n",
    "wide.to_csv(csv_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'Within-subjectワイドテーブル: {csv_path}')\n",
    "print(f'行数: {len(wide)} (被験者×ステージ組み合わせ)')\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('ΔCHI (Temazepam − Placebo) ステージ別平均:')\n",
    "print(wide.groupby('stage')['ΔCHI'].agg(['mean','std','count']).round(4))"
   ]

  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "step9_wilcoxon"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 9: Within-subject Wilcoxon符号順位検定\n",
    "# メイン統計解析\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "from scipy.stats import wilcoxon, rankdata\n",
    "\n",
    "METRICS = {\n",
    "    'CHI':          ('CHI_mean_P',          'CHI_mean_T',          'ΔCHI'),\n",
    "    'D_eff_rel':    ('D_eff_rel_mean_P',    'D_eff_rel_mean_T',    'ΔD_eff_rel'),\n",
    "    'PhaseV':       ('PhaseV_rate_P',       'PhaseV_rate_T',       'ΔPhaseV'),\n",
    "    'alpha_global': ('alpha_global_mean_P', 'alpha_global_mean_T', 'Δalpha_global'),  # ★追加: conventional single-exponent DFA\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "def rank_biserial_wilcoxon(x, y, zero_method='wilcox'):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    ★修正: Matched-pairs rank-biserial correlation (Kerby 2014)。\n",
    "    従来の r = Z/sqrt(N) 近似は p が極小の時に |r| > 1 となり得る不正な値を\n",
    "    返すことがある(実際にalpha_global N3でr=1.07が発生)。\n",
    "    こちらは常に [-1, 1] に収まる、Wilcoxon符号順位検定に対応した正しい効果量。\n",
    "\n",
    "    r_rb = (W+ - W-) / (W+ + W-)\n",
    "    符号: 正 → x が y より系統的に大きい (ここでは Temazepam > Placebo)\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    d = np.asarray(x) - np.asarray(y)\n",
    "    if zero_method == 'wilcox':\n",
    "        d = d[d != 0]\n",
    "    n = len(d)\n",
    "    if n == 0:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    ranks = rankdata(np.abs(d))\n",
    "    W_pos = ranks[d > 0].sum()\n",
    "    W_neg = ranks[d < 0].sum()\n",
    "    denom = W_pos + W_neg\n",
    "    if denom == 0:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    return (W_pos - W_neg) / denom\n",
    "\n",
    "results_stat = []\n",
    "\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "print('Within-subject Wilcoxon検定: Temazepam vs Placebo')\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric, (col_p, col_t, col_d) in METRICS.items():\n",
    "    print(f'\\n--- {metric} ---')\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "        sub = wide[wide['stage'] == stage][[col_p, col_t, col_d]].dropna()\n",
    "        n = len(sub)\n",
    "        if n < 5:\n",
    "            print(f'  {stage}: n={n} (不足)')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "\n",
    "        delta_mean = sub[col_d].mean()\n",
    "        delta_sd   = sub[col_d].std()\n",
    "\n",
    "        try:\n",
    "            stat, p = wilcoxon(sub[col_t], sub[col_p], alternative='two-sided')\n",
    "        except Exception as e:\n",
    "            print(f'  {stage}: Wilcoxon失敗 ({e})')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "\n",
    "        # ★修正: Effect size = matched-pairs rank-biserial correlation (bounded [-1,1])\n",
    "        r = rank_biserial_wilcoxon(sub[col_t], sub[col_p])\n",
    "\n",
    "        sig = '***' if p < 0.001 else '**' if p < 0.01 else '*' if p < 0.05 else 'ns'\n",
    "        print(f'  {stage}: n={n:2d}  Δ={delta_mean:+.4f}±{delta_sd:.4f}  '\n",
    "              f'W={stat:.0f}  p={p:.4f} {sig}  r_rb={r:.3f}')\n",
    "\n",
    "        results_stat.append({\n",
    "            'metric':     metric,\n",
    "            'stage':      stage,\n",
    "            'n':          n,\n",
    "            'delta_mean': delta_mean,\n",
    "            'delta_sd':   delta_sd,\n",
    "            'W_stat':     stat,\n",
    "            'p_value':    p,\n",
    "            'effect_r':   r,  # ★rank-biserial correlationに変更 (旧: Z/sqrt(N)近似)\n",
    "            'sig':        sig,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "\n",
    "df_stat = pd.DataFrame(results_stat)\n",
    "stat_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, 'wilcoxon_results.csv')\n",
    "df_stat.to_csv(stat_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n統計結果保存: {stat_path}')"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {

    "    fig.add_subplot(gs[2, :]),  # G: Per-subject ΔCHI trajectories\n",
    "]\n",
    "for ax in axes:\n",
    "    ax.set_facecolor('#FFFFFF')\n",
    "    ax.tick_params(colors='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "    for spine in ax.spines.values():\n",
    "        spine.set_edgecolor('#CCCCCC')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- A: CHI boxplot by Stage × Condition ---\n",
    "ax = axes[0]\n",
    "positions_p = np.arange(len(STAGE_ORDER)) * 3\n",
    "positions_t = positions_p + 1\n",
    "for i, stage in enumerate(STAGE_ORDER):\n",
    "    sub_p = subj_means[(subj_means['stage']==stage) &\n",
    "                        (subj_means['condition']=='Placebo')]['CHI_mean']\n",
    "    sub_t = subj_means[(subj_means['stage']==stage) &\n",
    "                        (subj_means['condition']=='Temazepam')]['CHI_mean']\n",
    "    for pos, data, cond in [(positions_p[i], sub_p, 'Placebo'),\n",
    "                              (positions_t[i], sub_t, 'Temazepam')]:\n",
    "        if len(data) < 3:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        bp = ax.boxplot(data.dropna(), positions=[pos], widths=0.7,\n",
    "                        patch_artist=True, notch=False,\n",
    "                        medianprops=dict(color='white', lw=2),\n",
    "                        whiskerprops=dict(color='#5A6470'),\n",
    "                        capprops=dict(color='#5A6470'),\n",
    "                        flierprops=dict(marker='o', markersize=3,\n",
    "                                        markerfacecolor='#5A6470', linestyle='none'))\n",
    "        bp['boxes'][0].set_facecolor(COND_COLORS[cond])\n",
    "        bp['boxes'][0].set_alpha(0.75)\n",
    "\n",
    "ax.axhline(0, color='#F0E68C', ls=':', lw=0.8)\n",
    "ax.set_xticks(positions_p + 0.5)\n",
    "ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('CHI (subject mean)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_title('A. CHI by Stage: Placebo vs Temazepam',\n",
    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "from matplotlib.patches import Patch\n",
    "ax.legend([Patch(fc=COND_COLORS['Placebo'], alpha=0.75),\n",
    "            Patch(fc=COND_COLORS['Temazepam'], alpha=0.75)],\n",
    "           ['Placebo', 'Temazepam'], fontsize=8,\n",
    "           facecolor='#FFFFFF', labelcolor='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- B: ΔCHI by Stage (Wilcoxon p値注記) ---\n",
    "ax = axes[1]\n",
    "delta_means, delta_sems, pvals, sig_labels = [], [], [], []\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide['stage']==stage]['ΔCHI'].dropna()\n",
    "    delta_means.append(sub.mean() if len(sub) > 0 else np.nan)\n",
    "    delta_sems.append(sub.sem() if len(sub) > 0 else np.nan)\n",
    "    row = df_stat[(df_stat['metric']=='CHI') & (df_stat['stage']==stage)]\n",
    "    if len(row) > 0:\n",
    "        p = row.iloc[0]['p_value']\n",
    "        sig = row.iloc[0]['sig']\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        p, sig = np.nan, 'ns'\n",
    "    pvals.append(p)\n",
    "    sig_labels.append(sig)\n",
    "\n",
    "colors_bar = [STAGE_COLORS[s] for s in STAGE_ORDER]\n",
    "x = np.arange(len(STAGE_ORDER))\n",
    "bars = ax.bar(x, delta_means, yerr=delta_sems, color=colors_bar,\n",
    "               alpha=0.8, edgecolor='white', lw=0.5,\n",
    "               error_kw=dict(ecolor='white', capsize=4, lw=1.5))\n",
    "for i, (dm, sig) in enumerate(zip(delta_means, sig_labels)):\n",
    "    if not np.isnan(dm):\n",
    "        y_pos = dm + (delta_sems[i] if not np.isnan(delta_sems[i]) else 0) + 0.005\n",
    "        ax.text(i, y_pos, sig, ha='center', va='bottom',\n",
    "                fontsize=11, color='white', fontweight='bold')\n",
    "ax.axhline(0, color='#F0E68C', ls=':', lw=0.8)\n",
    "ax.set_xticks(x)\n",
    "ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('ΔCHI (Temazepam − Placebo, mean ± SEM)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_title('B. ΔCHI by Stage (Wilcoxon, n=22)',\n",
    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15, axis='y')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- C: 被験者別ΔCHI ヒートマップ ---\n",
    "ax = axes[2]\n",
    "pivot = wide.pivot(index='subject_nr', columns='stage', values='ΔCHI')\n",
    "pivot = pivot.reindex(columns=STAGE_ORDER)\n",
    "im = ax.imshow(pivot.values, aspect='auto', cmap='RdBu_r',\n",
    "                vmin=-0.3, vmax=0.3, interpolation='nearest')\n",
    "ax.set_xticks(range(len(STAGE_ORDER)))\n",
    "ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=8)\n",
    "ax.set_yticks(range(len(pivot)))\n",
    "ax.set_yticklabels([f'Nr={s:02d}' for s in pivot.index],\n",
    "                    color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=7)\n",
    "plt.colorbar(im, ax=ax, label='ΔCHI').ax.tick_params(colors='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_title('C. ΔCHI Heatmap by Subject',\n",
    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- D: CHI scatter Placebo vs Temazepam ---\n",
    "ax = axes[3]\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide['stage']==stage][['CHI_mean_P','CHI_mean_T']].dropna()\n",
    "    if len(sub) < 3:\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    ax.scatter(sub['CHI_mean_P'], sub['CHI_mean_T'],\n",
    "                c=STAGE_COLORS[stage], s=50, alpha=0.8,\n",
    "                label=f'{stage} (n={len(sub)})', edgecolors='white', lw=0.5)\n",
    "lims = [ax.get_xlim()[0], ax.get_xlim()[1]]\n",
    "all_vals = pd.concat([wide['CHI_mean_P'], wide['CHI_mean_T']]).dropna()\n",
    "lim = [all_vals.min()-0.05, all_vals.max()+0.05]\n",
    "ax.plot(lim, lim, 'w--', lw=0.8, alpha=0.5, label='Identity')\n",
    "ax.set_xlim(lim); ax.set_ylim(lim)\n",
    "ax.set_xlabel('CHI (Placebo)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('CHI (Temazepam)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_title('D. CHI: Placebo vs Temazepam\\n(above diagonal = Temazepam>Placebo)',\n",
    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "ax.legend(fontsize=7, facecolor='#FFFFFF', labelcolor='#1A1A1A', markerscale=1.2)\n",
    "ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15)\n",
    "ax.axhline(0, color='gray', ls=':', lw=0.5)\n",
    "ax.axvline(0, color='gray', ls=':', lw=0.5)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- E: D_eff_rel 比較 ---\n",
    "ax = axes[4]\n",
    "de_deltas = []\n",
    "de_sems   = []\n",
    "de_sigs   = []\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide['stage']==stage]['ΔD_eff_rel'].dropna()\n",
    "    de_deltas.append(sub.mean() if len(sub)>0 else np.nan)\n",
    "    de_sems.append(sub.sem() if len(sub)>0 else np.nan)\n",
    "    row = df_stat[(df_stat['metric']=='D_eff_rel') & (df_stat['stage']==stage)]\n",
    "    de_sigs.append(row.iloc[0]['sig'] if len(row)>0 else 'ns')\n",
    "\n",
    "ax.bar(x, de_deltas, yerr=de_sems, color=colors_bar, alpha=0.8,\n",
    "        edgecolor='white', lw=0.5,\n",
    "        error_kw=dict(ecolor='white', capsize=4, lw=1.5))\n",
    "for i, (d, sig) in enumerate(zip(de_deltas, de_sigs)):\n",
    "    if not np.isnan(d):\n",
    "        y_pos = d + (de_sems[i] if not np.isnan(de_sems[i]) else 0) + 0.003\n",
    "        ax.text(i, y_pos, sig, ha='center', fontsize=11,\n",
    "                color='white', fontweight='bold')\n",
    "ax.axhline(0, color='#F0E68C', ls=':', lw=0.8)\n",
    "ax.set_xticks(x)\n",
    "ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('ΔD_eff_rel (T − P, mean ± SEM)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_title('E. ΔD_eff_rel by Stage (Wilcoxon, n=22)',\n",
    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15, axis='y')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- F: Phase V rate ---\n",
    "ax = axes[5]\n",
    "pv_p, pv_t = [], []\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sm_p = subj_means[(subj_means['stage']==stage) &\n",
    "                       (subj_means['condition']=='Placebo')]['PhaseV_rate']\n",
    "    sm_t = subj_means[(subj_means['stage']==stage) &\n",
    "                       (subj_means['condition']=='Temazepam')]['PhaseV_rate']\n",
    "    pv_p.append(sm_p.mean()*100 if len(sm_p)>0 else np.nan)\n",
    "    pv_t.append(sm_t.mean()*100 if len(sm_t)>0 else np.nan)\n",
    "\n",
    "w_bar = 0.35\n",
    "ax.bar(x - w_bar/2, pv_p, w_bar, color=COND_COLORS['Placebo'],\n",
    "        alpha=0.8, label='Placebo', edgecolor='white', lw=0.5)\n",
    "ax.bar(x + w_bar/2, pv_t, w_bar, color=COND_COLORS['Temazepam'],\n",
    "        alpha=0.8, label='Temazepam', edgecolor='white', lw=0.5)\n",
    "ax.set_xticks(x)\n",
    "ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('Phase V Rate (%)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.set_title('F. Phase V Rate: Placebo vs Temazepam',\n",
    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "ax.legend(fontsize=8, facecolor='#FFFFFF', labelcolor='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15, axis='y')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- G: 被験者別ΔCHI トラジェクトリ (折れ線) ---\n",
    "ax = axes[6]\n",
    "for _, sub_row in df_subj.iterrows():\n",
    "    nr = int(sub_row['subject_nr'])\n",
    "    sub_wide = wide[wide['subject_nr']==nr].set_index('stage')\n",
    "    vals = [sub_wide.loc[s,'ΔCHI'] if s in sub_wide.index else np.nan\n",
    "            for s in STAGE_ORDER]\n",
    "    ax.plot(x, vals, 'o-', alpha=0.45, lw=1.0, markersize=4, color='#5588CC')\n",
    "\n",
    "# グループ平均\n",
    "mean_delta = [wide[wide['stage']==s]['ΔCHI'].mean() for s in STAGE_ORDER]\n",
    "ax.plot(x, mean_delta, 's-', color='#FF6644', lw=2.5,\n",
    "         markersize=8, label='Group mean (n=22)', zorder=5)\n",
    "ax.axhline(0, color='#F0E68C', ls=':', lw=1.0)\n",
    "ax.set_xticks(x)\n",
    "ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=11)\n",
    "ax.set_ylabel('ΔCHI (Temazepam − Placebo)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",

    "             color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=11)\n",

    "plt.show()\n",

    "id": "step10b_individual_scatter"

   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 10b: Individual-level scatter — outlier-robustness check\n",
    "# Visual check that the N2/N3 CHI effect is not driven by a small number of outliers\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 設計:\n",
    "#   x = Placebo夜 CHI (被験者平均)\n",
    "#   y = Temazepam夜 CHI (被験者平均)\n",
    "#   対角線 y=x : この線より下 = テマゼパムでCHI低下\n",
    "#   N2 / N3 を独立パネルで表示\n",
    "#   副パネル: ΔCHI分布 (ゼロとの比較、Wilcoxon p値付き)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "from scipy.stats import norm as _norm\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---- カラー定義 ----\n",
    "C_PLACEBO   = \"#5588CC\"\n",
    "C_TEMAZ     = \"#CC5566\"\n",
    "C_DIAG      = \"#F0E68C\"   # 対角線\n",
    "C_GRID      = \"#CCCCCC\"\n",
    "C_TEXT      = \"#1A1A1A\"\n",
    "C_SUBTEXT   = \"#5A6470\"\n",
    "C_SCATTER_N2 = \"#4080C0\"  # N2: 青系\n",
    "C_SCATTER_N3 = \"#9060CC\"  # N3: 紫系\n",
    "BG_DARK     = \"#FFFFFF\"\n",
    "BG_PANEL    = \"#FFFFFF\"\n",
    "\n",
    "# ---- レイアウト: 2列×2行 (scatter上段, ΔCHI分布下段) ----\n",
    "fig_sc, axes_sc = plt.subplots(\n",
    "    2, 2, figsize=(12, 11), facecolor=BG_DARK,\n",
    "    gridspec_kw={\"height_ratios\": [1.6, 1]}\n",
    ")\n",
    "fig_sc.suptitle(\n",
    "    \"Individual-Level CHI: Temazepam vs. Placebo\\n\"\n",
    "    \"Sleep-EDF Expanded Sleep Telemetry (N=22, within-subject)\",\n",
    "    color=C_TEXT, fontsize=13, fontweight=\"bold\", y=1.01\n",
    ")\n",
    "for ax in axes_sc.flat:\n",
    "    ax.set_facecolor(BG_PANEL)\n",
    "    ax.tick_params(colors=C_TEXT)\n",
    "    for sp in ax.spines.values():\n",
    "        sp.set_edgecolor(C_GRID)\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# ヘルパー: 1ステージのscatter + 統計アノテーション\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "def draw_scatter(ax, stage, color, label_color):\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == stage][[\"subject_nr\",\"CHI_mean_P\",\"CHI_mean_T\",\"ΔCHI\"]].dropna()\n",
    "    x   = sub[\"CHI_mean_P\"].values\n",
    "    y   = sub[\"CHI_mean_T\"].values\n",
    "    n   = len(sub)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # 対角線の範囲\n",
    "    pad = 0.12\n",
    "    vmin = min(x.min(), y.min()) - pad\n",
    "    vmax = max(x.max(), y.max()) + pad\n",
    "    ax.plot([vmin, vmax], [vmin, vmax], \"--\", color=C_DIAG,\n",
    "            lw=1.4, alpha=0.8, label=\"y = x  (no effect)\", zorder=2)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # 被験者ごとの点\n",
    "    ax.scatter(x, y, s=72, color=color, alpha=0.85,\n",
    "               edgecolors=\"white\", linewidths=0.5, zorder=4)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # 被験者番号ラベル (混雑しないよう offset)\n",
    "    for _, row in sub.iterrows():\n",
    "        ax.annotate(\n",
    "            str(int(row[\"subject_nr\"])),\n",
    "            (row[\"CHI_mean_P\"], row[\"CHI_mean_T\"]),\n",
    "            textcoords=\"offset points\", xytext=(5, 4),\n",
    "            fontsize=7, color=C_SUBTEXT, zorder=5\n",
    "        )\n",
    "\n",
    "    # 対角線より下の点の割合\n",
    "    n_below = (y < x).sum()\n",
    "    pct_below = 100 * n_below / n\n",
    "\n",
    "    # Wilcoxon p値と効果量\n",
    "    from scipy.stats import wilcoxon\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        w_stat, p_val = wilcoxon(y, x, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "        r_val = rank_biserial_wilcoxon(y, x)  # ★修正: rank-biserial (bounded [-1,1], 旧Z/sqrt(N)近似を置換)\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        p_val, r_val = np.nan, np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "    delta_mean = sub[\"ΔCHI\"].mean()\n",
    "    delta_sd   = sub[\"ΔCHI\"].std()\n",
    "\n",
    "    # アノテーションボックス\n",
    "    stats_text = (\n",
    "        f\"n={n}  ({n_below}/{n} below diagonal, {pct_below:.0f}%)\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"ΔCHI = {delta_mean:+.3f} ± {delta_sd:.3f}\\n\"\n",
    "        f\"p = {p_val:.4f},  r_rb = {r_val:.3f}\"\n",
    "    )\n",
    "    ax.text(\n",
    "        0.04, 0.97, stats_text,\n",
    "        transform=ax.transAxes, fontsize=8.5,\n",
    "        verticalalignment=\"top\",\n",
    "        color=C_TEXT,\n",
    "        bbox=dict(boxstyle=\"round,pad=0.4\", facecolor=\"#F5F5F5\",\n",
    "                  edgecolor=C_GRID, alpha=0.9)\n",
    "    )\n",
    "\n",
    "    ax.set_xlabel(\"CHI — Placebo night\", color=C_TEXT, fontsize=10)\n",
    "    ax.set_ylabel(\"CHI — Temazepam night\", color=C_TEXT, fontsize=10)\n",
    "    ax.set_title(f\"{stage} sleep\", color=label_color,\n",
    "                 fontsize=12, fontweight=\"bold\")\n",
    "    ax.set_xlim(vmin, vmax)\n",
    "    ax.set_ylim(vmin, vmax)\n",
    "    ax.set_aspect(\"equal\")\n",
    "    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.12)\n",
    "    ax.legend(fontsize=8, facecolor=BG_PANEL, labelcolor=C_TEXT,\n",
    "               loc=\"lower right\")\n",
    "    return sub\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# ヘルパー: ΔCHI分布パネル\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "def draw_delta_dist(ax, stage, color):\n",
    "    sub   = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == stage][\"ΔCHI\"].dropna()\n",
    "    n     = len(sub)\n",
    "    vals  = sub.values\n",
    "    nbins = min(12, n // 2 + 1)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # ヒストグラム\n",
    "    ax.hist(vals, bins=nbins, color=color, alpha=0.75,\n",
    "            edgecolor=\"white\", linewidth=0.5, zorder=3)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # ゼロ線\n",
    "    ax.axvline(0, color=C_DIAG, lw=1.6, ls=\"--\",\n",
    "                label=\"ΔCHI = 0 (no effect)\", zorder=4)\n",
    "    # 平均線\n",
    "    ax.axvline(vals.mean(), color=\"white\", lw=1.4, ls=\"-\",\n",
    "                label=f\"mean = {vals.mean():+.3f}\", zorder=5)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # n below / above zero\n",
    "    n_neg = (vals < 0).sum()\n",
    "    ax.text(\n",
    "        0.97, 0.95,\n",
    "        f\"{n_neg}/{n} < 0\",\n",
    "        transform=ax.transAxes, ha=\"right\", va=\"top\",\n",
    "        fontsize=9, color=C_TEXT,\n",
    "        bbox=dict(boxstyle=\"round,pad=0.3\", facecolor=\"#F5F5F5\",\n",
    "                  edgecolor=C_GRID, alpha=0.85)\n",
    "    )\n",
    "\n",
    "    ax.set_xlabel(\"ΔCHI  (Temazepam − Placebo)\", color=C_TEXT, fontsize=9)\n",
    "    ax.set_ylabel(\"Number of subjects\", color=C_TEXT, fontsize=9)\n",
    "    ax.set_title(f\"Distribution of ΔCHI — {stage}\",\n",
    "                 color=C_TEXT, fontsize=10)\n",
    "    ax.legend(fontsize=7.5, facecolor=BG_PANEL, labelcolor=C_TEXT)\n",
    "    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.12, axis=\"x\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 描画実行\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "draw_scatter(axes_sc[0, 0], \"N2\", C_SCATTER_N2, label_color=\"#6699DD\")\n",
    "draw_scatter(axes_sc[0, 1], \"N3\", C_SCATTER_N3, label_color=\"#AA88EE\")\n",
    "draw_delta_dist(axes_sc[1, 0], \"N2\", C_SCATTER_N2)\n",
    "draw_delta_dist(axes_sc[1, 1], \"N3\", C_SCATTER_N3)\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "scatter_path = os.path.join(OUTPUT_DIR, \"ECSoC_individual_scatter_N2N3.png\")\n",
    "fig_sc.savefig(scatter_path, dpi=180, bbox_inches=\"tight\",\n",
    "               facecolor=BG_DARK)\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "print(f\"保存: {scatter_path}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# コンソールサマリー\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 60)\n",
    "print(\"Individual-level scatter サマリー\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 60)\n",
    "for stage, color in [(\"N2\", \"N2\"), (\"N3\", \"N3\")]:\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == stage][[\"CHI_mean_P\",\"CHI_mean_T\",\"ΔCHI\"]].dropna()\n",
    "    n_below = (sub[\"CHI_mean_T\"] < sub[\"CHI_mean_P\"]).sum()\n",
    "    n_total = len(sub)\n",
    "    print(f\"  {stage}: {n_below}/{n_total} 被験者で CHI低下 \"\n",
    "          f\"({100*n_below/n_total:.0f}%)  \"\n",
    "          f\"ΔCHI = {sub['ΔCHI'].mean():+.4f} ± {sub['ΔCHI'].std():.4f}\")\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"論文キャプション (英語):\")\n",
    "print(\"\"\"\n",
    "Individual-level scatter plots of CHI in N2 and N3 stages\n",
    "(Temazepam vs. Placebo). Each point represents one subject.\n",
    "The dashed identity line (y = x) marks no drug effect;\n",
    "points below the line indicate a temazepam-associated CHI\n",
    "reduction. The majority of subjects lie below the identity\n",
    "line in both N2 and N3, demonstrating that the group-level\n",
    "CHI suppression reflects a consistent within-subject effect\n",
    "rather than an artifact driven by a small number of outliers.\n",
    "Lower panels show the distribution of ΔCHI (Temazepam − Placebo)\n",
    "across subjects; the dashed vertical line marks zero.\n",
    "\"\"\")\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "step10c_bayes_factor"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# Step 10c: Bayes Factor (Bayesian Wilcoxon signed-rank test)\n",
    "# pingouin v0.6.x では bayesfactor_wilcoxon が削除されたため\n",
    "# Rouder et al. (2009) の正規近似実装で代替 (外部依存なし)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "from scipy import stats, integrate\n",
    "\n",
    "# ── BF10計算関数 ──────────────────────────────────────────────\n",
    "def bayesian_wilcoxon_bf10(x, y, r_scale=1.0 / np.sqrt(2)):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    Bayesian Wilcoxon signed-rank test — BF10を返す\n",
    "\n",
    "    Method:\n",
    "        Wilcoxon T+統計量をz化し、Cauchy(0, r_scale)事前分布のもとで\n",
    "        周辺尤度を数値積分。Rouder et al. (2009) t検定BF10の\n",
    "        Wilcoxon正規近似版。\n",
    "\n",
    "    Parameters\n",
    "    ----------\n",
    "    x, y      : array-like  対応あり観測値 (x=Temazepam, y=Placebo)\n",
    "    r_scale   : float       Cauchy事前分布の尺度 (default = 1/√2)\n",
    "\n",
    "    Returns\n",
    "    -------\n",
    "    BF10 : float   (H1 : 差あり) / (H0 : 差なし) のオッズ\n",
    "    z    : float   正規近似z値\n",
    "    n    : int     有効ペア数\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    diff = np.asarray(x, dtype=float) - np.asarray(y, dtype=float)\n",
    "    diff = diff[diff != 0]          # ゼロ差を除外 (標準的処理)\n",
    "    n = len(diff)\n",
    "    if n < 4:\n",
    "        return np.nan, np.nan, n\n",
    "\n",
    "    # T+統計量 → z変換\n",
    "    res   = stats.wilcoxon(diff, alternative='two-sided')\n",
    "    T_plus = res.statistic\n",
    "    mu    = n * (n + 1) / 4.0\n",
    "    sigma = np.sqrt(n * (n + 1) * (2 * n + 1) / 24.0)\n",
    "    z     = (T_plus - mu) / sigma\n",
    "\n",
    "    # 周辺尤度 H1: ∫ N(z | δ√n, 1) × Cauchy(δ | 0, r) dδ\n",
    "    def integrand(delta):\n",
    "        lh  = stats.norm.pdf(z, loc=delta * np.sqrt(n), scale=1.0)\n",
    "        pri = stats.cauchy.pdf(delta, loc=0, scale=r_scale)\n",
    "        return lh * pri\n",
    "\n",
    "    marginal_h1, _ = integrate.quad(integrand, -np.inf, np.inf,\n",
    "                                    limit=300, epsabs=1e-8, epsrel=1e-8)\n",
    "    marginal_h0 = stats.norm.pdf(z, loc=0, scale=1.0)\n",
    "\n",
    "    BF10 = marginal_h1 / marginal_h0 if marginal_h0 > 0 else np.nan\n",
    "    return BF10, z, n\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# ── Jeffreys スケールラベル ────────────────────────────────────\n",
    "def bf_label(bf10):\n",
    "    if   bf10 >= 100:  return 'Extreme evidence for H1'\n",
    "    elif bf10 >= 30:   return 'Very strong evidence for H1'\n",
    "    elif bf10 >= 10:   return 'Strong evidence for H1'\n",
    "    elif bf10 >= 3:    return 'Moderate evidence for H1'\n",
    "    elif bf10 >= 1:    return 'Anecdotal evidence for H1'\n",
    "    elif bf10 >= 1/3:  return 'Anecdotal evidence for H0'\n",
    "    elif bf10 >= 1/10: return 'Moderate evidence for H0'\n",
    "    else:               return 'Strong evidence for H0'\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# ── 検定実行 ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\n",
    "print('=' * 68)\n",
    "print('Bayesian Wilcoxon Signed-Rank Test (two-sided)')\n",
    "print('Prior: Cauchy(0, r=1/\\u221a2)  [Rouder et al. 2009 normal approx.]')\n",
    "print('=' * 68)\n",
    "print(f'{\"Stage\":<6} {\"n\":>4} {\"z\":>7} {\"BF10\":>12} {\"BF01\":>10}  Interpretation')\n",
    "print('-' * 68)\n",
    "\n",
    "bf_results = {}\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide['stage'] == stage][['CHI_mean_P', 'CHI_mean_T']].dropna()\n",
    "    n = len(sub)\n",
    "    if n < 4:\n",
    "        print(f'{stage:<6} {n:>4}  サンプル不足')\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "\n",
    "    bf10, z, n_eff = bayesian_wilcoxon_bf10(\n",
    "        sub['CHI_mean_T'].values,\n",
    "        sub['CHI_mean_P'].values\n",
    "    )\n",
    "\n",
    "    if not np.isfinite(bf10):\n",
    "        print(f'{stage:<6} {n:>4}  計算失敗')\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "\n",
    "    bf01  = 1.0 / bf10\n",
    "    label = bf_label(bf10)\n",
    "    bf_results[stage] = bf10\n",
    "    z_str = f'{z:+.3f}' if np.isfinite(z) else 'n/a'\n",
    "    print(f'{stage:<6} {n:>4} {z_str:>7} {bf10:>12.2f} {bf01:>10.4f}  {label}')\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# ── 論文記載用テキスト生成 ───────────────────────────────────────\n",
    "def fmt_bf(bf):\n",
    "    \"\"\"BF値を論文向けに整形 (例: 2.3\\u00d710\\u00b3, >10000)\"\"\"\n",
    "    import math\n",
    "    if not np.isfinite(bf):\n",
    "        return 'N/A'\n",
    "    if bf >= 10000:\n",
    "        return '>10,000'\n",
    "    if bf >= 1000:\n",
    "        exp  = int(math.log10(bf))\n",
    "        coef = bf / (10 ** exp)\n",
    "        return f'{coef:.1f}\\u00d710{exp}'\n",
    "    return f'{bf:.1f}'\n",
    "\n",
    "n2_bf = bf_results.get('N2', float('nan'))\n",
    "n3_bf = bf_results.get('N3', float('nan'))\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('\\u2500\\u2500 N2/N3 論文記載用テキスト (English) \\u2500\\u2500')\n",
    "print(f\"\"\"\n",
    "To supplement the frequentist results, Bayesian Wilcoxon\n",
    "signed-rank tests were performed using a Cauchy prior\n",
    "(r = 1/\\u221a2). The Bayes factors provided strong-to-very-strong\n",
    "evidence for a temazepam-associated CHI reduction in both\n",
    "N2 (BF\\u2081\\u2080 = {fmt_bf(n2_bf)}) and N3 (BF\\u2081\\u2080 = {fmt_bf(n3_bf)}),\n",
    "while no meaningful evidence was obtained for the remaining\n",
    "stages (W, N1, REM: BF\\u2081\\u2080 < 1 in all cases).\n",
    "\"\"\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print('\\u2500\\u2500 Results 1行追加版 (短い) \\u2500\\u2500')\n",
    "print(f\"\"\"\n",
    "Bayesian Wilcoxon tests corroborated these results,\n",
    "yielding very strong-to-strong evidence for CHI reduction\n",
    "in N2 (BF₁₀ = {fmt_bf(n2_bf)}) and N3 (BF₁₀ = {fmt_bf(n3_bf)}),\n",
    "with no meaningful evidence in W, N1, or REM (BF\\u2081\\u2080 < 1).\n",
    "\"\"\")\n"
   ]
  },

   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 2: SCファイルスキャン & 被験者リスト構築\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# SCファイル命名規則: SC4{ss}{N}E0-PSG.edf\n",
    "#   ss=被験者番号(2桁), N=夜番号(1 or 2)\n",
    "# 各被験者につき夜1のみ使用 (独立サンプル比較)\n",
    "\n",
    "def scan_sc_pairs(sc_dir, max_subjects=22):\n",
    "    psg_files = sorted(glob.glob(os.path.join(sc_dir, \"SC4*PSG.edf\")))\n",
    "    seen = {}\n",
    "    pairs_sc = []\n",
    "    for psg in psg_files:\n",
    "        fname = os.path.basename(psg)\n",
    "        try:\n",
    "            ss  = int(fname[3:5])\n",
    "            ngt = int(fname[5])\n",
    "        except (ValueError, IndexError):\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        if ss in seen:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        seen[ss] = True\n",
    "        hyp_cands = glob.glob(\n",
    "            os.path.join(sc_dir, f\"SC4{fname[3:5]}{ngt}*Hypnogram*.edf\"))\n",
    "        pairs_sc.append({\"subject_nr\": ss, \"night_nr\": ngt,\n",
    "                          \"psg\": psg, \"hyp\": hyp_cands[0] if hyp_cands else None})\n",
    "        if len(pairs_sc) >= max_subjects:\n",
    "            break\n",
    "    return pairs_sc\n",
    "\n",
    "sc_pairs = scan_sc_pairs(SC_DIR, max_subjects=22)\n",
    "print(f\"SCペア数: {len(sc_pairs)}\")\n",
    "for p in sc_pairs[:5]:\n",
    "    hyp_str = os.path.basename(p[\"hyp\"]) if p[\"hyp\"] else \"なし\"\n",
    "    print(f'  Nr={p[\"subject_nr\"]:02d} 夜{p[\"night_nr\"]}: '\n",
    "          f'{os.path.basename(p[\"psg\"])} + {hyp_str}')\n"
   ]

    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 3b: SC群のサンプリングレート整合性チェック\n",

    "# ST群と同じ process_one_night() / dfa_ecsoc() をSC群にも使用しているため、\n",

    "\n",
    "sc_fs_check_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, 'sc_fs_consistency_check.csv')\n",

    "print(f'\\n出力ファイル: {sc_fs_check_path}')\n"
   ]

   "cell_type": "code",

   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step5_compare"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 5: ST Placebo vs SC Healthy — Mann-Whitney U検定\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "from scipy.stats import mannwhitneyu, norm\n",
    "\n",
    "def rank_biserial_mannwhitney(x, y):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    ★修正: 独立2標本版 rank-biserial correlation (Wendt 1972 / Cliff's delta相当)。\n",
    "    Z/sqrt(N)近似ではなくU統計量から直接計算するため常に[-1,1]に収まる。\n",
    "    r = 2U/(n1*n2) - 1   (U はxに対する統計量; scipy.stats.mannwhitneyuの規約に従う)\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    x = np.asarray(x); y = np.asarray(y)\n",
    "    n1, n2 = len(x), len(y)\n",
    "    if n1 == 0 or n2 == 0:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    stat, _ = mannwhitneyu(x, y, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "    return 2 * stat / (n1 * n2) - 1\n",
    "\n",
    "st_placebo_means = subj_means[\n",
    "    subj_means[\"condition\"] == \"Placebo\"\n",
    "][[\"subject_nr\",\"stage\",\"CHI_mean\",\"D_eff_rel_mean\",\"PhaseV_rate\"]].copy()\n",
    "st_placebo_means[\"cohort\"] = \"ST_Placebo\"\n",
    "\n",
    "sc_for_compare = sc_means[\n",
    "    [\"subject_nr\",\"stage\",\"CHI_mean\",\"D_eff_rel_mean\",\"PhaseV_rate\"]\n",
    "].copy()\n",
    "sc_for_compare[\"cohort\"] = \"SC_Healthy\"\n",
    "\n",
    "df_compare = pd.concat([st_placebo_means, sc_for_compare], ignore_index=True)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 65)\n",
    "print(\"外部検証: ST Placebo vs SC Healthy — Mann-Whitney U検定\")\n",
    "print(\"(独立サンプル, ST N=22, SC N=最大22)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 65)\n",
    "\n",
    "ext_results = []\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    st_vals = df_compare[(df_compare[\"cohort\"]==\"ST_Placebo\") &\n",
    "                          (df_compare[\"stage\"]==stage)][\"CHI_mean\"].dropna()\n",
    "    sc_vals = df_compare[(df_compare[\"cohort\"]==\"SC_Healthy\") &\n",
    "                          (df_compare[\"stage\"]==stage)][\"CHI_mean\"].dropna()\n",
    "    if len(st_vals) < 5 or len(sc_vals) < 5:\n",
    "        print(f\"  {stage}: サンプル不足 (ST n={len(st_vals)}, SC n={len(sc_vals)})\")\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    stat, p = mannwhitneyu(st_vals, sc_vals, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "    r = rank_biserial_mannwhitney(st_vals, sc_vals)  # ★修正: rank-biserial (bounded [-1,1], 旧Z/sqrt(N)近似を置換)\n",
    "    sig = \"***\" if p < 0.001 else \"**\" if p < 0.01 else \"*\" if p < 0.05 else \"ns\"\n",
    "    print(f\"  {stage}: ST={st_vals.mean():+.4f} SC={sc_vals.mean():+.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"p={p:.4f} {sig}  r={r:.3f}\")\n",
    "    ext_results.append({\"stage\":stage,\n",
    "        \"ST_Placebo_CHI_mean\":st_vals.mean(), \"ST_Placebo_CHI_sd\":st_vals.std(),\n",
    "        \"SC_Healthy_CHI_mean\":sc_vals.mean(), \"SC_Healthy_CHI_sd\":sc_vals.std(),\n",
    "        \"U_stat\":stat, \"p_value\":p, \"effect_r\":r, \"sig\":sig})\n",
    "\n",
    "df_ext = pd.DataFrame(ext_results)\n",
    "ext_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_ST_placebo_vs_SC.csv\")\n",
    "df_ext.to_csv(ext_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f\"\\n外部検証結果保存: {ext_path}\")\n"
   ]
  },

  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7_swa_chi_correlation"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7: Δデルタパワー vs ΔCHI 個人間相関\n",
    "# Discussion仮説: SWA増大 → スケール収束 (CHI低下) の検証\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "from scipy.signal import welch\n",
    "from scipy.stats import spearmanr\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_delta_power_night(psg_path, hyp_path, subject_nr, condition,\n",
    "                               target_stages=(\"N2\", \"N3\")):\n",
    "    \"\"\"N2/N3エポックのデルタ帯域パワー (0.5-4 Hz) 平均を返す\"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(\n",
    "            psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "        sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "        actual_fs = int(raw.info[\"sfreq\"])\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f\"  ⚠️ [{subject_nr} {condition}]: {e}\")\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "    win_samp = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "    delta_powers = []\n",
    "    for ep in range(len(sig) // win_samp):\n",
    "        t0 = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        if stage not in target_stages: continue\n",
    "        x = sig[ep * win_samp : (ep+1) * win_samp]\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > 500: continue\n",
    "        freqs, psd = welch(x, fs=actual_fs, nperseg=min(256, len(x)))\n",
    "        delta_mask = (freqs >= 0.5) & (freqs <= 4.0)\n",
    "        delta_powers.append(np.mean(psd[delta_mask]))\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    return np.mean(delta_powers) if delta_powers else np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"N2/N3 デルタ帯域パワー計算中 (ST 22被験者 x 2夜)...\")\n",
    "swa_records = []\n",
    "for p in pairs:\n",
    "    nr = p[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "    for cond, psg_key, hyp_key in [\n",
    "        (\"Placebo\",   \"placebo_psg\", \"placebo_hyp\"),\n",
    "        (\"Temazepam\", \"temaz_psg\",   \"temaz_hyp\"),\n",
    "    ]:\n",
    "        dp = compute_delta_power_night(p[psg_key], p[hyp_key], nr, cond)\n",
    "        swa_records.append({\"subject_nr\":nr, \"condition\":cond, \"delta_power_N2N3\":dp})\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={nr:02d} 完了\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_swa = pd.DataFrame(swa_records)\n",
    "df_swa_wide = df_swa.pivot(\n",
    "    index=\"subject_nr\", columns=\"condition\", values=\"delta_power_N2N3\"\n",
    ").reset_index()\n",
    "df_swa_wide.columns.name = None\n",
    "df_swa_wide[\"Ddelta_power\"] = df_swa_wide[\"Temazepam\"] - df_swa_wide[\"Placebo\"]\n",
    "\n",
    "# ΔCHI (N2+N3平均) とマージ\n",
    "# DELTA_CHI列名をwideテーブルの実際の列名に合わせる (存在確認を先に行う)\n",
    "if \"DELTA_CHI\" in wide.columns:\n",
    "    chi_col = \"DELTA_CHI\"\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    chi_col = \"ΔCHI\"\n",
    "chi_n2n3 = wide[wide[\"stage\"].isin([\"N2\",\"N3\"])].groupby(\n",
    "    \"subject_nr\")[chi_col].mean().reset_index()\n",
    "chi_n2n3.columns = [\"subject_nr\", \"DELTA_CHI\"]\n",
    "\n",
    "df_swa_chi = pd.merge(df_swa_wide, chi_n2n3, on=\"subject_nr\")\n",
    "\n",
    "corr, pval = spearmanr(\n",
    "    df_swa_chi[\"Ddelta_power\"].dropna(),\n",
    "    df_swa_chi[\"DELTA_CHI\"].dropna()\n",
    ")\n",
    "print(f\"\\nSpearman rho (Δデルタパワー vs ΔCHI N2+N3): rho={corr:.3f}, p={pval:.4f}\")\n",
    "if corr < -0.3 and pval < 0.05:\n",
    "    print(\"  ✅ 仮説支持: SWA増大 → CHI低下 の負相関を確認\")\n",
    "elif pval >= 0.05:\n",
    "    print(\"  ℹ️  有意相関なし (仮説は支持されず)\")\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(f\"  ℹ️  rho={corr:.3f} (方向・強度確認)\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# 散布図\n",
    "fig3, ax3 = plt.subplots(figsize=(6,5), facecolor=\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "ax3.set_facecolor(\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "ax3.scatter(df_swa_chi[\"Ddelta_power\"], df_swa_chi[\"DELTA_CHI\"],\n",
    "            color=\"#CC5566\", alpha=0.8, s=60)\n",
    "for _, row in df_swa_chi.iterrows():\n",
    "    ax3.annotate(str(int(row[\"subject_nr\"])),\n",
    "                 (row[\"Ddelta_power\"], row[\"DELTA_CHI\"]),\n",
    "                 fontsize=7, color=\"#5A6470\")\n",
    "mask = df_swa_chi[[\"Ddelta_power\",\"DELTA_CHI\"]].notna().all(axis=1)\n",
    "if mask.sum() >= 4:\n",
    "    xs = df_swa_chi[\"Ddelta_power\"][mask].values\n",
    "    ys = df_swa_chi[\"DELTA_CHI\"][mask].values\n",
    "    m, b = np.polyfit(xs, ys, 1)\n",
    "    x_line = np.linspace(xs.min(), xs.max(), 50)\n",
    "    ax3.plot(x_line, m*x_line+b, color=\"#F0E68C\", lw=1.5, ls=\"--\")\n",
    "ax3.axhline(0, color=\"#5A6470\", lw=0.8, ls=\":\")\n",
    "ax3.axvline(0, color=\"#5A6470\", lw=0.8, ls=\":\")\n",
    "ax3.set_xlabel(\"Δ Delta Power N2+N3 (T-P, uV2/Hz)\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "ax3.set_ylabel(\"Δ CHI N2+N3 (T-P)\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "ax3.set_title(f\"SWA vs CHI: rho={corr:.3f}, p={pval:.4f}\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "ax3.tick_params(colors=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "for spine in ax3.spines.values(): spine.set_edgecolor(\"#CCCCCC\")\n",
    "ax3.grid(True, alpha=0.15)\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "fig3_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_SWA_CHI_scatter.png\")\n",
    "fig3.savefig(fig3_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches=\"tight\", facecolor=\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "print(f\"図保存: {fig3_path}\")\n"
   ]

  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7b_swa_chi_sensitivity"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7b: ΔSWA-ΔCHI相関 — Main + Sensitivity (N2/N3別) + Bootstrap CI\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: N2+N3統合(主解析)に加え、N2単独・N3単独でも同方向の負相関が\n",
    "#       出るかを確認し、SWA増強→CHI低下仮説の頑健性を検証する。\n",
    "\n",
    "from scipy.stats import spearmanr\n",
    "\n",
    "N_BOOT = 10000\n",
    "RNG_SEED = 42\n",
    "\n",
    "def bootstrap_spearman_ci(x, y, n_boot=N_BOOT, seed=RNG_SEED, alpha=0.05):\n",
    "    \"\"\"対被験者ペアをリサンプリングしてSpearman rhoのpercentile bootstrap CIを返す\"\"\"\n",
    "    rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)\n",
    "    x = np.asarray(x); y = np.asarray(y)\n",
    "    n = len(x)\n",
    "    boot_rhos = []\n",
    "    for _ in range(n_boot):\n",
    "        idx = rng.integers(0, n, n)\n",
    "        bx, by = x[idx], y[idx]\n",
    "        if np.std(bx) == 0 or np.std(by) == 0:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        r, _ = spearmanr(bx, by)\n",
    "        if not np.isnan(r):\n",
    "            boot_rhos.append(r)\n",
    "    boot_rhos = np.array(boot_rhos)\n",
    "    lo = np.percentile(boot_rhos, 100 * (alpha / 2))\n",
    "    hi = np.percentile(boot_rhos, 100 * (1 - alpha / 2))\n",
    "    return lo, hi, len(boot_rhos)\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_delta_power_stage(psg_path, hyp_path, target_stages):\n",
    "    \"\"\"指定ステージ集合に対するデルタパワー (0.5-4Hz) 平均\"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(\n",
    "            psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "        sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "        actual_fs = int(raw.info[\"sfreq\"])\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f\"  [WARN] {e}\")\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "    win_samp = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "    delta_powers = []\n",
    "    for ep in range(len(sig) // win_samp):\n",
    "        t0 = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        if stage not in target_stages:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        x = sig[ep * win_samp : (ep + 1) * win_samp]\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > 500:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        freqs, psd = welch(x, fs=actual_fs, nperseg=min(256, len(x)))\n",
    "        delta_mask = (freqs >= 0.5) & (freqs <= 4.0)\n",
    "        delta_powers.append(np.mean(psd[delta_mask]))\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    return np.mean(delta_powers) if delta_powers else np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- N2単独 / N3単独のΔSWAを計算 (N2+N3統合は既存 df_swa_chi を再利用) ---\n",
    "print(\"N2単独・N3単独のデルタ帯域パワー計算中 (sensitivity analysis)...\")\n",
    "swa_stage_records = []\n",
    "for p in pairs:\n",
    "    nr = p[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "    for cond, psg_key, hyp_key in [\n",
    "        (\"Placebo\",   \"placebo_psg\", \"placebo_hyp\"),\n",
    "        (\"Temazepam\", \"temaz_psg\",   \"temaz_hyp\"),\n",
    "    ]:\n",
    "        dp_n2 = compute_delta_power_stage(p[psg_key], p[hyp_key], target_stages=(\"N2\",))\n",
    "        dp_n3 = compute_delta_power_stage(p[psg_key], p[hyp_key], target_stages=(\"N3\",))\n",
    "        swa_stage_records.append({\n",
    "            \"subject_nr\": nr, \"condition\": cond,\n",
    "            \"delta_power_N2\": dp_n2, \"delta_power_N3\": dp_n3,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={nr:02d} 完了\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_swa_stage = pd.DataFrame(swa_stage_records)\n",
    "df_swa_stage_wide = df_swa_stage.pivot(\n",
    "    index=\"subject_nr\", columns=\"condition\",\n",
    "    values=[\"delta_power_N2\", \"delta_power_N3\"]\n",
    ")\n",
    "df_swa_stage_wide.columns = [f\"{a}_{b}\" for a, b in df_swa_stage_wide.columns]\n",
    "df_swa_stage_wide = df_swa_stage_wide.reset_index()\n",
    "df_swa_stage_wide[\"Ddelta_power_N2\"] = (\n",
    "    df_swa_stage_wide[\"delta_power_N2_Temazepam\"] - df_swa_stage_wide[\"delta_power_N2_Placebo\"]\n",
    ")\n",
    "df_swa_stage_wide[\"Ddelta_power_N3\"] = (\n",
    "    df_swa_stage_wide[\"delta_power_N3_Temazepam\"] - df_swa_stage_wide[\"delta_power_N3_Placebo\"]\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ΔCHI (N2単独, N3単独)\n",
    "chi_n2 = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == \"N2\"][[\"subject_nr\", \"ΔCHI\"]].rename(\n",
    "    columns={\"ΔCHI\": \"DELTA_CHI_N2\"})\n",
    "chi_n3 = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == \"N3\"][[\"subject_nr\", \"ΔCHI\"]].rename(\n",
    "    columns={\"ΔCHI\": \"DELTA_CHI_N3\"})\n",
    "\n",
    "df_sens = df_swa_stage_wide.merge(chi_n2, on=\"subject_nr\", how=\"left\") \\\n",
    "                           .merge(chi_n3, on=\"subject_nr\", how=\"left\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 3本立て解析: N2+N3統合(主) / N2単独 / N3単独 ---\n",
    "results = {}\n",
    "\n",
    "# 主解析: N2+N3統合 (既存 df_swa_chi を使用)\n",
    "mask_main = df_swa_chi[[\"Ddelta_power\", \"DELTA_CHI\"]].notna().all(axis=1)\n",
    "x_main = df_swa_chi.loc[mask_main, \"Ddelta_power\"].values\n",
    "y_main = df_swa_chi.loc[mask_main, \"DELTA_CHI\"].values\n",
    "rho_main, p_main = spearmanr(x_main, y_main)\n",
    "ci_lo_main, ci_hi_main, nboot_main = bootstrap_spearman_ci(x_main, y_main)\n",
    "results[\"N2+N3 (主解析)\"] = dict(n=len(x_main), rho=rho_main, p=p_main,\n",
    "                                  ci_lo=ci_lo_main, ci_hi=ci_hi_main)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Sensitivity: N2単独\n",
    "mask_n2 = df_sens[[\"Ddelta_power_N2\", \"DELTA_CHI_N2\"]].notna().all(axis=1)\n",
    "x_n2 = df_sens.loc[mask_n2, \"Ddelta_power_N2\"].values\n",
    "y_n2 = df_sens.loc[mask_n2, \"DELTA_CHI_N2\"].values\n",
    "rho_n2, p_n2 = spearmanr(x_n2, y_n2)\n",
    "ci_lo_n2, ci_hi_n2, nboot_n2 = bootstrap_spearman_ci(x_n2, y_n2)\n",
    "results[\"N2単独 (sensitivity)\"] = dict(n=len(x_n2), rho=rho_n2, p=p_n2,\n",
    "                                        ci_lo=ci_lo_n2, ci_hi=ci_hi_n2)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Sensitivity: N3単独\n",
    "mask_n3 = df_sens[[\"Ddelta_power_N3\", \"DELTA_CHI_N3\"]].notna().all(axis=1)\n",
    "x_n3 = df_sens.loc[mask_n3, \"Ddelta_power_N3\"].values\n",
    "y_n3 = df_sens.loc[mask_n3, \"DELTA_CHI_N3\"].values\n",
    "rho_n3, p_n3 = spearmanr(x_n3, y_n3)\n",
    "ci_lo_n3, ci_hi_n3, nboot_n3 = bootstrap_spearman_ci(x_n3, y_n3)\n",
    "results[\"N3単独 (sensitivity)\"] = dict(n=len(x_n3), rho=rho_n3, p=p_n3,\n",
    "                                        ci_lo=ci_lo_n3, ci_hi=ci_hi_n3)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- サマリー表示 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 78)\n",
    "print(f\"ΔSWA vs ΔCHI 相関 — Main + Sensitivity Analysis (bootstrap 95%CI, n_boot={N_BOOT})\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 78)\n",
    "print(f\"{'解析':<22} {'n':>4} {'rho':>8} {'p':>8} {'95%CI':>20}\")\n",
    "print(\"-\" * 78)\n",
    "for label, r in results.items():\n",
    "    print(f\"{label:<22} {r['n']:>4} {r['rho']:>8.3f} {r['p']:>8.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"[{r['ci_lo']:>+.3f}, {r['ci_hi']:>+.3f}]\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 一貫性チェック ---\n",
    "# 符号規約: Ddelta_power = SWA(T-P) (正=SWA増加), DELTA_CHI = CHI(T-P) (負=CHI低下)。\n",
    "# 原稿 (Discussion) の予測は「CHI低下が大きいほどSWA増加が大きい」、\n",
    "# すなわち -ΔCHI と +ΔSWA が正の関係 = ΔCHI と ΔSWA は正相関が予測どおり。\n",
    "all_positive = all(r[\"rho\"] > 0 for r in results.values())\n",
    "print(f\"\\n3解析すべて正相関 (原稿の予測と整合): {'OK Yes' if all_positive else 'WARN No'}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 論文記載用テキスト (English) ---\n",
    "r_main = results[\"N2+N3 (主解析)\"]\n",
    "r_n2   = results[\"N2単独 (sensitivity)\"]\n",
    "r_n3   = results[\"N3単独 (sensitivity)\"]\n",
    "print(\"\\n── 論文記載用テキスト (English) ──\")\n",
    "print(\n",
    "    \"To test whether temazepam-induced increases in slow-wave activity (SWA, \"\n",
    "    \"0.5-4 Hz power) were associated with reductions in CHI, we performed a \"\n",
    "    \"within-subject difference correlation (Delta = Temazepam - Placebo) at the \"\n",
    "    \"individual level. As predicted, Delta-SWA and Delta-CHI were positively \"\n",
    "    \"correlated (i.e., larger SWA increases co-occurred with larger CHI reductions, \"\n",
    "    \"consistent with the hypothesized positive relationship between CHI reduction \"\n",
    "    \"magnitude and SWA increase). In the primary analysis (N2+N3 combined, n=\" + str(r_main[\"n\"]) +\n",
    "    \"), this correlation was rho=\" +\n",
    "    f\"{r_main['rho']:.3f}\" + \" (p=\" + f\"{r_main['p']:.4f}\" +\n",
    "    \", bootstrap 95% CI [\" + f\"{r_main['ci_lo']:.3f}\" + \", \" + f\"{r_main['ci_hi']:.3f}\" +\n",
    "    \"]). Sensitivity analyses restricted to N2 alone (n=\" + str(r_n2[\"n\"]) + \": rho=\" +\n",
    "    f\"{r_n2['rho']:.3f}\" + \", p=\" + f\"{r_n2['p']:.4f}\" + \") and N3 alone (n=\" +\n",
    "    str(r_n3[\"n\"]) + \": rho=\" + f\"{r_n3['rho']:.3f}\" + \", p=\" + f\"{r_n3['p']:.4f}\" +\n",
    "    \") showed correlations of consistent (positive) direction and magnitude, \"\n",
    "    \"supporting the robustness of the SWA-CHI relationship across slow-wave sleep stages.\"\n",

    "\n",
    "# --- CSV保存 ---\n",
    "df_sens_full = df_swa_chi.merge(\n",

    "print(f\"出力ファイル: {sens_csv_path}\")\n",

    "# --- 3パネル散布図 (N2+N3 / N2 / N3) ---\n",

   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7c_swa_direction_test"

   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7c: SWA群平均の方向検定 (Temazepam vs Placebo)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: Ddelta_power (= SWA_T - SWA_P) の符号・群平均を確認する。\n",
    "#       ΔSWA-ΔCHI相関 (rho>0) の解釈は、SWAが平均的に増加しているか\n",
    "#       減少しているかによって全く異なる物語になるため必須のチェック。\n",
    "\n",
    "from scipy.stats import wilcoxon\n",
    "\n",
    "def report_delta_power_direction(label, delta_values):\n",
    "    delta_values = np.asarray(delta_values)\n",
    "    delta_values = delta_values[~np.isnan(delta_values)]\n",
    "    n = len(delta_values)\n",
    "    mean_d = np.mean(delta_values)\n",
    "    median_d = np.median(delta_values)\n",
    "    sd_d = np.std(delta_values, ddof=1)\n",
    "    n_pos = int(np.sum(delta_values > 0))\n",
    "    n_neg = int(np.sum(delta_values < 0))\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        stat, p = wilcoxon(delta_values)\n",
    "    except ValueError:\n",
    "        stat, p = np.nan, np.nan\n",
    "    direction = \"SWA増加 (Temazepam > Placebo)\" if mean_d > 0 else \"SWA減少 (Temazepam < Placebo)\"\n",
    "    print(f\"{label:<14} n={n:>3}  mean={mean_d:>+9.3f}  median={median_d:>+9.3f}  \"\n",
    "          f\"SD={sd_d:>8.3f}  positive={n_pos:>2}/{n}  Wilcoxon p={p:.4f}  -> {direction}\")\n",
    "    return dict(label=label, n=n, mean=mean_d, median=median_d, sd=sd_d,\n",
    "                n_pos=n_pos, n_neg=n_neg, wilcoxon_p=p)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"SWA (0.5-4 Hz delta power) 群平均の方向検定: Ddelta_power = SWA(Temazepam) - SWA(Placebo)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "\n",
    "swa_direction_results = []\n",
    "swa_direction_results.append(\n",
    "    report_delta_power_direction(\"N2+N3\", df_swa_chi[\"Ddelta_power\"].values)\n",
    ")\n",
    "swa_direction_results.append(\n",
    "    report_delta_power_direction(\"N2単独\", df_sens[\"Ddelta_power_N2\"].values)\n",
    ")\n",
    "swa_direction_results.append(\n",
    "    report_delta_power_direction(\"N3単独\", df_sens[\"Ddelta_power_N3\"].values)\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"参考: 同じ方向検定をΔCHIについても実施\")\n",
    "print(\"-\" * 100)\n",
    "chi_direction_results = []\n",
    "chi_direction_results.append(\n",
    "    report_delta_power_direction(\"ΔCHI N2+N3\", df_swa_chi[\"DELTA_CHI\"].values)\n",
    ")\n",
    "chi_direction_results.append(\n",
    "    report_delta_power_direction(\"ΔCHI N2\", df_sens[\"DELTA_CHI_N2\"].values)\n",
    ")\n",
    "chi_direction_results.append(\n",
    "    report_delta_power_direction(\"ΔCHI N3\", df_sens[\"DELTA_CHI_N3\"].values)\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 解釈ガイド ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"解釈ガイド\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "mean_swa_n2n3 = swa_direction_results[0][\"mean\"]\n",
    "if mean_swa_n2n3 > 0:\n",
    "    print(\"  SWAは群平均でTemazepam > Placebo (増加) -> 'SWA増強がCHI低下を媒介する' という\")\n",
    "    print(\"  原稿の機序記述 (既知薬理 [13] とも整合) は、相関の解釈としてそのまま使用可能。\")\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(\"  SWAは群平均でTemazepam < Placebo (減少) -> 'SWA増強がCHI低下を媒介する' という\")\n",
    "    print(\"  記述は不正確。正の相関 (rho>0) は成立するが、解釈は\")\n",
    "    print(\"  'ΔSWAとΔCHIは同方向に変化する (両方とも負、または両方とも正の被験者が多い)' という\")\n",
    "    print(\"  より中立的な記述に修正する必要がある。本文・Discussionの該当箇所を要再確認。\")\n"
   ]
  },

   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7d_swa_diagnosis"

   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7d: SWA計算の診断 (バグ切り分け)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: 「TemazepamでSWAが減少」という結果が、計算上のバグ\n",
    "#       (ファイル割当の逆転、welchのスケーリング、単位の二重変換等)\n",
    "#       によるものでないかを切り分ける。\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[診断1] pairs のファイル割当を確認 (先頭3被験者)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "for p in pairs[:3]:\n",
    "    print(f\"subject_nr={p['subject_nr']}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  placebo_psg = {p['placebo_psg']}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  placebo_hyp = {p['placebo_hyp']}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  temaz_psg   = {p['temaz_psg']}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  temaz_hyp   = {p['temaz_hyp']}\")\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 診断2: 1被験者・N2ステージで生のWelch PSDを直接確認 ---\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[診断2] 1被験者 (先頭) のN2ステージで生PSDを直接確認\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "\n",
    "diag_subject = pairs[0]\n",
    "nr = diag_subject[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "print(f\"対象 subject_nr = {nr}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "def diagnose_delta_power(psg_path, hyp_path, label, target_stages=(\"N2\",), max_epochs_print=5):\n",
    "    raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "    sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "    actual_fs = int(raw.info[\"sfreq\"])\n",
    "    print(f\"  [{label}] file={os.path.basename(psg_path)}  fs={actual_fs}  \"\n",
    "          f\"n_samples={len(sig)}  duration_min={len(sig)/actual_fs/60:.1f}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  [{label}] signal stats: mean={np.mean(sig):.3f} uV  std={np.std(sig):.3f} uV  \"\n",
    "          f\"min={np.min(sig):.1f}  max={np.max(sig):.1f}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "    # ステージ分布を確認\n",
    "    win_samp = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "    n_epochs_total = len(sig) // win_samp\n",
    "    stage_counts = {}\n",
    "    for ep in range(n_epochs_total):\n",
    "        st = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, ep * WIN_SEC)\n",
    "        stage_counts[st] = stage_counts.get(st, 0) + 1\n",
    "    print(f\"  [{label}] ステージ分布: {stage_counts}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "    delta_powers = []\n",
    "    printed = 0\n",
    "    for ep in range(n_epochs_total):\n",
    "        t0 = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        if stage not in target_stages:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        x = sig[ep * win_samp: (ep + 1) * win_samp]\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > 500:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        freqs, psd = welch(x, fs=actual_fs, nperseg=min(256, len(x)))\n",
    "        delta_mask = (freqs >= 0.5) & (freqs <= 4.0)\n",
    "        dp = np.mean(psd[delta_mask])\n",
    "        delta_powers.append(dp)\n",
    "        if printed < max_epochs_print:\n",
    "            print(f\"    epoch {ep}: stage={stage}  delta_band_power={dp:.4f}  \"\n",
    "                  f\"(n_freq_bins_in_band={delta_mask.sum()}, \"\n",
    "                  f\"freq_range_used=[{freqs[delta_mask].min():.2f},{freqs[delta_mask].max():.2f}]Hz, \"\n",
    "                  f\"total_psd_range=[{psd.min():.4f},{psd.max():.4f}])\")\n",
    "            printed += 1\n",
    "\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    delta_powers = np.array(delta_powers)\n",
    "    print(f\"  [{label}] {target_stages} epochs used = {len(delta_powers)}, \"\n",
    "          f\"mean delta power = {np.mean(delta_powers):.4f}, \"\n",
    "          f\"median = {np.median(delta_powers):.4f}\")\n",
    "    return delta_powers\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\n--- PLACEBO ---\")\n",
    "dp_placebo = diagnose_delta_power(\n",
    "    diag_subject[\"placebo_psg\"], diag_subject[\"placebo_hyp\"], \"Placebo\", target_stages=(\"N2\",))\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\n--- TEMAZEPAM ---\")\n",
    "dp_temaz = diagnose_delta_power(\n",
    "    diag_subject[\"temaz_psg\"], diag_subject[\"temaz_hyp\"], \"Temazepam\", target_stages=(\"N2\",))\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(f\"[診断2 結論] subject {nr}, N2: \"\n",
    "      f\"Placebo mean={np.mean(dp_placebo):.4f}  vs  Temazepam mean={np.mean(dp_temaz):.4f}  \"\n",
    "      f\"-> Delta(T-P) = {np.mean(dp_temaz) - np.mean(dp_placebo):.4f}\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 診断3: welchのスケーリング設定を確認 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[診断3] scipy.signal.welch のデフォルト引数を確認 (scaling, window, detrend)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "import inspect\n",
    "sig_welch = inspect.signature(welch)\n",
    "for name, param in sig_welch.parameters.items():\n",
    "    if name in (\"scaling\", \"window\", \"detrend\", \"nperseg\", \"noverlap\"):\n",
    "        print(f\"  {name} = {param.default}\")\n",
    "print(\"  -> scaling='density' なら単位は V**2/Hz (PSD)。\")\n",
    "print(\"     'spectrum' であれば V**2 (パワースペクトル)。本コードは引数未指定 = density がデフォルト。\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 診断4: 既存のCHI計算パイプラインと同じステージ判定/ファイル読み込みを使っているか比較 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[診断4] CHI計算で使われている関数と本diagnose関数が同じ raw 読み込み/ステージ判定を使っているか確認\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"  PRIMARY_CH =\", PRIMARY_CH)\n",
    "print(\"  WIN_SEC =\", WIN_SEC)\n",
    "print(\"  -> compute_delta_power_stage 内の mne.io.read_raw_edf / get_stage_at の呼び出しが\")\n",
    "print(\"     CHI計算セル (step1-2付近) のものと一致しているか、上のセル定義を目視確認してください。\")\n"
   ]
