  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7e_amplitude_check"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7e: 全被験者での信号振幅 (Placebo vs Temazepam) 系統チェック\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: diag2でsubject 1のPlacebo夜がTemazepam夜よりSD約15倍・DCオフセット\n",
    "#       -206uVという異常な値を示した。これが単発の異常記録か、ST cohort全体に\n",
    "#       系統的に存在する記録条件差 (アンプ較正・電極状態等) かを確認する。\n",
    "#       系統的であれば、ΔSWAの逆転方向は生理学的効果ではなく記録品質の\n",
    "#       交絡によって説明できる可能性が高い。\n",
    "\n",
    "def signal_amplitude_stats(psg_path):\n",
    "    raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "    sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    return dict(\n",
    "        mean=float(np.mean(sig)),\n",
    "        std=float(np.std(sig)),\n",
    "        abs_max=float(np.max(np.abs(sig))),\n",
    "        pct_over_500uv=float(np.mean(np.abs(sig) > 500) * 100),\n",
    "    )\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"全被験者の信号振幅統計を計算中 (ST 22被験者 x 2夜)...\")\n",
    "amp_records = []\n",
    "for p in pairs:\n",
    "    nr = p[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "    stats_p = signal_amplitude_stats(p[\"placebo_psg\"])\n",
    "    stats_t = signal_amplitude_stats(p[\"temaz_psg\"])\n",
    "    amp_records.append({\n",
    "        \"subject_nr\": nr,\n",
    "        \"placebo_mean\": stats_p[\"mean\"], \"placebo_std\": stats_p[\"std\"],\n",
    "        \"placebo_absmax\": stats_p[\"abs_max\"], \"placebo_pct_over_500uv\": stats_p[\"pct_over_500uv\"],\n",
    "        \"temaz_mean\": stats_t[\"mean\"], \"temaz_std\": stats_t[\"std\"],\n",
    "        \"temaz_absmax\": stats_t[\"abs_max\"], \"temaz_pct_over_500uv\": stats_t[\"pct_over_500uv\"],\n",
    "        \"std_ratio_P_over_T\": stats_p[\"std\"] / stats_t[\"std\"] if stats_t[\"std\"] > 0 else np.nan,\n",
    "    })\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={nr:02d}  Placebo SD={stats_p['std']:8.2f} uV (>500uV: {stats_p['pct_over_500uv']:5.2f}%)   \"\n",
    "          f\"Temazepam SD={stats_t['std']:8.2f} uV (>500uV: {stats_t['pct_over_500uv']:5.2f}%)   \"\n",
    "          f\"ratio(P/T)={amp_records[-1]['std_ratio_P_over_T']:.2f}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_amp = pd.DataFrame(amp_records)\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"信号振幅 (SD) の群比較: Placebo vs Temazepam\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(df_amp[[\"placebo_std\", \"temaz_std\", \"std_ratio_P_over_T\"]].describe().to_string())\n",
    "\n",
    "stat_amp, p_amp = wilcoxon(df_amp[\"placebo_std\"], df_amp[\"temaz_std\"])\n",
    "print(f\"\\nWilcoxon (Placebo SD vs Temazepam SD): stat={stat_amp:.2f}, p={p_amp:.4f}\")\n",
    "n_p_larger = int((df_amp[\"placebo_std\"] > df_amp[\"temaz_std\"]).sum())\n",
    "print(f\"Placebo SD > Temazepam SD: {n_p_larger}/{len(df_amp)} 被験者\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"解釈ガイド\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "if p_amp < 0.05 and n_p_larger >= len(df_amp) * 0.7:\n",
    "    print(\"  -> Placebo夜の信号振幅がTemazepam夜より系統的に大きい (有意)。\")\n",
    "    print(\"     これはECSoC論文のNegative-Control limitations (point 9) で既に議論されている\")\n",
    "    print(\"     'ST/SC間およびナイト間の記録条件差' と同種の交絡が、\")\n",
    "    print(\"     同一被験者のPlacebo/Temazepam夜間にも存在する可能性を示唆する。\")\n",
    "    print(\"     -> ΔSWAの逆転方向 (Temazepam < Placebo) は、生理学的なSWA減少ではなく、\")\n",
    "    print(\"        記録振幅の系統差によるartefactual な delta-band power 水増しである疑いが強い。\")\n",
    "    print(\"     -> 対応: (1) 振幅正規化 (z-score化 or 相対パワー化) してから再計算、\")\n",
    "    print(\"              (2) より厳格なartefact閾値 (例: 200uV) での再計算、\")\n",
    "    print(\"              (3) 結果次第でSWA-CHI相関セクションの記述・解釈を全面的に見直す。\")\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(\"  -> Placebo/Temazepam間で振幅の系統差は明確ではない。\")\n",
    "    print(\"     SWA減少という結果は記録振幅の交絡だけでは説明しきれない可能性がある。\")\n",
    "\n",
    "amp_csv_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_signal_amplitude_check.csv\")\n",
    "df_amp.to_csv(amp_csv_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f\"\\n出力ファイル: {amp_csv_path}\")\n"
   ]
  },

   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7f_strict_artifact_recompute"

   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7f: 厳格なartefact閾値でのSWA再計算 (頑健性チェック)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: 全被験者振幅チェック (7e) でPlacebo夜のSDがTemazepam夜より系統的に\n",
    "#       大きいことが判明 (p=0.0093, 中央比1.55, 一部被験者で5-15倍)。\n",
    "#       500uV閾値では捕捉しきれない低周波ドリフト/アーティファクトの混入を疑い、\n",
    "#       より厳格な閾値 (150uV) でエポックを再選別し、SWA群平均と\n",
    "#       SWA-CHI相関がどう変化するかを直接確認する。\n",
    "\n",
    "STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV = 150.0\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_delta_power_stage_strict(psg_path, hyp_path, target_stages,\n",
    "                                      artifact_uv=STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV):\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(\n",
    "            psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "        sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "        actual_fs = int(raw.info[\"sfreq\"])\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f\"  [WARN] {e}\")\n",
    "        return np.nan, 0, 0\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "    win_samp = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "    delta_powers = []\n",
    "    n_stage_total = 0\n",
    "    for ep in range(len(sig) // win_samp):\n",
    "        t0 = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        if stage not in target_stages:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        n_stage_total += 1\n",
    "        x = sig[ep * win_samp : (ep + 1) * win_samp]\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > artifact_uv:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        freqs, psd = welch(x, fs=actual_fs, nperseg=min(256, len(x)))\n",
    "        delta_mask = (freqs >= 0.5) & (freqs <= 4.0)\n",
    "        delta_powers.append(np.mean(psd[delta_mask]))\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    n_kept = len(delta_powers)\n",
    "    return (np.mean(delta_powers) if delta_powers else np.nan), n_kept, n_stage_total\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f\"厳格閾値 ({STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV} uV) でN2+N3デルタパワーを再計算中...\")\n",
    "strict_records = []\n",
    "for p in pairs:\n",
    "    nr = p[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "    for cond, psg_key, hyp_key in [\n",
    "        (\"Placebo\",   \"placebo_psg\", \"placebo_hyp\"),\n",
    "        (\"Temazepam\", \"temaz_psg\",   \"temaz_hyp\"),\n",
    "    ]:\n",
    "        dp, n_kept, n_total = compute_delta_power_stage_strict(\n",
    "            p[psg_key], p[hyp_key], target_stages=(\"N2\", \"N3\"))\n",
    "        strict_records.append({\n",
    "            \"subject_nr\": nr, \"condition\": cond,\n",
    "            \"delta_power_strict\": dp,\n",
    "            \"n_epochs_kept\": n_kept, \"n_epochs_total\": n_total,\n",
    "            \"pct_rejected\": 100 * (1 - n_kept / n_total) if n_total > 0 else np.nan,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={nr:02d} 完了\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_strict = pd.DataFrame(strict_records)\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"各条件での平均除外率 (厳格閾値 %d uV):\" % STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV)\n",
    "print(df_strict.groupby(\"condition\")[\"pct_rejected\"].mean())\n",
    "\n",
    "df_strict_wide = df_strict.pivot(\n",
    "    index=\"subject_nr\", columns=\"condition\", values=\"delta_power_strict\"\n",
    ").reset_index()\n",
    "df_strict_wide[\"Ddelta_power_strict\"] = (\n",
    "    df_strict_wide[\"Temazepam\"] - df_strict_wide[\"Placebo\"]\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ΔCHI (N2+N3) とマージ (既存 chi_n2n3 を再利用)\n",
    "df_strict_chi = pd.merge(df_strict_wide, chi_n2n3, on=\"subject_nr\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(f\"[厳格閾値 {STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV}uV] SWA群平均の方向検定\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "strict_direction = report_delta_power_direction(\n",
    "    \"N2+N3 (strict)\", df_strict_chi[\"Ddelta_power_strict\"].values)\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(f\"[厳格閾値 {STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV}uV] SWA-CHI相関 (再計算)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "mask_strict = df_strict_chi[[\"Ddelta_power_strict\", \"DELTA_CHI\"]].notna().all(axis=1)\n",
    "x_strict = df_strict_chi.loc[mask_strict, \"Ddelta_power_strict\"].values\n",
    "y_strict = df_strict_chi.loc[mask_strict, \"DELTA_CHI\"].values\n",
    "rho_strict, p_strict = spearmanr(x_strict, y_strict)\n",
    "ci_lo_strict, ci_hi_strict, _ = bootstrap_spearman_ci(x_strict, y_strict)\n",
    "print(f\"n={len(x_strict)}  rho={rho_strict:.3f}  p={p_strict:.4f}  \"\n",
    "      f\"95%CI=[{ci_lo_strict:+.3f}, {ci_hi_strict:+.3f}]\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"元の結果 (500uV閾値) との比較\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(f\"  500uV閾値: ΔSWA mean={swa_direction_results[0]['mean']:+.3f}  \"\n",
    "      f\"rho(ΔSWA,ΔCHI)={results['N2+N3 (主解析)']['rho']:.3f}\")\n",
    "print(f\"  {STRICT_ARTIFACT_UV:.0f}uV閾値: ΔSWA mean={strict_direction['mean']:+.3f}  \"\n",
    "      f\"rho(ΔSWA,ΔCHI)={rho_strict:.3f}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "if np.sign(strict_direction[\"mean\"]) != np.sign(swa_direction_results[0][\"mean\"]):\n",
    "    print(\"\\n  -> 閾値を厳格化するとΔSWAの符号が反転。500uV閾値での'SWA減少'という結果は\")\n",
    "    print(\"     アーティファクト混入による交絡だった可能性が高い。\")\n",
    "elif np.sign(strict_direction[\"mean\"]) == np.sign(swa_direction_results[0][\"mean\"]):\n",
    "    print(\"\\n  -> 閾値を厳格化してもΔSWAの符号は変化せず。'SWA減少'は\")\n",
    "    print(\"     単純なアーティファクト閾値の問題では説明できない。\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 振幅と除外率の相関 (どの被験者が影響を受けたか) ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"被験者別: 元の結果 vs 厳格閾値での結果 比較表\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "compare_df = df_swa_chi[[\"subject_nr\", \"Ddelta_power\", \"DELTA_CHI\"]].merge(\n",
    "    df_strict_chi[[\"subject_nr\", \"Ddelta_power_strict\"]], on=\"subject_nr\"\n",
    ").merge(\n",
    "    df_amp[[\"subject_nr\", \"std_ratio_P_over_T\"]], on=\"subject_nr\"\n",
    ")\n",
    "print(compare_df.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "\n",
    "strict_csv_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_SWA_strict_artifact_sensitivity.csv\")\n",
    "compare_df.to_csv(strict_csv_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f\"\\n出力ファイル: {strict_csv_path}\")\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step7g"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 7g: 正規化デルタパワーによるSWA-CHI関連の再検証\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 背景:\n",
    "#   絶対デルタパワー (uV^2/Hz) では Temazepam < Placebo という\n",
    "#   群平均方向が、artefact閾値を厳格化 (500uV -> 150uV) しても\n",
    "#   変わらなかった。一方で std_ratio_P_over_T (夜間振幅比) が\n",
    "#   被験者ごとに 0.2~15倍と大きく変動しており、これは増幅器\n",
    "#   ゲイン・インピーダンス等、夜間ごとの「信号スケール」自体が\n",
    "#   異なる可能性を示す。絶対パワーはこの記録条件差に汚染される\n",
    "#   ため、各夜ごとに信号スケールで正規化した指標で再検証する。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 正規化方式 (2種類):\n",
    "#   (A) 相対パワー比: delta(0.5-4Hz)power / broadband(0.5-40Hz)power\n",
    "#       -> 同一夜内のスペクトル形状のみを見る。ゲイン依存性をほぼ除去。\n",
    "#   (B) z-score正規化: 各夜のepoch全体内でdelta powerをz-score化してから\n",
    "#       N2/N3epochのみ平均。\n",
    "#       -> 夜全体のパワー分布を基準にするため、その夜の記録条件\n",
    "#          (ゲイン・インピーダンス) に対して相対的な強度を見る。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 出力:\n",
    "#   - 群平均の方向検定 (Temazepam vs Placebo) を両方式で実施\n",
    "#   - ΔSWA(正規化) vs ΔCHI のSpearman相関 (N2+N3, N2単独, N3単独)\n",
    "#   - 元の絶対パワー結果との比較表\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "from scipy.signal import welch\n",
    "from scipy.stats import spearmanr, wilcoxon\n",
    "\n",
    "ARTIFACT_THR_NORM = 500  # uV, 元の主解析と揃える (正規化なので閾値自体の影響は小さいはず)\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_norm_delta_power_night(psg_path, hyp_path, subject_nr, condition,\n",
    "                                    target_stages_list):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    1夜分のPSGについて、指定ステージ群ごとに\n",
    "      - 絶対delta power (参考, 既存と同じ)\n",
    "      - 相対delta power (delta / broadband)\n",
    "      - z-score化delta power (夜全体のepoch分布基準)\n",
    "    を計算して返す。\n",
    "\n",
    "    target_stages_list: 例 [(\"N2N3\", (\"N2\",\"N3\")), (\"N2\", (\"N2\",)), (\"N3\", (\"N3\",))]\n",
    "    戻り値: dict of {label: {\"abs\":..., \"rel\":..., \"z\":...}}\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(\n",
    "            psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "        sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "        actual_fs = int(raw.info[\"sfreq\"])\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f\"  [WARN] [{subject_nr} {condition}]: {e}\")\n",
    "        return {label: {\"abs\": np.nan, \"rel\": np.nan, \"z\": np.nan}\n",
    "                for label, _ in target_stages_list}\n",
    "\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "    win_samp = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "    n_ep = len(sig) // win_samp\n",
    "\n",
    "    # --- 夜全体を1パスでスキャンし、epochごとの delta power と\n",
    "    #     broadband power を全部保持する (z-score / 相対パワーの基準母集団) ---\n",
    "    epoch_records = []  # list of dict: stage, delta_power, broadband_power\n",
    "    for ep in range(n_ep):\n",
    "        t0 = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        if stage not in VALID_STAGES:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        x = sig[ep * win_samp: (ep + 1) * win_samp]\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > ARTIFACT_THR_NORM:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        freqs, psd = welch(x, fs=actual_fs, nperseg=min(256, len(x)))\n",
    "        delta_mask = (freqs >= 0.5) & (freqs <= 4.0)\n",
    "        broadband_mask = (freqs >= 0.5) & (freqs <= 40.0)\n",
    "        delta_p = np.mean(psd[delta_mask])\n",
    "        broadband_p = np.mean(psd[broadband_mask])\n",
    "        epoch_records.append({\n",
    "            \"stage\": stage,\n",
    "            \"delta_power\": delta_p,\n",
    "            \"broadband_power\": broadband_p,\n",
    "            \"rel_delta\": delta_p / broadband_p if broadband_p > 0 else np.nan,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "\n",
    "    df_night = pd.DataFrame(epoch_records)\n",
    "    out = {}\n",
    "    if len(df_night) == 0:\n",
    "        for label, _ in target_stages_list:\n",
    "            out[label] = {\"abs\": np.nan, \"rel\": np.nan, \"z\": np.nan}\n",
    "        del raw\n",
    "        return out\n",
    "\n",
    "    # z-score基準: その夜の全epoch (全ステージ) のdelta_power分布\n",
    "    night_mean = df_night[\"delta_power\"].mean()\n",
    "    night_std = df_night[\"delta_power\"].std(ddof=0)\n",
    "    if night_std > 0:\n",
    "        df_night[\"z_delta\"] = (df_night[\"delta_power\"] - night_mean) / night_std\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        df_night[\"z_delta\"] = np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "    for label, stages in target_stages_list:\n",
    "        sub = df_night[df_night[\"stage\"].isin(stages)]\n",
    "        if len(sub) == 0:\n",
    "            out[label] = {\"abs\": np.nan, \"rel\": np.nan, \"z\": np.nan}\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            out[label] = {\n",
    "                \"abs\": sub[\"delta_power\"].mean(),\n",
    "                \"rel\": sub[\"rel_delta\"].mean(),\n",
    "                \"z\":   sub[\"z_delta\"].mean(),\n",
    "            }\n",
    "\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    return out\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"正規化デルタパワー計算中 (ST 22被験者 x 2夜)...\")\n",
    "TARGET_STAGE_SETS = [(\"N2N3\", (\"N2\", \"N3\")), (\"N2\", (\"N2\",)), (\"N3\", (\"N3\",))]\n",
    "\n",
    "norm_records = []\n",
    "for p in pairs:\n",
    "    nr = p[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "    for cond, psg_key, hyp_key in [\n",
    "        (\"Placebo\",   \"placebo_psg\", \"placebo_hyp\"),\n",
    "        (\"Temazepam\", \"temaz_psg\",   \"temaz_hyp\"),\n",
    "    ]:\n",
    "        res = compute_norm_delta_power_night(\n",
    "            p[psg_key], p[hyp_key], nr, cond, TARGET_STAGE_SETS)\n",
    "        for label, vals in res.items():\n",
    "            norm_records.append({\n",
    "                \"subject_nr\": nr, \"condition\": cond, \"stage_label\": label,\n",
    "                \"abs_delta\": vals[\"abs\"], \"rel_delta\": vals[\"rel\"], \"z_delta\": vals[\"z\"],\n",
    "            })\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={nr:02d} 完了\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_norm = pd.DataFrame(norm_records)\n",
    "norm_out_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_SWA_normalized_raw.csv\")\n",
    "df_norm.to_csv(norm_out_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f\"\\n生データ保存: {norm_out_path}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 群平均の方向検定 (正規化指標、絶対パワーと並べて表示)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"群平均の方向検定 (Temazepam - Placebo): 絶対パワー vs 相対パワー vs z-score\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "\n",
    "direction_rows = []\n",
    "for label, _ in TARGET_STAGE_SETS:\n",
    "    sub = df_norm[df_norm[\"stage_label\"] == label]\n",
    "    wide_norm = sub.pivot(index=\"subject_nr\", columns=\"condition\",\n",
    "                           values=[\"abs_delta\", \"rel_delta\", \"z_delta\"])\n",
    "    for metric in [\"abs_delta\", \"rel_delta\", \"z_delta\"]:\n",
    "        p_vals = wide_norm[metric][\"Placebo\"]\n",
    "        t_vals = wide_norm[metric][\"Temazepam\"]\n",
    "        diff = (t_vals - p_vals).dropna()\n",
    "        if len(diff) < 4:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        try:\n",
    "            stat, pval = wilcoxon(diff)\n",
    "        except ValueError:\n",
    "            pval = np.nan\n",
    "        n_pos = int((diff > 0).sum())\n",
    "        direction = \"増加 (T>P)\" if diff.mean() > 0 else \"減少 (T<P)\"\n",
    "        direction_rows.append({\n",
    "            \"stage_label\": label, \"metric\": metric, \"n\": len(diff),\n",
    "            \"mean\": diff.mean(), \"median\": diff.median(), \"SD\": diff.std(),\n",
    "            \"positive\": f\"{n_pos}/{len(diff)}\", \"wilcoxon_p\": pval,\n",
    "            \"direction\": direction,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "        print(f\"{label:6s} {metric:12s} n={len(diff):3d}  mean={diff.mean():8.4f}  \"\n",
    "              f\"median={diff.median():8.4f}  positive={n_pos}/{len(diff)}  \"\n",
    "              f\"p={pval:.4f}  -> {direction}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_direction = pd.DataFrame(direction_rows)\n",
    "direction_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_SWA_normalized_direction.csv\")\n",
    "df_direction.to_csv(direction_path, index=False)\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# ΔSWA(正規化) vs ΔCHI 相関 (N2+N3 / N2単独 / N3単独 x rel / z)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"ΔSWA(正規化) vs ΔCHI 相関 (bootstrap 95%CI, n_boot=10000)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "\n",
    "if \"DELTA_CHI\" in wide.columns:\n",
    "    chi_col = \"DELTA_CHI\"\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    chi_col = \"DELTA_CHI\" if \"DELTA_CHI\" in wide.columns else \"\\u0394CHI\"\n",
    "\n",
    "chi_stage_map = {\n",
    "    \"N2N3\": [\"N2\", \"N3\"],\n",
    "    \"N2\":   [\"N2\"],\n",
    "    \"N3\":   [\"N3\"],\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "def bootstrap_ci_spearman(x, y, n_boot=10000, seed=42):\n",
    "    rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)\n",
    "    n = len(x)\n",
    "    boots = np.empty(n_boot)\n",
    "    x = np.asarray(x); y = np.asarray(y)\n",
    "    for i in range(n_boot):\n",
    "        idx = rng.integers(0, n, n)\n",
    "        r, _ = spearmanr(x[idx], y[idx])\n",
    "        boots[i] = r\n",
    "    lo, hi = np.percentile(boots, [2.5, 97.5])\n",
    "    return lo, hi\n",
    "\n",
    "corr_rows = []\n",
    "for label, stages in chi_stage_map.items():\n",
    "    chi_sub = wide[wide[\"stage\"].isin(stages)].groupby(\"subject_nr\")[chi_col].mean().reset_index()\n",
    "    chi_sub.columns = [\"subject_nr\", \"DELTA_CHI\"]\n",
    "\n",
    "    sub_norm = df_norm[df_norm[\"stage_label\"] == label]\n",
    "    wide_norm = sub_norm.pivot(index=\"subject_nr\", columns=\"condition\",\n",
    "                                values=[\"rel_delta\", \"z_delta\"])\n",
    "    # pivot後はMultiIndex列 (metric, condition) かつ index=subject_nr。\n",
    "    # reset_index()するとsubject_nrは単一階層になるが、元のMultiIndex列\n",
    "    # と混在するとmerge時にlevel数不一致でエラーになるため、subject_nrは\n",
    "    # indexから直接取得し、差分は配列として計算する。\n",
    "\n",
    "    for metric in [\"rel_delta\", \"z_delta\"]:\n",
    "        d = pd.DataFrame({\n",
    "            \"subject_nr\": wide_norm.index,\n",
    "            \"delta_metric\": (wide_norm[(metric, \"Temazepam\")]\n",
    "                              - wide_norm[(metric, \"Placebo\")]).values,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "        merged = pd.merge(d, chi_sub, on=\"subject_nr\")\n",
    "        merged = merged.dropna(subset=[\"delta_metric\", \"DELTA_CHI\"])\n",
    "        if len(merged) < 4:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        rho, pval = spearmanr(merged[\"delta_metric\"], merged[\"DELTA_CHI\"])\n",
    "        ci_lo, ci_hi = bootstrap_ci_spearman(\n",
    "            merged[\"delta_metric\"].values, merged[\"DELTA_CHI\"].values)\n",
    "        corr_rows.append({\n",
    "            \"stage_label\": label, \"metric\": metric, \"n\": len(merged),\n",
    "            \"rho\": rho, \"p\": pval, \"ci_lo\": ci_lo, \"ci_hi\": ci_hi,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "        print(f\"{label:6s} {metric:12s} n={len(merged):3d}  rho={rho:7.3f}  \"\n",
    "              f\"p={pval:.4f}  95%CI=[{ci_lo:+.3f}, {ci_hi:+.3f}]\")\n",
    "\n",
    "df_corr_norm = pd.DataFrame(corr_rows)\n",
    "corr_norm_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_SWA_normalized_correlation.csv\")\n",
    "df_corr_norm.to_csv(corr_norm_path, index=False)\n",
    "\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 絶対パワーとの比較サマリー\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"解釈ガイド\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\n",
    "\"\"\"\n",
    "本解析は、絶対デルタパワーで観察された 'Temazepam < Placebo' という\n",
    "群平均の方向が、夜間ごとの信号スケール差 (増幅器ゲイン等) によって\n",
    "説明可能かどうかを、2種類の正規化指標で検証するものである。\n",
    "\n",
    "(A) 相対パワー比 (delta/broadband):\n",
    "    同一夜内のスペクトル形状のみを反映するため、夜間ゲイン差の影響を\n",
    "    ほぼ受けない。絶対パワーと方向が一致すれば、'真の'生理学的効果と\n",
    "    解釈できる。方向が逆転・消失すれば、絶対パワーの所見はゲイン差の\n",
    "    人工物である可能性が高まる。\n",
    "\n",
    "(B) z-score正規化:\n",
    "    その夜のepoch全体の分布を基準とするため、ゲイン差を部分的に補正\n",
    "    しつつ、夜内でのN2/N3 deltaの相対的な強さを保持する。\n",
    "\n",
    "上記の方向検定・相関の結果を確認し、絶対パワー (500uV閾値: 減少,\n",
    "150uV閾値: 減少, rho=0.602->0.334) と比較すること。\n",
    "両方の正規化指標で 'Temazepam < Placebo' の方向が消失または逆転する\n",
    "場合、絶対パワーでの所見は記録条件差に起因する人工物である可能性が\n",
    "高く、Discussion・Limitationsの記述を「SWA-CHI関係は本データセットの\n",
    "記録条件の制約により評価不能」と修正することが適切と考えられる。\n",
    "逆に正規化後も同方向が残る場合は、より慎重に取り扱うべき、データに\n",
    "根拠のある所見として報告する必要がある。\n",
    "\"\"\"\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f\"出力ファイル:\")\n",
    "print(f\"  {norm_out_path}\")\n",
    "print(f\"  {direction_path}\")\n",
    "print(f\"  {corr_norm_path}\")\n"
   ]
  },

   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step9_order_effect"

   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 9: Order Effect (Night 1 vs Night 2 順序効果) 解析\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: Limitations point 10 で「a formal order-by-condition interaction\n",
    "#       analysis would be required」と明記されている検証を実施する。\n",
    "#       ST cohortではplacebo/temazepamの順序がcounterbalanceされているが、\n",
    "#       実際に順序 (どちらが1晩目だったか) がΔCHIに系統的な影響を与えて\n",
    "#       いないかを直接検定する。\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 被験者ごとのnight順序情報を取得 (pairsより) ---\n",
    "order_info = pd.DataFrame([\n",
    "    {\"subject_nr\": p[\"subject_nr\"],\n",
    "     \"placebo_night\": p[\"placebo_night\"],\n",
    "     \"temaz_night\": p[\"temaz_night\"],\n",
    "     # placebo_night==1 なら \"Placebo first\"、temaz_night==1 なら \"Temazepam first\"\n",
    "     \"order_group\": \"Placebo first\" if p[\"placebo_night\"] == 1 else \"Temazepam first\"}\n",
    "    for p in pairs\n",
    "])\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[1] Counterbalancing確認: Placebo-first / Temazepam-first の人数\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(order_info[\"order_group\"].value_counts())\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- N2+N3統合 ΔCHI を order_group別に比較 ---\n",
    "wide_order = wide.merge(order_info, on=\"subject_nr\", how=\"left\")\n",
    "wide_n2n3 = wide_order[wide_order[\"stage\"].isin([\"N2\", \"N3\"])]\n",
    "subj_dchi_n2n3 = wide_n2n3.groupby([\"subject_nr\", \"order_group\"])[\"ΔCHI\"].mean().reset_index()\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[2] ΔCHI (N2+N3) の順序群別記述統計\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(subj_dchi_n2n3.groupby(\"order_group\")[\"ΔCHI\"].agg([\"count\", \"mean\", \"std\", \"median\"]).round(4))\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- Mann-Whitney U検定: 順序によるΔCHIの違い ---\n",
    "g1 = subj_dchi_n2n3.loc[subj_dchi_n2n3[\"order_group\"] == \"Placebo first\", \"ΔCHI\"].values\n",
    "g2 = subj_dchi_n2n3.loc[subj_dchi_n2n3[\"order_group\"] == \"Temazepam first\", \"ΔCHI\"].values\n",
    "\n",
    "from scipy.stats import mannwhitneyu\n",
    "if len(g1) >= 2 and len(g2) >= 2:\n",
    "    u_stat, u_p = mannwhitneyu(g1, g2, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "    n1, n2 = len(g1), len(g2)\n",
    "    z_approx = (u_stat - n1 * n2 / 2) / np.sqrt(n1 * n2 * (n1 + n2 + 1) / 12)\n",
    "    r_effect = abs(z_approx) / np.sqrt(n1 + n2)\n",
    "    print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "    print(\"[3] Mann-Whitney U検定: ΔCHI (N2+N3) ~ order_group\")\n",
    "    print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "    print(f\"  Placebo first (n={n1}): mean={np.mean(g1):+.4f}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  Temazepam first (n={n2}): mean={np.mean(g2):+.4f}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  U={u_stat:.2f}, p={u_p:.4f}, r={r_effect:.3f}\")\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    u_p = np.nan\n",
    "    print(\"[3] サンプルサイズ不足のため検定スキップ\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- ステージ別 (N2, N3個別) でも同様の検定 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[4] ステージ別 order effect (N2単独 / N3単独)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "stage_order_results = {}\n",
    "for stage in [\"N2\", \"N3\"]:\n",
    "    sub = wide_order[wide_order[\"stage\"] == stage]\n",
    "    g1s = sub.loc[sub[\"order_group\"] == \"Placebo first\", \"ΔCHI\"].dropna().values\n",
    "    g2s = sub.loc[sub[\"order_group\"] == \"Temazepam first\", \"ΔCHI\"].dropna().values\n",
    "    if len(g1s) >= 2 and len(g2s) >= 2:\n",
    "        u_s, p_s = mannwhitneyu(g1s, g2s, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "        print(f\"  {stage}: Placebo-first n={len(g1s)} mean={np.mean(g1s):+.4f}  |  \"\n",
    "              f\"Temazepam-first n={len(g2s)} mean={np.mean(g2s):+.4f}  |  \"\n",
    "              f\"U={u_s:.2f}, p={p_s:.4f}\")\n",
    "        stage_order_results[stage] = dict(p=p_s, n1=len(g1s), n2=len(g2s))\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print(f\"  {stage}: サンプルサイズ不足\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 解釈ガイド ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"解釈ガイド\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "if not np.isnan(u_p):\n",
    "    if u_p >= 0.05:\n",
    "        print(\"  -> N2+N3統合のΔCHIに、検査順序 (Placebo-first vs Temazepam-first) による\")\n",
    "        print(\"     有意な系統差は認められない (p={:.4f} >= 0.05)。\".format(u_p))\n",
    "        print(\"     これはLimitations point 10の懸念に対する直接的な反証となり、\")\n",
    "        print(\"     within-subject N2/N3 CHI効果がorder effect (順序・馴化効果) では\")\n",
    "        print(\"     説明できないことを支持する。\")\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print(\"  -> N2+N3統合のΔCHIに、検査順序による有意な系統差が認められる\")\n",
    "        print(\"     (p={:.4f} < 0.05)。order effectが交絡している可能性があり、\".format(u_p))\n",
    "        print(\"     主効果の解釈には注意が必要。順序を共変量とした再解析を検討すべき。\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 出力 ---\n",
    "order_csv_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_order_effect.csv\")\n",
    "wide_order.to_csv(order_csv_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f\"\\n出力ファイル: {order_csv_path}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 論文記載用テキスト ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"── 論文記載用テキスト (English, Limitations point 10向け) ──\")\n",
    "if not np.isnan(u_p):\n",
    "    print(\n",
    "        f\"To directly test for an order-by-condition interaction, ΔCHI (N2+N3 combined) \"\n",
    "        f\"was compared between participants who received placebo on the first night \"\n",
    "        f\"(n={len(g1)}) and those who received temazepam on the first night (n={len(g2)}) \"\n",
    "        f\"using a two-sided Mann-Whitney U test. No significant difference was observed \"\n",
    "        f\"(U={u_stat:.2f}, p={u_p:.4f}), indicating that the within-subject N2/N3 CHI \"\n",
    "        f\"reduction is not attributable to a systematic first-night versus second-night \"\n",
    "        f\"order effect specific to the pharmacological manipulation.\"\n",
    "        if u_p >= 0.05 else\n",
    "        f\"To directly test for an order-by-condition interaction, ΔCHI (N2+N3 combined) \"\n",
    "        f\"was compared between participants who received placebo on the first night \"\n",
    "        f\"(n={len(g1)}) and those who received temazepam on the first night (n={len(g2)}) \"\n",
    "        f\"using a two-sided Mann-Whitney U test. A significant difference was observed \"\n",
    "        f\"(U={u_stat:.2f}, p={u_p:.4f}), indicating that order may confound the \"\n",
    "        f\"within-subject N2/N3 CHI effect and warranting further investigation.\"\n",
    "    )\n"
   ]

   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step9b_n3_order_individual"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 9b: N3 Order Effect の個別データ確認\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: N3単独でorder group間に有意差 (p=0.018) が出た原因が、\n",
    "#       1-2名の外れ値によるものか、群全体に広がるパターンかを確認する。\n",
    "\n",
    "n3_order = wide_order[wide_order[\"stage\"] == \"N3\"][\n",
    "    [\"subject_nr\", \"order_group\", \"ΔCHI\", \"age\", \"sex\"]\n",
    "].dropna(subset=[\"ΔCHI\"]).sort_values([\"order_group\", \"ΔCHI\"])\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[1] N3 ΔCHI 個別値 (順序群別、ΔCHI昇順)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(n3_order.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 記述統計 + 外れ値チェック (IQR法) ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[2] 群別記述統計 + IQR法による外れ値チェック\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "for grp_name, grp_df in n3_order.groupby(\"order_group\"):\n",
    "    vals = grp_df[\"ΔCHI\"].values\n",
    "    q1, q3 = np.percentile(vals, [25, 75])\n",
    "    iqr = q3 - q1\n",
    "    lo_fence, hi_fence = q1 - 1.5 * iqr, q3 + 1.5 * iqr\n",
    "    outliers = grp_df[(grp_df[\"ΔCHI\"] < lo_fence) | (grp_df[\"ΔCHI\"] > hi_fence)]\n",
    "    print(f\"\\n{grp_name} (n={len(vals)}):\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  mean={np.mean(vals):+.4f}  median={np.median(vals):+.4f}  \"\n",
    "          f\"SD={np.std(vals, ddof=1):.4f}  range=[{vals.min():+.4f}, {vals.max():+.4f}]\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  IQR fence = [{lo_fence:+.4f}, {hi_fence:+.4f}]\")\n",
    "    if len(outliers) > 0:\n",
    "        print(f\"  外れ値候補 ({len(outliers)}名):\")\n",
    "        print(outliers.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print(\"  外れ値候補: なし\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 外れ値を1名ずつ除外した場合のp値の頑健性チェック (leave-one-out) ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "print(\"[3] Leave-one-out 感度分析: 各被験者を1名ずつ除外してMann-Whitney再検定\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 100)\n",
    "loo_results = []\n",
    "for excl_nr in n3_order[\"subject_nr\"].values:\n",
    "    sub = n3_order[n3_order[\"subject_nr\"] != excl_nr]\n",
    "    g1 = sub.loc[sub[\"order_group\"] == \"Placebo first\", \"ΔCHI\"].values\n",
    "    g2 = sub.loc[sub[\"order_group\"] == \"Temazepam first\", \"ΔCHI\"].values\n",
    "    if len(g1) >= 2 and len(g2) >= 2:\n",
    "        _, p_loo = mannwhitneyu(g1, g2, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "        loo_results.append({\"excluded_subject\": excl_nr, \"p_value\": p_loo})\n",
    "\n",
    "df_loo = pd.DataFrame(loo_results).sort_values(\"p_value\")\n",
    "print(df_loo.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "n_still_sig = int((df_loo[\"p_value\"] < 0.05).sum())\n",
    "print(f\"\\n除外後もp<0.05を維持: {n_still_sig}/{len(df_loo)} 通り\")\n",
    "if n_still_sig == len(df_loo):\n",
    "    print(\"  -> 特定の1名に依存せず、群全体に広がるパターン。外れ値駆動ではない可能性が高い。\")\n",
    "elif n_still_sig <= len(df_loo) * 0.5:\n",
    "    print(\"  -> 半数以上の除外パターンでp>=0.05に転じる。少数の被験者に強く依存しており、\")\n",
    "    print(\"     外れ値駆動の可能性が高い。\")\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print(\"  -> 一部の被験者除外でp>=0.05に転じる。中間的な頑健性。\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 箱ひげ図 + 個別点プロット ---\n",
    "fig_n3, ax_n3 = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 5.5), facecolor=\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "ax_n3.set_facecolor(\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "groups_order = [\"Placebo first\", \"Temazepam first\"]\n",
    "box_data = [n3_order.loc[n3_order[\"order_group\"] == g, \"ΔCHI\"].values for g in groups_order]\n",
    "bp = ax_n3.boxplot(box_data, labels=groups_order, patch_artist=True, widths=0.5,\n",
    "                    showmeans=True, meanline=True)\n",
    "for patch, color in zip(bp[\"boxes\"], [\"#F0E68C\", \"#CC5566\"]):\n",
    "    patch.set_facecolor(color)\n",
    "    patch.set_alpha(0.4)\n",
    "for i, g in enumerate(groups_order, start=1):\n",
    "    vals = n3_order.loc[n3_order[\"order_group\"] == g, \"ΔCHI\"].values\n",
    "    jitter = np.random.default_rng(0).normal(0, 0.04, size=len(vals))\n",
    "    ax_n3.scatter(np.full(len(vals), i) + jitter, vals, color=\"#333333\", s=45, zorder=5, alpha=0.8)\n",
    "ax_n3.axhline(0, color=\"#5A6470\", lw=0.8, ls=\":\")\n",
    "ax_n3.set_ylabel(\"ΔCHI N3 (Temazepam − Placebo)\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "ax_n3.set_title(\"N3 ΔCHI by Night Order\\n(Mann-Whitney p=0.018)\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",

  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "ext_step10_alpha1_alpha2_decomposition"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 外部検証 Step 10: α₁ と α₂ の個別解析 (CHI分解)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 目的: CHI = 2(α₁ - α₂) を構成する2つのDFA指数を個別に検定し、\n",
    "#       N2/N3でのCHI低下が α₁ (短時間スケール) の変化主導か、\n",
    "#       α₂ (長時間スケール) の変化主導かを確認する。\n",
    "#       SHHS補足解析 (本文 Supplementary Analysis) では α₁ の段階的上昇が\n",
    "#       CHI勾配を駆動し α₂ は相対的に安定、という非対称パターンが報告されている。\n",
    "#       ここではST cohort本体 (within-subject, Temazepam vs Placebo) で\n",
    "#       同じ非対称性が見られるかを検証する。\n",
    "\n",
    "from scipy.stats import norm\n",
    "\n",
    "def rank_biserial_r(W_stat, n):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    Matched-pairs rank-biserial correlation (Kerby, 2014 simple-difference formula).\n",
    "    W_stat: scipy.stats.wilcoxon が返す統計量 (= min(W+, W-)、タイなし前提)。\n",
    "    z/sqrt(n) 近似と異なり、完全分離 (p が理論的下限に達する場合) でも\n",
    "    必ず [0, 1] に収まる。符号は delta_mean 側で別途表現する。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    S = n * (n + 1) / 2\n",
    "    return 1 - 2 * W_stat / S\n",
    "\n",
    "ALPHA_METRICS = {\n",
    "    \"alpha1\": (\"alpha1_mean_P\", \"alpha1_mean_T\", \"Δalpha1\"),\n",
    "    \"alpha2\": (\"alpha2_mean_P\", \"alpha2_mean_T\", \"Δalpha2\"),\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "alpha_results = []\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 90)\n",
    "print(\"Within-subject Wilcoxon検定: α₁ と α₂ 個別 (Temazepam vs Placebo)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 90)\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric, (col_p, col_t, col_d) in ALPHA_METRICS.items():\n",
    "    print(f\"\\n--- {metric} ---\")\n",
    "    # Δ列をwideに追加 (未作成の場合)\n",
    "    if col_d not in wide.columns:\n",
    "        wide[col_d] = wide[col_t] - wide[col_p]\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "        sub = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == stage][[col_p, col_t, col_d]].dropna()\n",
    "        n = len(sub)\n",
    "        if n < 5:\n",
    "            print(f\"  {stage}: n={n} (不足)\")\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        delta_mean = sub[col_d].mean()\n",
    "        delta_sd = sub[col_d].std()\n",
    "        try:\n",
    "            stat, p = wilcoxon(sub[col_t], sub[col_p], alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "        except Exception as e:\n",
    "            print(f\"  {stage}: Wilcoxon失敗 ({e})\")\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        r = rank_biserial_r(stat, n)\n",
    "        sig = \"***\" if p < 0.001 else \"**\" if p < 0.01 else \"*\" if p < 0.05 else \"ns\"\n",
    "        print(f\"  {stage}: n={n:2d}  Δ={delta_mean:+.4f}±{delta_sd:.4f}  \"\n",
    "              f\"W={stat:.0f}  p={p:.4f} {sig}  r={r:.3f}\")\n",
    "        alpha_results.append({\n",
    "            \"metric\": metric, \"stage\": stage, \"n\": n,\n",
    "            \"delta_mean\": delta_mean, \"delta_sd\": delta_sd,\n",
    "            \"W_stat\": stat, \"p_value\": p, \"effect_r\": r, \"sig\": sig,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "\n",
    "df_alpha = pd.DataFrame(alpha_results)\n",
    "alpha_csv_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_alpha1_alpha2_decomposition.csv\")\n",
    "df_alpha.to_csv(alpha_csv_path, index=False)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- N2, N3 における α₁ vs α₂ の変化量を直接比較 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 90)\n",
    "print(\"N2 / N3 における Δα₁ vs Δα₂ の比較 (どちらが主導か)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 90)\n",
    "for stage in [\"N2\", \"N3\"]:\n",
    "    row1 = df_alpha[(df_alpha[\"metric\"] == \"alpha1\") & (df_alpha[\"stage\"] == stage)]\n",
    "    row2 = df_alpha[(df_alpha[\"metric\"] == \"alpha2\") & (df_alpha[\"stage\"] == stage)]\n",
    "    if len(row1) == 0 or len(row2) == 0:\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    d1, p1, r1 = row1.iloc[0][[\"delta_mean\", \"p_value\", \"effect_r\"]]\n",
    "    d2, p2, r2 = row2.iloc[0][[\"delta_mean\", \"p_value\", \"effect_r\"]]\n",
    "    print(f\"\\n{stage}:\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  Δα₁ = {d1:+.4f} (p={p1:.4f}, r={r1:.3f})\")\n",
    "    print(f\"  Δα₂ = {d2:+.4f} (p={p2:.4f}, r={r2:.3f})\")\n",
    "    if abs(d1) > abs(d2) and p1 < 0.05 and p2 >= 0.05:\n",
    "        print(f\"  -> α₁主導パターン (SHHS補足解析と一致): \"\n",
    "              f\"α₁のみ有意に変化し、α₂は安定\")\n",
    "    elif abs(d2) > abs(d1) and p2 < 0.05 and p1 >= 0.05:\n",
    "        print(f\"  -> α₂主導パターン (SHHS補足解析と不一致): \"\n",
    "              f\"α₂のみ有意に変化し、α₁は安定\")\n",
    "    elif p1 < 0.05 and p2 < 0.05:\n",
    "        print(f\"  -> 両方とも有意に変化 (サチュレーション以外の複合作用)\")\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print(f\"  -> どちらも有意ではない / 明確な非対称性は見られない\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- α1/α2 散布図 (Placebo vs Temazepam, N2/N3) ---\n",
    "fig_a, axes_a = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(11, 5), facecolor=\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "for ax, stage in zip(axes_a, [\"N2\", \"N3\"]):\n",
    "    ax.set_facecolor(\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "    sub = wide[wide[\"stage\"] == stage]\n",
    "    ax.scatter(sub[\"alpha1_mean_P\"], sub[\"alpha1_mean_T\"], color=\"#CC5566\",\n",
    "               label=\"α₁\", alpha=0.8, s=40)\n",
    "    ax.scatter(sub[\"alpha2_mean_P\"], sub[\"alpha2_mean_T\"], color=\"#5588AA\",\n",
    "               label=\"α₂\", alpha=0.8, s=40, marker=\"^\")\n",
    "    lims = [min(ax.get_xlim()[0], ax.get_ylim()[0]), max(ax.get_xlim()[1], ax.get_ylim()[1])]\n",
    "    ax.plot(lims, lims, color=\"#999999\", lw=1, ls=\"--\")\n",
    "    ax.set_xlabel(\"Placebo\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "    ax.set_ylabel(\"Temazepam\", color=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "    ax.set_title(f\"{stage}: α₁ / α₂ Placebo vs Temazepam\", color=\"#1A1A1A\", fontsize=10)\n",
    "    ax.legend()\n",
    "    ax.tick_params(colors=\"#1A1A1A\")\n",
    "    for spine in ax.spines.values():\n",
    "        spine.set_edgecolor(\"#CCCCCC\")\n",
    "    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15)\n",
    "plt.tight_layout()\n",
    "alpha_fig_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"extval_alpha1_alpha2_scatter.png\")\n",
    "fig_a.savefig(alpha_fig_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches=\"tight\", facecolor=\"#FFFFFF\")\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "print(f\"\\n図保存: {alpha_fig_path}\")\n",
    "print(f\"出力ファイル: {alpha_csv_path}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 論文記載用テキスト ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(\"── 論文記載用テキスト (English) ──\")\n",
    "for stage in [\"N2\", \"N3\"]:\n",
    "    row1 = df_alpha[(df_alpha[\"metric\"] == \"alpha1\") & (df_alpha[\"stage\"] == stage)]\n",
    "    row2 = df_alpha[(df_alpha[\"metric\"] == \"alpha2\") & (df_alpha[\"stage\"] == stage)]\n",
    "    if len(row1) == 0 or len(row2) == 0:\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    d1, p1, r1, n1 = row1.iloc[0][[\"delta_mean\", \"p_value\", \"effect_r\", \"n\"]]\n",
    "    d2, p2, r2, n2 = row2.iloc[0][[\"delta_mean\", \"p_value\", \"effect_r\", \"n\"]]\n",
    "    print(f\"In {stage} (n={int(n1)}), temazepam was associated with Delta-alpha1 = \"\n",
    "          f\"{d1:+.3f} (p={p1:.4f}, r={r1:.3f}) and Delta-alpha2 = {d2:+.3f} \"\n",
    "          f\"(p={p2:.4f}, r={r2:.3f}).\")\n"
   ]

  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "sc_night_ctrl_intro"
   },
   "source": [
    "---\n",
    "# 陰性対照 2: SC群 夜1 vs 夜2 within-subject比較\n",
    "## 「薬剤なし条件での自然な夜間変動」の定量化\n",
    "\n",
    "### 設計・目的\n",
    "- **データ**: Sleep-EDF Expanded Cassette (SC群) — 各被験者の夜1 (SC4{ss}1E0) と夜2 (SC4{ss}2E0)\n",
    "- **比較**: Within-subject 夜1 vs 夜2 (Wilcoxon符号順位検定)\n",
    "- **薬剤**: なし (true negative)\n",
    "- **機材**: ST群と完全に同一の Sleep Cassette recorder → コホート間の系統差を完全排除\n",
    "\n",
    "### 解釈の枠組み\n",
    "| ΔCHI(SC夜1vs夜2) | 意味 |\n",
    "|---|---|\n",
    "| \\|ΔCHI\\| ≪ ST群(−0.15, −0.18) かつ ns | N2/N3 CHI低下はテマゼパム特異的 → 主張強化 |\n",
    "| \\|ΔCHI\\| ≈ ST群 かつ 有意 | 自然変動が同程度 → within-subject設計の頑健性を主張 |\n",
    "| \\|ΔCHI\\| ≈ ST群 かつ ns | 変動は大きいが非系統的 → 検出力議論が必要 |"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "sc_night_ctrl_step1_scan"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# SC夜間対照 Step 1: 夜1・夜2ペアのスキャン\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 命名規則: SC4{ss}{N}E0-PSG.edf  (N=1 or 2)\n",
    "# scan_sc_pairs()は夜1のみ取得しているため、夜2も別途取得\n",
    "\n",
    "def scan_sc_night_pairs(sc_dir):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    夜1・夜2両方が存在するSC被験者のペアリストを返す。\n",
    "    Returns: list of dict with keys\n",
    "        subject_nr, night1_psg, night1_hyp, night2_psg, night2_hyp\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    # 全PSGファイルをスキャン\n",
    "    psg_files = sorted(glob.glob(os.path.join(sc_dir, \"SC4*PSG.edf\")))\n",
    "    # {ss: {1: path, 2: path}} の辞書を構築\n",
    "    by_subj = defaultdict(dict)\n",
    "    for psg in psg_files:\n",
    "        fname = os.path.basename(psg)\n",
    "        try:\n",
    "            ss  = int(fname[3:5])\n",
    "            ngt = int(fname[5])\n",
    "        except (ValueError, IndexError):\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        if ngt in (1, 2):\n",
    "            by_subj[ss][ngt] = psg\n",
    "\n",
    "    pairs_sc_night = []\n",
    "    for ss in sorted(by_subj.keys()):\n",
    "        if 1 not in by_subj[ss] or 2 not in by_subj[ss]:\n",
    "            continue  # 両夜揃っている被験者のみ\n",
    "        p1 = by_subj[ss][1]\n",
    "        p2 = by_subj[ss][2]\n",
    "        fname1 = os.path.basename(p1)\n",
    "        fname2 = os.path.basename(p2)\n",
    "        # Hypnogram検索\n",
    "        h1 = glob.glob(os.path.join(sc_dir, f\"SC4{fname1[3:5]}1*Hypnogram*.edf\"))\n",
    "        h2 = glob.glob(os.path.join(sc_dir, f\"SC4{fname2[3:5]}2*Hypnogram*.edf\"))\n",
    "        pairs_sc_night.append({\n",
    "            \"subject_nr\":  ss,\n",
    "            \"night1_psg\":  p1,\n",
    "            \"night1_hyp\":  h1[0] if h1 else None,\n",
    "            \"night2_psg\":  p2,\n",
    "            \"night2_hyp\":  h2[0] if h2 else None,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "\n",
    "    return pairs_sc_night\n",
    "\n",
    "sc_night_pairs = scan_sc_night_pairs(SC_DIR)\n",
    "print(f\"両夜揃っているSC被験者数: {len(sc_night_pairs)}\")\n",
    "missing_hyp = sum(\n",
    "    1 for p in sc_night_pairs\n",
    "    if p[\"night1_hyp\"] is None or p[\"night2_hyp\"] is None\n",
    ")\n",
    "print(f\"Hypnogram欠損あり: {missing_hyp}\")\n",
    "for p in sc_night_pairs[:4]:\n",
    "    h1 = os.path.basename(p['night1_hyp']) if p['night1_hyp'] else '❌'\n",
    "    h2 = os.path.basename(p['night2_hyp']) if p['night2_hyp'] else '❌'\n",
    "    print(f\"  Nr={p['subject_nr']:02d}  \"\n",
    "          f\"夜1: {os.path.basename(p['night1_psg'])} ({h1})  \"\n",
    "          f\"夜2: {os.path.basename(p['night2_psg'])} ({h2})\")\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "sc_night_ctrl_step2_process"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# SC夜間対照 Step 2: 全被験者の夜1・夜2を処理\n",
    "# 既存の process_one_night() を再利用 — 新規コードなし\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "SC_NIGHT_CACHE = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"sc_night12_epochs_raw.csv\")\n",
    "\n",
    "if os.path.exists(SC_NIGHT_CACHE):\n",
    "    df_sc_n12 = pd.read_csv(SC_NIGHT_CACHE)\n",
    "    print(f\"既存キャッシュ読み込み: {len(df_sc_n12):,} エポック\")\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    sc_n12_results = []\n",
    "    for i, p in enumerate(sc_night_pairs):\n",
    "        nr = p[\"subject_nr\"]\n",
    "        print(f\"[{i+1:02d}/{len(sc_night_pairs)}] Nr={nr:02d}\")\n",
    "        for night_label, psg_key, hyp_key in [\n",
    "            (\"SC_Night1\", \"night1_psg\", \"night1_hyp\"),\n",
    "            (\"SC_Night2\", \"night2_psg\", \"night2_hyp\"),\n",
    "        ]:\n",
    "            df_night = process_one_night(\n",
    "                p[psg_key], p[hyp_key], nr, night_label\n",
    "            )\n",
    "            if df_night is not None:\n",
    "                sc_n12_results.append(df_night)\n",
    "        # 5被験者ごとに中間保存\n",
    "        if (i + 1) % 5 == 0 and sc_n12_results:\n",
    "            pd.concat(sc_n12_results, ignore_index=True).to_csv(\n",
    "                SC_NIGHT_CACHE, index=False)\n",
    "            print(f\"  → 中間保存\")\n",
    "\n",
    "    df_sc_n12 = pd.concat(sc_n12_results, ignore_index=True)\n",
    "    df_sc_n12.to_csv(SC_NIGHT_CACHE, index=False)\n",
    "    print(f\"SC夜1/夜2処理完了: {len(df_sc_n12):,} エポック\")\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "sc_night_ctrl_step3_wilcoxon"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# SC夜間対照 Step 3: 被験者平均 → ワイドフォーマット → Wilcoxon\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "sc_n12_valid = df_sc_n12[\n",
    "    df_sc_n12[\"stage\"].isin(VALID_STAGES) &\n",
    "    df_sc_n12[\"CHI\"].notna()\n",
    "].copy()\n",
    "print(f\"SC夜1/夜2 有効エポック: {len(sc_n12_valid):,}\")\n",
    "print(sc_n12_valid.groupby([\"condition\",\"stage\"])[\"CHI\"].count().unstack(fill_value=0))\n",
    "\n",
    "# 被験者×夜×ステージ の平均CHI\n",
    "sc_n12_means = sc_n12_valid.groupby(\n",
    "    [\"subject_nr\", \"condition\", \"stage\"]\n",
    ").agg(\n",
    "    n_epochs       = (\"CHI\",       \"count\"),\n",
    "    CHI_mean       = (\"CHI\",       \"mean\"),\n",
    "    alpha1_mean    = (\"alpha1\",    \"mean\"),\n",
    "    alpha2_mean    = (\"alpha2\",    \"mean\"),\n",
    "    R2_mean        = (\"R2\",        \"mean\"),\n",
    "    PhaseV_rate    = (\"PhaseV\",    \"mean\"),\n",
    "    D_eff_rel_mean = (\"D_eff_rel\", \"mean\"),\n",
    ").reset_index()\n",
    "\n",
    "# ワイド変換: 夜1・夜2を列に展開\n",
    "sc_n12_wide = sc_n12_means.pivot_table(\n",
    "    index=[\"subject_nr\", \"stage\"],\n",
    "    columns=\"condition\",\n",
    "    values=[\"CHI_mean\", \"alpha1_mean\", \"alpha2_mean\",\n",
    "            \"PhaseV_rate\", \"D_eff_rel_mean\", \"n_epochs\"]\n",
    ").reset_index()\n",
    "# フラット化\n",
    "sc_n12_wide.columns = [\n",
    "    \"_\".join(c).strip(\"_\") if c[1] else c[0]\n",
    "    for c in sc_n12_wide.columns\n",
    "]\n",
    "\n",
    "# ΔCHI (夜2 − 夜1) : テマゼパム比較と方向性を合わせるため夜2−夜1\n",
    "sc_n12_wide[\"ΔCHI_N2N1\"] = (\n",
    "    sc_n12_wide[\"CHI_mean_SC_Night2\"] - sc_n12_wide[\"CHI_mean_SC_Night1\"]\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "# Wilcoxon符号順位検定: ステージ別\n",
    "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 70)\n",
    "print(\"SC群 夜1 vs 夜2 CHI — Wilcoxon符号順位検定\")\n",
    "print(\"(陰性対照: 薬剤なし自然変動の定量化)\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 70)\n",
    "print(f\"{'Stage':<6} {'夜1 CHI':>16} {'夜2 CHI':>16} {'ΔCHI(N2-N1)':>14} \"\n",
    "      f\"{'W':>8} {'p':>8} {'sig':>5} {'r':>6}\")\n",
    "print(\"-\" * 80)\n",
    "\n",
    "sc_night_stat = []\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sub = sc_n12_wide[sc_n12_wide[\"stage\"] == stage].dropna(\n",
    "        subset=[\"CHI_mean_SC_Night1\", \"CHI_mean_SC_Night2\"]\n",
    "    )\n",
    "    n1_vals = sub[\"CHI_mean_SC_Night1\"].values\n",
    "    n2_vals = sub[\"CHI_mean_SC_Night2\"].values\n",
    "    delta   = sub[\"ΔCHI_N2N1\"].values\n",
    "    n = len(n1_vals)\n",
    "    if n < 4:\n",
    "        print(f\"{stage:<6} サンプル不足 (n={n})\")\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    stat, p = wilcoxon(n1_vals, n2_vals, alternative=\"two-sided\")\n",
    "    r   = rank_biserial_wilcoxon(n1_vals, n2_vals)  # ★修正: rank-biserial (bounded [-1,1], 旧Z/sqrt(N)近似を置換)\n",
    "    sig = \"***\" if p < 0.001 else \"**\" if p < 0.01 else \"*\" if p < 0.05 else \"ns\"\n",
    "    print(f\"{stage:<6} {np.mean(n1_vals):>+.4f}±{np.std(n1_vals):.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"{np.mean(n2_vals):>+.4f}±{np.std(n2_vals):.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"{np.mean(delta):>+.4f}±{np.std(delta):.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"{stat:>8.1f} {p:>8.4f} {sig:>5} {r:>6.3f}\")\n",
    "    sc_night_stat.append({\n",
    "        \"stage\":          stage,\n",
    "        \"n_subjects\":     n,\n",
    "        \"night1_CHI_mean\": np.mean(n1_vals),\n",
    "        \"night1_CHI_sd\":   np.std(n1_vals),\n",
    "        \"night2_CHI_mean\": np.mean(n2_vals),\n",
    "        \"night2_CHI_sd\":   np.std(n2_vals),\n",
    "        \"delta_mean\":     np.mean(delta),\n",
    "        \"delta_sd\":       np.std(delta),\n",
    "        \"W_stat\":         stat,\n",
    "        \"p_value\":        p,\n",
    "        \"effect_r\":       r,\n",
    "        \"sig\":            sig,\n",
    "    })\n",
    "\n",
    "df_sc_night_stat = pd.DataFrame(sc_night_stat)\n",
    "sc_stat_path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, \"sc_night1_vs_night2_wilcoxon.csv\")\n",
    "df_sc_night_stat.to_csv(sc_stat_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f\"\\n統計結果保存: {sc_stat_path}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 薬剤効果との大きさ比較 ---\n",
    "print(\"\\n\" + \"=\" * 70)\n",
    "print(\"ΔCHI 大きさ比較: SC自然変動 vs ST Temazepam効果\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 70)\n",
    "TEMAZEPAM_REF = {\"N2\": -0.15, \"N3\": -0.18}  # 既知ST群結果\n",
    "for stage in [\"N2\", \"N3\"]:\n",
    "    row = df_sc_night_stat[df_sc_night_stat[\"stage\"] == stage]\n",
    "    if len(row) == 0:\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    sc_d   = row.iloc[0][\"delta_mean\"]\n",
    "    st_ref = TEMAZEPAM_REF.get(stage, np.nan)\n",
    "    ratio  = abs(sc_d / st_ref) if st_ref != 0 else np.nan\n",
    "    p      = row.iloc[0][\"p_value\"]\n",
    "    sig    = row.iloc[0][\"sig\"]\n",
    "    print(f\"  {stage}: SC ΔCHI={sc_d:+.4f} ({sig}), \"\n",
    "          f\"ST Temazepam ΔCHI={st_ref:+.4f}, \"\n",
    "          f\"比率={ratio:.2f}x\")\n",
    "    if abs(sc_d) < abs(st_ref) * 0.5 and p >= 0.05:\n",
    "        print(f\"    ✅ 自然変動は薬剤効果の{ratio:.0%}以下かつ非有意 → 薬剤特異性を支持\")\n",
    "    elif abs(sc_d) >= abs(st_ref) * 0.7:\n",
    "        print(f\"    ⚠️  自然変動が薬剤効果の{ratio:.0%} → 非薬剤因子の関与を要検討\")\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print(f\"    ℹ️  中間的な変動幅 — 詳細解釈はDiscussionで\")\n"
   ]
  },

    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# SC夜間対照 Step 5: 統合サマリー & 論文用解釈\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 70)\n",
    "print(\"陰性対照 2: SC群 夜1 vs 夜2 — 統合サマリー\")\n",
    "print(\"=\" * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f\"\\n対象被験者数: {len(sc_night_pairs)} (両夜揃い)\")\n",
    "print(f\"使用ステージ: {', '.join(STAGE_ORDER)}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\n── CHI ステージ別 (夜2−夜1) ──\")\n",
    "print(f\"{'Stage':<6} {'夜1':>14} {'夜2':>14} {'Δ(N2-N1)':>12} \"\n",
    "      f\"{'p':>8} {'sig':>5} {'r':>6}\")\n",
    "print(\"-\" * 65)\n",
    "for _, row in df_sc_night_stat.iterrows():\n",
    "    print(f\"{row['stage']:<6} \"\n",
    "          f\"{row['night1_CHI_mean']:>+.4f}±{row['night1_CHI_sd']:.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"{row['night2_CHI_mean']:>+.4f}±{row['night2_CHI_sd']:.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"{row['delta_mean']:>+.4f}±{row['delta_sd']:.4f} \"\n",
    "          f\"{row['p_value']:>8.4f} {row['sig']:>5} {row['effect_r']:>6.3f}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\n── 薬剤効果との比較 (N2/N3) ──\")\n",
    "for stage, st_ref in [(\"N2\", -0.15), (\"N3\", -0.18)]:\n",
    "    row = df_sc_night_stat[df_sc_night_stat[\"stage\"] == stage]\n",
    "    if len(row) == 0:\n",
    "        print(f\"  {stage}: データなし\")\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    sc_d = row.iloc[0][\"delta_mean\"]\n",
    "    p    = row.iloc[0][\"p_value\"]\n",
    "    sig  = row.iloc[0][\"sig\"]\n",
    "    ratio = abs(sc_d / st_ref)\n",
    "    print(f\"  {stage}:  SC自然変動 ΔCHI = {sc_d:+.4f} ({sig})\")\n",
    "    print(f\"       ST薬剤効果 ΔCHI = {st_ref:+.4f}\")\n",
    "    print(f\"       SC/ST比 = {ratio:.2f}x\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\n── 論文記載用テキスト (English) ──\")\n",
    "n2_row = df_sc_night_stat[df_sc_night_stat[\"stage\"] == \"N2\"]\n",
    "n3_row = df_sc_night_stat[df_sc_night_stat[\"stage\"] == \"N3\"]\n",
    "if len(n2_row) > 0 and len(n3_row) > 0:\n",
    "    n2_d, n2_p, n2_sig = (\n",
    "        n2_row.iloc[0][\"delta_mean\"],\n",
    "        n2_row.iloc[0][\"p_value\"],\n",
    "        n2_row.iloc[0][\"sig\"]\n",
    "    )\n",
    "    n3_d, n3_p, n3_sig = (\n",
    "        n3_row.iloc[0][\"delta_mean\"],\n",
    "        n3_row.iloc[0][\"p_value\"],\n",
    "        n3_row.iloc[0][\"sig\"]\n",
    "    )\n",
    "    print(f\"\"\"\n",
    "To assess whether the observed CHI reductions under temazepam could\n",
    "reflect spontaneous night-to-night variability rather than drug effects,\n",
    "we performed a within-subject Night 1 vs. Night 2 comparison in the\n",
    "drug-free SC cohort (N={len(sc_night_pairs)}, both nights available, identical\n",
    "recording protocol). The natural night-to-night ΔCHI was\n",
    "{n2_d:+.3f} (N2, {n2_sig}) and {n3_d:+.3f} (N3, {n3_sig}), corresponding\n",
    "to {abs(n2_d/(-0.15)):.0%} and {abs(n3_d/(-0.18)):.0%} of the temazepam effect\n",
    "in the same stages (N2: −0.15, N3: −0.18). This indicates that the\n",
    "CHI suppression in N2/N3 under temazepam substantially exceeds\n",
    "spontaneous variability, supporting its pharmacological specificity.\n",
    "\"\"\")\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\n出力ファイル:\")\n",
    "for f in [\"sc_night12_epochs_raw.csv\",\n",
    "           \"sc_night1_vs_night2_wilcoxon.csv\",\n",
    "           \"sc_night1_vs_night2_negctrl.png\"]:\n",
    "    path = os.path.join(EXT_OUTPUT_DIR, f)\n",
    "    status = \"✓\" if os.path.exists(path) else \"✗\"\n",
    "    print(f\"  {status} {path}\")\n"
   ]

   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "nlcompare_intro"
   },
   "source": [
    "---\n",
    "# 補助解析: 他の非線形指標との比較 (Comparison with Other Nonlinear Metrics)\n",
    "## CHIが既存指標に対して増分的情報 (incremental information) を持つかの検証\n",
    "\n",
    "### 目的\n",
    "CHI (scale asymmetry) が単なる「もう一つの複雑性指標」ではなく、独自の情報を\n",
    "含むかどうかを、代表的な非線形・複雑性指標との直接比較によって検証する。\n",
    "\n",
    "### 比較指標\n",
    "- **Sample Entropy (SampEn)**: 信号の規則性・予測可能性 (m=2, r=0.2×SD)\n",
    "- **Permutation Entropy (PermEn)**: 順序パターンの多様性 (order=3, delay=1, 正規化)\n",
    "- **Lempel–Ziv Complexity (LZC)**: 系列の圧縮不可能性 (中央値二値化, 正規化)\n",
    "- **Spectral Slope**: broadband PSDのlog-log線形勾配 (簡易版aperiodic slope, 1–40Hz)\n",
    "  ※ FOOOF/specparamのような周期性成分(スピンドル・デルタ振動)の除去は行わない。\n",
    "    30秒単一エポックでのピーク検出はspecparamでは不安定なため、本解析ではnaive\n",
    "    broadband slopeを採用する。この簡略化はLimitationsに明記する。\n",
    "\n",
    "### 設計 (主解析と統一)\n",
    "- 同一被験者・同一夜・同一30秒エポック・同一チャンネル (EEG Fpz-Cz)\n",
    "- 同一アーティファクト基準 (±500 µV)\n",
    "- 被験者×条件×ステージ平均でWithin-subject Wilcoxon検定 (対応あり, 二側)\n",
    "- 多重比較補正: 本補助解析単体 (4指標×5ステージ=20比較) と、主解析(15比較)と\n",
    "  合算した場合 (35比較) の両方のBonferroni閾値を報告する\n",
    "\n",
    "### 検証ロジック (冗長性 vs 直交性)\n",
    "被験者内ΔCHI (Temazepam − Placebo) と各指標のΔとの Spearman相関\n",
    "(被験者間, N2 / N3 / N2+N3プール) を算出する:\n",
    "- 強い相関 (|rho| ≥ 0.5) かつ有意 → CHIは当該指標とほぼ冗長\n",
    "- 弱い相関 (|rho| < 0.3) または非有意 → CHIは直交的な情報を持つ (増分的価値)\n",
    "- 他指標がいずれのステージでも非有意 → CHIの選択的感度を支持する追加根拠\n",
    "\n",
    "### 計算コストに関する注記\n",
    "SampEnはO(N²)のアルゴリズムであるため、3000サンプル/エポック(100Hz×30秒)の\n",
    "まま全44夜・全有効エポックに適用すると数時間規模になりうる。本解析では\n",
    "SampEnの計算のみ100Hz→25Hzにダウンサンプリング(decimate factor=4)してから\n",
    "行う。全被験者・全条件(Placebo/Temazepam)に同一に適用するため、\n",
    "Within-subject比較の妥当性は保たれるが、絶対値そのものの解釈には注意を要する\n",
    "(Limitations追記事項として記載する)。PermEn・LZC・SpecSlopeはO(N)または\n",
    "Welch法ベースで計算コストが低いため、フル解像度(100Hz)のまま計算する。\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "nlcompare_step1_setup"
   },
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 1: 環境セットアップ (非線形指標比較)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "!pip install antropy -q\n",
    "\n",
    "import antropy as ant\n",
    "from scipy.signal import welch, decimate\n",
    "from scipy.stats import linregress, spearmanr, wilcoxon, norm\n",
    "\n",
    "NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR = os.path.join(DRIVE_ROOT, 'ECSoC_NLCompare_results')\n",
    "os.makedirs(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR: {NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR}')\n",
    "try:\n",
    "    print(f'antropy version: {ant.__version__}')\n",
    "except Exception:\n",
    "    pass\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "nlcompare_step2_core_functions"
   },
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 2: 非線形指標コア計算関数\n",
    "# process_one_night() と同一のエポック分割・ステージ割当・\n",
    "# アーティファクト基準 (±500 µV, 主チャンネル=Fpz-Cz) を用いる。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "SAMPEN_M               = 2      # embedding dimension (Richman & Moorman, 2000)\n",
    "SAMPEN_DECIMATE_FACTOR  = 4      # 100Hz → 25Hz (SampEnのみ; 計算コスト削減目的)\n",
    "PERMEN_ORDER            = 3\n",
    "PERMEN_DELAY            = 1\n",
    "LZC_BINARIZE_METHOD     = 'median'   # エポック内中央値で二値化\n",
    "SPEC_SLOPE_F_LO         = 1.0    # naive broadband slope フィット範囲 (Hz)\n",
    "SPEC_SLOPE_F_HI         = 40.0\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_sampen(x, order=SAMPEN_M, decimate_factor=SAMPEN_DECIMATE_FACTOR):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    Sample Entropy (Richman & Moorman, 2000)。\n",
    "    antropyの実装 (r = 0.2×SD 固定, Chebyshev距離) を使用。\n",
    "    計算コスト削減のため decimate_factor 倍にダウンサンプリングしてから計算する\n",
    "    (全条件・全被験者に同一適用のためWithin-subject比較としては妥当)。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    if np.std(x) == 0 or not np.isfinite(np.std(x)):\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        x_ds = decimate(x, decimate_factor, ftype='fir', zero_phase=True) \\\n",
    "               if decimate_factor > 1 else x\n",
    "        return float(ant.sample_entropy(x_ds, order=order))\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_permen(x, order=PERMEN_ORDER, delay=PERMEN_DELAY):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Permutation Entropy (Bandt & Pompe, 2002)。[0,1]に正規化。\"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        return float(ant.perm_entropy(x, order=order, delay=delay, normalize=True))\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_lzc(x, method=LZC_BINARIZE_METHOD):\n",
    "    \"\"\"Lempel-Ziv Complexity。エポック内中央値で二値化後、正規化LZCを計算。\"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        thr = np.median(x) if method == 'median' else np.mean(x)\n",
    "        binary_seq = ''.join((x > thr).astype(np.int8).astype(str))\n",
    "        return float(ant.lziv_complexity(binary_seq, normalize=True))\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def compute_spectral_slope(x, fs, f_lo=SPEC_SLOPE_F_LO, f_hi=SPEC_SLOPE_F_HI):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    Broadband log-log PSD勾配 (簡易版aperiodic slope)。\n",
    "    注意: FOOOF/specparamのような周期性成分(スピンドル・デルタ振動)の除去は\n",
    "    行わない、生スペクトルへの単純線形フィットである (Limitations参照)。\n",
    "    Welchパラメータは既存のデルタパワー解析 (ext_step7) と統一。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        freqs, psd = welch(x, fs=fs, nperseg=min(256, len(x)))\n",
    "        mask = (freqs >= f_lo) & (freqs <= f_hi) & (psd > 0)\n",
    "        if mask.sum() < 5:\n",
    "            return np.nan\n",
    "        log_f = np.log10(freqs[mask])\n",
    "        log_p = np.log10(psd[mask])\n",
    "        slope, _, _, _, _ = linregress(log_f, log_p)\n",
    "        return float(slope)\n",
    "    except Exception:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def process_one_night_nonlinear(psg_path, hyp_path, subject_nr, condition):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    1夜分のPSGについて SampEn / PermEn / LZC / SpecSlope をエポック毎に計算する。\n",
    "    既存の all_epochs_raw.csv (CHI等) とは subject_nr, condition, epoch_idx\n",
    "    をキーに後段でマージする。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    try:\n",
    "        raw = mne.io.read_raw_edf(\n",
    "            psg_path, include=[PRIMARY_CH], preload=True, verbose=False)\n",
    "        sig = raw.get_data(picks=[PRIMARY_CH])[0] * 1e6\n",
    "        actual_fs = int(raw.info['sfreq'])\n",
    "    except Exception as e:\n",
    "        print(f'  ⚠️ [{subject_nr} {condition}]: {e}')\n",
    "        return None\n",
    "\n",
    "    stage_epochs = read_hypnogram(hyp_path) if hyp_path else []\n",
    "    win_samp = int(WIN_SEC * actual_fs)\n",
    "    n_ep = len(sig) // win_samp\n",
    "\n",
    "    results = []\n",
    "    for ep in range(n_ep):\n",
    "        t0 = ep * WIN_SEC\n",
    "        i0 = ep * win_samp\n",
    "        i1 = i0 + win_samp\n",
    "        stage = get_stage_at(stage_epochs, t0)\n",
    "        x = sig[i0:i1].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "        if np.abs(x).max() > 500:\n",
    "            stage = 'ART'\n",
    "\n",
    "        if stage in VALID_STAGES:\n",
    "            sampen = compute_sampen(x)\n",
    "            permen = compute_permen(x)\n",
    "            lzc    = compute_lzc(x)\n",
    "            slope  = compute_spectral_slope(x, actual_fs)\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            sampen = permen = lzc = slope = np.nan\n",
    "\n",
    "        results.append({\n",
    "            'subject_nr': subject_nr,\n",
    "            'condition':  condition,\n",
    "            'epoch_idx':  ep,\n",
    "            't_start':    t0,\n",
    "            'stage':      stage,\n",
    "            'actual_fs':  actual_fs,\n",
    "            'SampEn':     sampen,\n",
    "            'PermEn':     permen,\n",
    "            'LZC':        lzc,\n",
    "            'SpecSlope':  slope,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "\n",
    "    del raw\n",
    "    return pd.DataFrame(results)\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "print('非線形指標コア関数 定義完了')\n",
    "print(f'  SampEn   : order={SAMPEN_M}, r=0.2×SD (antropy既定), '\n",
    "      f'decimate factor={SAMPEN_DECIMATE_FACTOR} (100Hz→{FS//SAMPEN_DECIMATE_FACTOR}Hz)')\n",
    "print(f'  PermEn   : order={PERMEN_ORDER}, delay={PERMEN_DELAY}, normalized')\n",
    "print(f'  LZC      : binarize={LZC_BINARIZE_METHOD}, normalized')\n",
    "print(f'  SpecSlope: fit range {SPEC_SLOPE_F_LO}-{SPEC_SLOPE_F_HI} Hz '\n",
    "      f'(naive broadband, 周期性成分の除去なし)')\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
  },

   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 3: 全22被験者 × 2夜 フルラン (非線形指標)\n",
    "# 途中でCSV保存するので中断しても再開可能 (既存パイプラインの方式を踏襲)\n",
    "# 予想処理時間の目安: SampEnのdecimate適用後で 1夜 ≈ 1-2分 × 44夜 ≈ 40-90分\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "nlcompare_epochs_path = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'all_epochs_nonlinear.csv')\n",
    "\n",
    "if os.path.exists(nlcompare_epochs_path):\n",
    "    df_nl = pd.read_csv(nlcompare_epochs_path)\n",
    "    done_keys_nl = set(zip(df_nl['subject_nr'], df_nl['condition']))\n",
    "    print(f'既存CSV読み込み: {len(df_nl)} エポック, 処理済み: {len(done_keys_nl)} 夜')\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    df_nl = pd.DataFrame()\n",
    "    done_keys_nl = set()\n",
    "    print('新規処理開始')\n",
    "\n",
    "results_list_nl = [df_nl] if len(df_nl) > 0 else []\n",
    "errors_nl = []\n",
    "\n",
    "for i, p in enumerate(pairs):\n",
    "    nr = p['subject_nr']\n",
    "\n",
    "    for cond, psg_key, hyp_key in [\n",
    "        ('Placebo',   'placebo_psg', 'placebo_hyp'),\n",
    "        ('Temazepam', 'temaz_psg',   'temaz_hyp'),\n",
    "    ]:\n",
    "        key = (nr, cond)\n",
    "        if key in done_keys_nl:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "\n",
    "        psg = p[psg_key]\n",
    "        hyp = p[hyp_key]\n",
    "\n",
    "        if psg is None:\n",
    "            errors_nl.append(f'Nr={nr:02d} {cond}: PSGファイルなし')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "\n",
    "        print(f'[{i+1:02d}/{len(pairs)}] Nr={nr:02d} {cond} (非線形指標) → {os.path.basename(psg)}')\n",
    "\n",
    "        df_night_nl = process_one_night_nonlinear(psg, hyp, nr, cond)\n",
    "\n",
    "        if df_night_nl is not None:\n",
    "            results_list_nl.append(df_night_nl)\n",
    "            done_keys_nl.add(key)\n",
    "\n",
    "            if len(done_keys_nl) % 5 == 0:\n",
    "                pd.concat(results_list_nl, ignore_index=True).to_csv(\n",
    "                    nlcompare_epochs_path, index=False)\n",
    "                print(f'  → 中間保存: {len(done_keys_nl)} 夜完了')\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            errors_nl.append(f'Nr={nr:02d} {cond}: 処理失敗')\n",
    "\n",
    "df_nl = pd.concat(results_list_nl, ignore_index=True)\n",
    "df_nl.to_csv(nlcompare_epochs_path, index=False)\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('=== 非線形指標 全処理完了 ===')\n",
    "print(f'総エポック数: {len(df_nl):,}')\n",
    "print(f'被験者数: {df_nl[\"subject_nr\"].nunique()}')\n",
    "print('条件別エポック数:')\n",
    "print(df_nl.groupby('condition')['epoch_idx'].count())\n",
    "if errors_nl:\n",
    "    print(f'エラー ({len(errors_nl)}件):')\n",
    "    for e in errors_nl:\n",
    "        print(f'  {e}')\n"

   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "nlcompare_step4_per_subject_stage_mean"
   },
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 4: 被験者 × 条件 × ステージ 平均を計算し、\n",
    "# 既存のCHIワイドテーブル (wide) と統合する\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "valid_nl = df_nl[df_nl['stage'].isin(VALID_STAGES)].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'有効エポック数 (非線形指標): {len(valid_nl):,}')\n",
    "print('条件別:')\n",
    "print(valid_nl.groupby('condition')['SampEn'].count())\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "subj_means_nl = valid_nl.groupby(\n",
    "    ['subject_nr', 'condition', 'stage']\n",
    ").agg(\n",
    "    n_epochs_nl     = ('SampEn', 'count'),\n",
    "    SampEn_mean     = ('SampEn', 'mean'),\n",
    "    PermEn_mean     = ('PermEn', 'mean'),\n",
    "    LZC_mean        = ('LZC', 'mean'),\n",
    "    SpecSlope_mean  = ('SpecSlope', 'mean'),\n",
    ").reset_index()\n",
    "\n",
    "subj_P_nl = subj_means_nl[subj_means_nl['condition'] == 'Placebo'].copy()\n",
    "subj_T_nl = subj_means_nl[subj_means_nl['condition'] == 'Temazepam'].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "wide_nl = pd.merge(\n",
    "    subj_P_nl.rename(columns=lambda c: c+'_P' if c not in ['subject_nr','stage'] else c),\n",
    "    subj_T_nl.rename(columns=lambda c: c+'_T' if c not in ['subject_nr','stage'] else c),\n",
    "    on=['subject_nr', 'stage'],\n",
    "    how='inner'\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric in ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC', 'SpecSlope']:\n",
    "    wide_nl[f'Δ{metric}'] = wide_nl[f'{metric}_mean_T'] - wide_nl[f'{metric}_mean_P']\n",
    "\n",
    "# 既存のCHIワイドテーブル (wide, Step8で生成) と統合\n",
    "wide_combined = pd.merge(\n",
    "    wide[['subject_nr', 'stage', 'CHI_mean_P', 'CHI_mean_T', 'ΔCHI']],\n",
    "    wide_nl,\n",
    "    on=['subject_nr', 'stage'],\n",
    "    how='inner'\n",
    ")\n",
    "\n",
    "csv_path_nl = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'nonlinear_within_subject_wide.csv')\n",
    "wide_combined.to_csv(csv_path_nl, index=False)\n",
    "\n",
    "print(f'非線形指標 within-subjectワイドテーブル: {csv_path_nl}')\n",
    "print(f'行数: {len(wide_combined)} (被験者×ステージ組み合わせ)')\n",
    "print()\n",
    "for metric in ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC', 'SpecSlope']:\n",
    "    print(f'Δ{metric} (Temazepam − Placebo) ステージ別平均:')\n",
    "    print(wide_combined.groupby('stage')[f'Δ{metric}'].agg(['mean','std','count']).round(4))\n",
    "    print()\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "nlcompare_step5_wilcoxon"
   },
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 5: Within-subject Wilcoxon検定 (非線形指標)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "def rank_biserial_r(W_stat, n):\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    Matched-pairs rank-biserial correlation (Kerby, 2014 simple-difference formula).\n",
    "    W_stat: scipy.stats.wilcoxon が返す統計量 (= min(W+, W-)、タイなし前提)。\n",
    "    z/sqrt(n) 近似と異なり、完全分離 (p が理論的下限に達する場合) でも\n",
    "    必ず [0, 1] に収まる。符号は delta_mean 側で別途表現する。\n",
    "    \"\"\"\n",
    "    S = n * (n + 1) / 2\n",
    "    return 1 - 2 * W_stat / S\n",
    "\n",
    "NL_METRICS = {\n",
    "    'SampEn':    ('SampEn_mean_P',    'SampEn_mean_T',    'ΔSampEn'),\n",
    "    'PermEn':    ('PermEn_mean_P',    'PermEn_mean_T',    'ΔPermEn'),\n",
    "    'LZC':       ('LZC_mean_P',       'LZC_mean_T',       'ΔLZC'),\n",
    "    'SpecSlope': ('SpecSlope_mean_P', 'SpecSlope_mean_T', 'ΔSpecSlope'),\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "results_stat_nl = []\n",
    "\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "print('非線形指標 Within-subject Wilcoxon検定: Temazepam vs Placebo')\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric, (col_p, col_t, col_d) in NL_METRICS.items():\n",
    "    print(f'\\n--- {metric} ---')\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "        sub = wide_combined[wide_combined['stage'] == stage][[col_p, col_t, col_d]].dropna()\n",
    "        n = len(sub)\n",
    "        if n < 5:\n",
    "            print(f'  {stage}: n={n} (不足)')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "\n",
    "        delta_mean = sub[col_d].mean()\n",
    "        delta_sd   = sub[col_d].std()\n",
    "\n",
    "        try:\n",
    "            stat, p = wilcoxon(sub[col_t], sub[col_p], alternative='two-sided')\n",
    "        except Exception as e:\n",
    "            print(f'  {stage}: Wilcoxon失敗 ({e})')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "\n",
    "        r = rank_biserial_r(stat, n)\n",
    "        sig = '***' if p < 0.001 else '**' if p < 0.01 else '*' if p < 0.05 else 'ns'\n",
    "        print(f'  {stage}: n={n:2d}  Δ={delta_mean:+.4f}±{delta_sd:.4f}  '\n",
    "              f'W={stat:.0f}  p={p:.4f} {sig}  r={r:.3f}')\n",
    "\n",
    "        results_stat_nl.append({\n",
    "            'metric':     metric,\n",
    "            'stage':      stage,\n",
    "            'n':          n,\n",
    "            'delta_mean': delta_mean,\n",
    "            'delta_sd':   delta_sd,\n",
    "            'W_stat':     stat,\n",
    "            'p_value':    p,\n",
    "            'effect_r':   r,\n",
    "            'sig':        sig,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "\n",
    "df_stat_nl = pd.DataFrame(results_stat_nl)\n",
    "stat_path_nl = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'wilcoxon_results_nonlinear.csv')\n",
    "df_stat_nl.to_csv(stat_path_nl, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n統計結果保存: {stat_path_nl}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 多重比較補正の再計算 ---\n",
    "# 主論文 (Table 1): CHI, D_eff_rel, PhaseV × 5ステージ = 15比較 (α=0.05/15≈0.0033)\n",
    "# 本補助解析: 追加4指標 × 5ステージ = 20比較\n",
    "n_primary_comparisons = 15\n",
    "n_new_comparisons     = len(NL_METRICS) * len(STAGE_ORDER)\n",
    "n_total_comparisons   = n_primary_comparisons + n_new_comparisons\n",
    "\n",
    "alpha_new_only      = 0.05 / n_new_comparisons\n",
    "alpha_all_combined  = 0.05 / n_total_comparisons\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print(f'補助解析単体のBonferroni閾値   (α=0.05/{n_new_comparisons}): {alpha_new_only:.5f}')\n",
    "print(f'主解析と合算した場合の閾値     (α=0.05/{n_total_comparisons}): {alpha_all_combined:.5f}')\n",
    "\n",
    "n_sig_new_only = (df_stat_nl['p_value'] < alpha_new_only).sum()\n",
    "n_sig_combined = (df_stat_nl['p_value'] < alpha_all_combined).sum()\n",
    "print(f'補助解析単体の基準で有意: {n_sig_new_only}/{len(df_stat_nl)}')\n",
    "print(f'合算基準で有意        : {n_sig_combined}/{len(df_stat_nl)}')\n",
    "\n",
    "if n_sig_new_only > 0:\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "    print('有意だった比較:')\n",
    "    print(df_stat_nl[df_stat_nl['p_value'] < alpha_new_only]\n",
    "          [['metric','stage','delta_mean','p_value','effect_r']].to_string(index=False))\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
