  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {
    "id": "nlcompare_step6_chi_correlation"
   },
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6: ΔCHI と Δ(他の非線形指標) の被験者間相関\n",
    "# 冗長性 (redundant) か 直交性 (orthogonal / incremental) かを判定する\n",
    "# 既存のSWA-CHI相関解析 (ext_step7) と同じブートストラップ方式を用いる\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "def bootstrap_spearman_ci(x, y, n_boot=10000, seed=42):\n",
    "    rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)\n",
    "    x = np.asarray(x)\n",
    "    y = np.asarray(y)\n",
    "    n = len(x)\n",
    "    boot_rhos = np.empty(n_boot)\n",
    "    idx_all = np.arange(n)\n",
    "    for b in range(n_boot):\n",
    "        idx = rng.choice(idx_all, size=n, replace=True)\n",
    "        rho, _ = spearmanr(x[idx], y[idx])\n",
    "        boot_rhos[b] = rho\n",
    "    lo, hi = np.percentile(boot_rhos, [2.5, 97.5])\n",
    "    return lo, hi\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "corr_records = []\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "print('ΔCHI vs Δ(非線形指標) 被験者間相関 (Spearman)')\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric in ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC', 'SpecSlope']:\n",
    "    dcol = f'Δ{metric}'\n",
    "    for stage_group_name, stages in [('N2', ['N2']), ('N3', ['N3']), ('N2+N3', ['N2', 'N3'])]:\n",
    "        sub = wide_combined[wide_combined['stage'].isin(stages)]\n",
    "        agg = sub.groupby('subject_nr')[['ΔCHI', dcol]].mean().dropna()\n",
    "        if len(agg) < 5:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        rho, pval = spearmanr(agg['ΔCHI'], agg[dcol])\n",
    "        ci_lo, ci_hi = bootstrap_spearman_ci(agg['ΔCHI'].values, agg[dcol].values)\n",
    "\n",
    "        corr_records.append({\n",
    "            'metric': metric, 'stage_group': stage_group_name, 'n': len(agg),\n",
    "            'rho': rho, 'p_value': pval, 'ci_lo': ci_lo, 'ci_hi': ci_hi,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "        print(f'ΔCHI vs Δ{metric:<10} [{stage_group_name:<5}]: '\n",
    "              f'rho={rho:+.3f} (95%CI [{ci_lo:+.3f}, {ci_hi:+.3f}]), '\n",
    "              f'p={pval:.4f}, n={len(agg)}')\n",
    "\n",
    "df_corr_nl = pd.DataFrame(corr_records)\n",
    "corr_path_nl = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'chi_vs_nonlinear_correlation.csv')\n",
    "df_corr_nl.to_csv(corr_path_nl, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n相関結果保存: {corr_path_nl}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('解釈の目安:')\n",
    "print('  |rho| >= 0.5 かつ有意   → CHIとほぼ冗長 (同一の変化を捉えている可能性)')\n",
    "print('  |rho| <  0.3 または非有意 → CHIは他指標から独立した情報を持つ (直交性の根拠)')\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6b: SpecSlope 陰性対照チェック (W / N1 / REM)\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 目的:\n",
    "#   ΔCHI–ΔSpecSlope 相関 (N2/N3 で |rho| ~ 0.6, Bonferroni後も生存) が\n",
    "#   ①テマゼパムのN2/N3特異的な薬理効果を反映しているのか、\n",
    "#   ②夜ごとのアンプゲイン・電極インピーダンス等の技術的差異による\n",
    "#     一般的な共変動 (gain confound) に過ぎないのかを判別する。\n",
    "#   CHI自体がテマゼパムで有意に変化しないW・N1・REM (Table 1: すべてns) は、\n",
    "#   ①なら相関が消えるはずの陰性対照ステージとなる。\n",
    "#   ロジックはSWA解析での gain-invariant relative power再検証\n",
    "#   (外部検証 Step 7g) と同一。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "negctrl_records = []\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('陰性対照: ΔCHI vs ΔSpecSlope 相関 (W / N1 / REM)')\n",
    "print('(これらのステージではCHI自体がテマゼパムで有意に変化しない — Table 1参照)')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "dcol = 'ΔSpecSlope'\n",
    "for stage in ['W', 'N1', 'REM']:\n",
    "    sub = wide_combined[wide_combined['stage'] == stage]\n",
    "    agg = sub.groupby('subject_nr')[['ΔCHI', dcol]].mean().dropna()\n",
    "    n = len(agg)\n",
    "    if n < 5:\n",
    "        print(f'  {stage}: n不足 (n={n})')\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    rho, pval = spearmanr(agg['ΔCHI'], agg[dcol])\n",
    "    ci_lo, ci_hi = bootstrap_spearman_ci(agg['ΔCHI'].values, agg[dcol].values)\n",
    "\n",
    "    negctrl_records.append({\n",
    "        'metric': 'SpecSlope', 'stage_group': stage, 'n': n,\n",
    "        'rho': rho, 'p_value': pval, 'ci_lo': ci_lo, 'ci_hi': ci_hi,\n",
    "    })\n",
    "    print(f'ΔCHI vs ΔSpecSlope  [{stage:<5}]: '\n",
    "          f'rho={rho:+.3f} (95%CI [{ci_lo:+.3f}, {ci_hi:+.3f}]), '\n",
    "          f'p={pval:.4f}, n={n}')\n",
    "\n",
    "df_negctrl_specslope = pd.DataFrame(negctrl_records)\n",
    "negctrl_path = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'chi_vs_specslope_negctrl_W_N1_REM.csv')\n",
    "df_negctrl_specslope.to_csv(negctrl_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n陰性対照結果保存: {negctrl_path}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- N2/N3 (主要所見) との並列比較 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('N2 / N3 (主要所見, Step 6で算出済み) との比較:')\n",
    "main_rows = df_corr_nl[\n",
    "    (df_corr_nl['metric'] == 'SpecSlope') & (df_corr_nl['stage_group'].isin(['N2', 'N3']))\n",
    "]\n",
    "for _, row in main_rows.iterrows():\n",
    "    print(f\"  {row['stage_group']:<5}: rho={row['rho']:+.3f} (p={row['p_value']:.4f}, n={row['n']:.0f})\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 解釈補助 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('解釈の目安:')\n",
    "print('  W/N1/REMでも |rho| >= 0.4 かつ有意   → 技術的差異(gain confound)由来の疑いが強い')\n",
    "print('  W/N1/REMで |rho| < 0.3 または非有意  → N2/N3限定の関連はgain confoundと独立に主張しやすい')\n",
    "\n",
    "if len(df_negctrl_specslope) > 0 and len(main_rows) > 0:\n",
    "    mean_abs_rho_negctrl = df_negctrl_specslope['rho'].abs().mean()\n",
    "    mean_abs_rho_main = main_rows['rho'].abs().mean()\n",
    "    n_negctrl_sig = (df_negctrl_specslope['p_value'] < 0.05).sum()\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "    print(f'  W/N1/REM |rho| 平均 = {mean_abs_rho_negctrl:.3f} '\n",
    "          f'(有意 {n_negctrl_sig}/{len(df_negctrl_specslope)} ステージ)')\n",
    "    print(f'  N2/N3    |rho| 平均 = {mean_abs_rho_main:.3f}')\n",
    "    if mean_abs_rho_negctrl >= 0.4 and n_negctrl_sig >= 2:\n",
    "        print('  -> 陰性対照ステージでも同程度の相関が見られ、gain confoundの疑いを排除できない。')\n",
    "        print('     Discussion/Limitationsで明記が必要。')\n",
    "    elif mean_abs_rho_negctrl < 0.3:\n",
    "        print('  -> 陰性対照ステージでは相関が明確に弱く、N2/N3限定の関連はgain confoundとは')\n",
    "        print('     独立した所見として主張しやすい。')\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print('  -> 中間的な結果。個別ステージのp値・CIを見て判断すること(自動判定は非推奨)。')\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
  },

   "cell_type": "code",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6c: ゲイン交絡の直接検証\n",
    "# SD比 (std_ratio_P_over_T; 外部検証 Step 7e で算出済み) と\n",
    "# ΔCHI・ΔSpecSlope の相関を全ステージで直接検定する。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 背景:\n",
    "#   Step 6bで、CHI自体が不変なW/N1/REMでもΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関が\n",
    "#   消えず、むしろN1で最強 (rho=-0.731) だった。これは両者が\n",
    "#   共通の第三変数 (被験者ごとの夜間記録振幅・アンプゲイン差) に\n",
    "#   よって駆動されている可能性を示唆する。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 方法:\n",
    "#   外部検証 Step 7e で算出済みの被験者ごとのSD比\n",
    "#   (std_ratio_P_over_T = Placebo夜SD / Temazepam夜SD, 全被験者で\n",
    "#   0.2~15倍のレンジ) を「ゲイン交絡の代理変数」として、\n",
    "#   ΔCHI・ΔSpecSlopeそれぞれとの被験者間Spearman相関を\n",
    "#   全5ステージで計算する (Step 6/6bと同じブートストラップCI方式)。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 判定:\n",
    "#   SD比がΔSpecSlopeとは強く相関するがΔCHIとは相関しない\n",
    "#     → ΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関はSpecSlope側のゲイン感受性に由来し、\n",
    "#       CHI自体はゲイン交絡から独立している可能性を支持\n",
    "#   SD比がΔCHIとも有意に相関する\n",
    "#     → CHIもゲイン交絡から自由でない可能性 → Limitationsに明記必須\n",
    "#   SD比がどちらとも相関しない\n",
    "#     → Step 6bの相関は単純な線形ゲイン交絡だけでは説明できない\n",
    "#       (別の共通要因の可能性を検討)\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "if 'df_amp' not in dir():\n",
    "    raise RuntimeError(\n",
    "        \"df_amp が未定義です。外部検証 Step 7e (信号振幅チェック) のセルを先に実行してください。\"\n",
    "    )\n",
    "\n",
    "gain_proxy = df_amp[['subject_nr', 'std_ratio_P_over_T']].copy()\n",
    "\n",
    "gain_corr_records = []\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('ゲイン交絡の直接検証: SD比(Placebo/Temazepam) vs ΔCHI / ΔSpecSlope')\n",
    "print('(全5ステージ)')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "for target_metric, dcol in [('CHI', 'ΔCHI'), ('SpecSlope', 'ΔSpecSlope')]:\n",
    "    print(f'\\n--- SD比(P/T) vs Δ{target_metric} ---')\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "        sub = wide_combined[wide_combined['stage'] == stage][['subject_nr', dcol]]\n",
    "        merged = sub.merge(gain_proxy, on='subject_nr', how='inner').dropna()\n",
    "        n = len(merged)\n",
    "        if n < 5:\n",
    "            print(f'  {stage}: n不足 (n={n})')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        rho, pval = spearmanr(merged['std_ratio_P_over_T'], merged[dcol])\n",
    "        ci_lo, ci_hi = bootstrap_spearman_ci(\n",
    "            merged['std_ratio_P_over_T'].values, merged[dcol].values\n",
    "        )\n",
    "        gain_corr_records.append({\n",
    "            'target_metric': target_metric, 'stage': stage, 'n': n,\n",
    "            'rho': rho, 'p_value': pval, 'ci_lo': ci_lo, 'ci_hi': ci_hi,\n",
    "        })\n",
    "        print(f'  {stage:<5}: rho={rho:+.3f} '\n",
    "              f'(95%CI [{ci_lo:+.3f}, {ci_hi:+.3f}]), p={pval:.4f}, n={n}')\n",
    "\n",
    "df_gain_corr = pd.DataFrame(gain_corr_records)\n",
    "gain_corr_path = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'gain_proxy_vs_chi_specslope_correlation.csv')\n",
    "df_gain_corr.to_csv(gain_corr_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n結果保存: {gain_corr_path}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 解釈補助 ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('解釈: 共通ゲイン交絡仮説の直接検証')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "n_total_tests = len(df_gain_corr)\n",
    "if n_total_tests > 0:\n",
    "    alpha_bonf = 0.05 / n_total_tests\n",
    "    n_sig_nominal = int((df_gain_corr['p_value'] < 0.05).sum())\n",
    "    n_sig_bonf = int((df_gain_corr['p_value'] < alpha_bonf).sum())\n",
    "    print(f'nominal p<0.05: {n_sig_nominal}/{n_total_tests}   '\n",
    "          f'Bonferroni (α=0.05/{n_total_tests}={alpha_bonf:.4f}) 生存: {n_sig_bonf}/{n_total_tests}')\n",
    "\n",
    "    chi_rows = df_gain_corr[df_gain_corr['target_metric'] == 'CHI']\n",
    "    specslope_rows = df_gain_corr[df_gain_corr['target_metric'] == 'SpecSlope']\n",
    "    chi_sig_stages = chi_rows[chi_rows['p_value'] < 0.05]['stage'].tolist()\n",
    "    specslope_sig_stages = specslope_rows[specslope_rows['p_value'] < 0.05]['stage'].tolist()\n",
    "\n",
    "    print(f'\\nSD比と有意 (nominal p<0.05) に相関したステージ:')\n",
    "    print(f'  ΔCHI:       {chi_sig_stages if chi_sig_stages else \"なし\"}')\n",
    "    print(f'  ΔSpecSlope: {specslope_sig_stages if specslope_sig_stages else \"なし\"}')\n",
    "\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "    if len(specslope_sig_stages) >= 3 and len(chi_sig_stages) == 0:\n",
    "        print('  -> SpecSlopeは複数ステージでSD比と直接相関する一方、CHIはSD比と相関しない。')\n",
    "        print('     Step 6bの「共通ゲイン交絡」懸念に対する反証材料:')\n",
    "        print('     ΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関はSpecSlope側のゲイン感受性に由来する可能性が高く、')\n",
    "        print('     CHI自体はゲイン交絡から独立している可能性を支持する。')\n",
    "    elif len(chi_sig_stages) >= 3:\n",
    "        print('  -> ΔCHI自体がSD比と有意に相関するステージが複数あり、')\n",
    "        print('     CHIもゲイン交絡から自由でない可能性がある。Limitationsでの明記が必須。')\n",
    "    elif len(specslope_sig_stages) == 0 and len(chi_sig_stages) == 0:\n",
    "        print('  -> SD比はΔCHI・ΔSpecSlopeいずれとも直接相関しない。')\n",
    "        print('     Step 6bで見られたΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関は、単純な線形ゲイン交絡だけでは')\n",
    "        print('     説明できない可能性が高く、別の共通要因 (例: 睡眠の深さの被験者間差) を要検討。')\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        print('  -> 部分的な関与が示唆される。ステージ別・指標別のパターンを個別に確認すること。')\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print('  有効な検定がありませんでした (n不足)。')\n"
   ],
   "execution_count": null,
   "outputs": []
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "aux_step6d_jackknife_n1"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6d: N1 jackknife (leave-one-out) — ΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関の頑健性検定\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 背景:\n",
    "#   Step 6bでN1のΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関が全ステージ中最も強く出た\n",
    "#   (rho=-0.731, p=0.0001)。CHI自体はN1でテマゼパムに反応しない (Table 1: ns)\n",
    "#   にもかかわらずこれほど強い相関が出ている点が疑わしい。\n",
    "#   Step 6cでSD比 (粗い一晩通しゲイン代理変数) による説明は否定されたが、\n",
    "#   それが「少数の外れ値被験者による駆動」なのか「集団全体で頑健な関係」\n",
    "#   なのかは未検証のまま。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 方法:\n",
    "#   N1のΔCHI・ΔSpecSlopeペア (n=22) から1被験者ずつ除いてSpearman rhoを\n",
    "#   再計算する (leave-one-out)。rhoの分布のばらつきが小さければ頑健、\n",
    "#   1〜2名の除外で符号反転/大きく減衰するなら外れ値駆動と判断する。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "stage_jk = 'N1'\n",
    "sub_jk = wide_combined[wide_combined['stage'] == stage_jk][\n",
    "    ['subject_nr', 'ΔCHI', 'ΔSpecSlope']\n",
    "].dropna()\n",
    "n_jk = len(sub_jk)\n",
    "\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print(f'{stage_jk}: ΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関 jackknife (leave-one-out, n={n_jk})')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "x_full = sub_jk['ΔCHI'].values\n",
    "y_full = sub_jk['ΔSpecSlope'].values\n",
    "subj_ids_jk = sub_jk['subject_nr'].values\n",
    "\n",
    "rho_full, p_full = spearmanr(x_full, y_full)\n",
    "print(f'フルサンプル: rho={rho_full:+.3f}, p={p_full:.4f}, n={n_jk}')\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "jk_records = []\n",
    "for i in range(n_jk):\n",
    "    mask = np.arange(n_jk) != i\n",
    "    rho_i, p_i = spearmanr(x_full[mask], y_full[mask])\n",
    "    jk_records.append({\n",
    "        'excluded_subject_nr': subj_ids_jk[i],\n",
    "        'rho_loo': rho_i,\n",
    "        'p_loo': p_i,\n",
    "        'delta_rho_from_full': rho_i - rho_full,\n",
    "    })\n",
    "\n",
    "df_jk = pd.DataFrame(jk_records).sort_values('rho_loo')\n",
    "jk_path = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, f'jackknife_chi_specslope_{stage_jk}.csv')\n",
    "df_jk.to_csv(jk_path, index=False)\n",
    "\n",
    "print('Leave-one-out rho の分布:')\n",
    "print(f'  range: [{df_jk[\"rho_loo\"].min():+.3f}, {df_jk[\"rho_loo\"].max():+.3f}]')\n",
    "print(f'  SD across LOO estimates: {df_jk[\"rho_loo\"].std():.4f}')\n",
    "print(f'  全て同符号か (元のrho_full={rho_full:+.3f} と同符号)?: '\n",
    "      f'{bool((np.sign(df_jk[\"rho_loo\"]) == np.sign(rho_full)).all())}')\n",
    "print(f'  全て有意 (p<0.05) か?: {bool((df_jk[\"p_loo\"] < 0.05).all())}')\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('フルサンプルから最も乖離させる被験者 (上位5件):')\n",
    "top5 = df_jk.reindex(\n",
    "    df_jk['delta_rho_from_full'].abs().sort_values(ascending=False).index\n",
    ").head(5)\n",
    "print(top5.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "print(f'\\n結果保存: {jk_path}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('解釈の目安:')\n",
    "print('  LOO rhoが全て同符号・|delta_rho|が小さい (目安<0.15)  → 少数外れ値駆動ではなく頑健')\n",
    "print('  1〜2名の除外で符号反転/大きく減衰                    → 外れ値駆動、解釈に注意')\n",
    "\n",
    "if bool((np.sign(df_jk[\"rho_loo\"]) == np.sign(rho_full)).all()) and df_jk['delta_rho_from_full'].abs().max() < 0.15:\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "    print('  -> 頑健。少数の外れ値被験者による駆動ではないと判断できる。')\n",
    "    print('     Step 6eのtrait反応性検定で、この頑健な相関の由来をさらに切り分ける。')\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "aux_step6e_trait_responsiveness"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6e: 被験者反応性 (trait responsiveness) 判別検定\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 目的:\n",
    "#   Step 6bで見られた「薬効のないN1でのΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関」が、\n",
    "#   「テマゼパムに全般的に強く反応する体質の被験者は、真の薬効がない\n",
    "#   ステージでも指標が大きく動く」というtrait交絡で説明できるかを検定する。\n",
    "#   Step 6cで一晩通しのSD比による説明は否定され、Step 6dで少数外れ値\n",
    "#   駆動でもないことが確認された前提での、残る主要な対立仮説の検証。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 論理:\n",
    "#   trait交絡が正しいなら、被験者ごとの反応性の大きさは薬効の有無に\n",
    "#   関わらずステージを横断して一貫するはずである。したがって\n",
    "#   |ΔCHI in N1| (薬効なし, Table 1: ns) は |ΔCHI in N2/N3| (真の薬効) と\n",
    "#   正相関するはずである。同様に |ΔSpecSlope in N1| も |ΔCHI in N2/N3| と\n",
    "#   正相関するはずである。\n",
    "#   いずれも無相関であれば、N1の相関はN1固有の測定要因\n",
    "#   (体動の少ない浅睡眠でのEOG/筋電混入など) を疑うべきである。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "def pivot_abs_delta(df, stages, col):\n",
    "    sub = df[df['stage'].isin(stages)][['subject_nr', col]].copy()\n",
    "    sub['abs_val'] = sub[col].abs()\n",
    "    return sub.groupby('subject_nr')['abs_val'].mean()\n",
    "\n",
    "abs_chi_n1       = pivot_abs_delta(wide_combined, ['N1'],       'ΔCHI')\n",
    "abs_specslope_n1 = pivot_abs_delta(wide_combined, ['N1'],       'ΔSpecSlope')\n",
    "abs_chi_n2n3     = pivot_abs_delta(wide_combined, ['N2', 'N3'], 'ΔCHI')\n",
    "\n",
    "trait_df = pd.concat(\n",
    "    {\n",
    "        'abs_ΔCHI_N1':       abs_chi_n1,\n",
    "        'abs_ΔSpecSlope_N1': abs_specslope_n1,\n",
    "        'abs_ΔCHI_N2N3':     abs_chi_n2n3,\n",
    "    },\n",
    "    axis=1\n",
    ").dropna()\n",
    "\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('trait反応性の判別検定: |Δ指標 in N1| vs |ΔCHI in N2/N3| (真の薬効)')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print(f'n = {len(trait_df)}')\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "trait_records = []\n",
    "for predictor in ['abs_ΔCHI_N1', 'abs_ΔSpecSlope_N1']:\n",
    "    rho, pval = spearmanr(trait_df[predictor], trait_df['abs_ΔCHI_N2N3'])\n",
    "    ci_lo, ci_hi = bootstrap_spearman_ci(\n",
    "        trait_df[predictor].values, trait_df['abs_ΔCHI_N2N3'].values\n",
    "    )\n",
    "    trait_records.append({\n",
    "        'predictor': predictor, 'target': 'abs_ΔCHI_N2N3', 'n': len(trait_df),\n",
    "        'rho': rho, 'p_value': pval, 'ci_lo': ci_lo, 'ci_hi': ci_hi,\n",
    "    })\n",
    "    print(f'{predictor:<20} vs |ΔCHI_N2N3|: rho={rho:+.3f} '\n",
    "          f'(95%CI [{ci_lo:+.3f}, {ci_hi:+.3f}]), p={pval:.4f}')\n",
    "\n",
    "df_trait = pd.DataFrame(trait_records)\n",
    "trait_path = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'trait_responsiveness_n1_vs_n2n3.csv')\n",
    "df_trait.to_csv(trait_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n結果保存: {trait_path}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('解釈の目安:')\n",
    "print('  有意な正相関  → trait交絡 (全般的反応性) を支持。N1の相関はN2/N3の真の')\n",
    "print('                  薬効と同じ「反応性」を反映している可能性がある。')\n",
    "print('  無相関/非有意 → trait交絡は支持されない。N1限定の相関はN1固有の測定要因')\n",
    "print('                  (EOG/筋電混入等、浅睡眠での不安定性) を疑うべき。')\n",
    "\n",
    "row_chi = df_trait[df_trait['predictor'] == 'abs_ΔCHI_N1'].iloc[0]\n",
    "row_spec = df_trait[df_trait['predictor'] == 'abs_ΔSpecSlope_N1'].iloc[0]\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "if row_chi['p_value'] < 0.05 and row_chi['rho'] > 0:\n",
    "    print('  -> |ΔCHI_N1| が真の薬効の大きさと有意に正相関。trait様の全般的反応性が')\n",
    "    print('     示唆される。Discussion/Limitationsで明記を検討。')\n",
    "elif row_chi['p_value'] >= 0.05:\n",
    "    print('  -> |ΔCHI_N1| は真の薬効の大きさと相関しない。trait交絡(CHI側)は支持されず、')\n",
    "    print('     N1のΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関は測定上の要因を疑うべき。')\n",
    "\n",
    "if row_spec['p_value'] < 0.05 and row_spec['rho'] > 0:\n",
    "    print('  -> |ΔSpecSlope_N1| も真の薬効の大きさと有意に正相関。SpecSlope側にも')\n",
    "    print('     同様のtrait様反応性がある可能性。')\n",
    "elif row_spec['p_value'] >= 0.05:\n",
    "    print('  -> |ΔSpecSlope_N1| は真の薬効の大きさと相関しない。')\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "aux_step6f_epoch_level_structural_coupling"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6f: エポックレベルでのCHI-SpecSlope構造的結合の検定\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 背景:\n",
    "#   Step 6c (SD比によるゲイン交絡)・6d (jackknife外れ値駆動)・6e (trait反応性)\n",
    "#   の3つがいずれも棄却された。残る主要な対立仮説は、\n",
    "#   「N1限定の測定要因 (EOG/筋電混入等)」ではなく、\n",
    "#   「CHIとSpecSlopeが、薬効・被験者・睡眠段階と無関係に、単一エポック内で\n",
    "#    数学的/構造的に相関する指標である」という可能性である\n",
    "#   (DFAスケーリング指数とPSDスロープの理論的関係: 例 Eke et al., 2000, 2002;\n",
    "#    β ≈ 2α−1 はfGn/fBm仮定下での一般的な対応関係)。\n",
    "#   後者が正しければ、被験者間Δ相関はこの構造的結合が単に伝播した結果であり、\n",
    "#   N1固有の現象ではなく全ステージ・全条件で一貫して観察されるはずである。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 方法:\n",
    "#   df_all (CHI, epoch-level) と df_nl (SpecSlope, epoch-level) を\n",
    "#   subject_nr / condition / epoch_idx でマージし、被験者・条件をプールした\n",
    "#   エポックレベルのCHI-SpecSlope相関をステージ別に計算する。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 注意 (pseudoreplication):\n",
    "#   同一被験者から数百エポックが得られるため、エポックレベルのp値は\n",
    "#   独立性の仮定に反し過大評価される。ここでのp値は参考値に過ぎず、\n",
    "#   判断は rho の大きさとステージ間の一貫性パターンで行う\n",
    "#   (正式な検定は被験者レベルのStep 6/6bに委ねる)。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "epoch_merged = pd.merge(\n",
    "    df_all[['subject_nr', 'condition', 'epoch_idx', 'stage', 'CHI']],\n",
    "    df_nl[['subject_nr', 'condition', 'epoch_idx', 'SpecSlope']],\n",
    "    on=['subject_nr', 'condition', 'epoch_idx'],\n",
    "    how='inner'\n",
    ").dropna(subset=['CHI', 'SpecSlope'])\n",
    "\n",
    "epoch_merged = epoch_merged[epoch_merged['stage'].isin(VALID_STAGES)]\n",
    "\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('エポックレベル CHI-SpecSlope相関 (被験者・条件をプール, 参考値)')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print(f'総エポック数: {len(epoch_merged):,}')\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "epoch_corr_records = []\n",
    "for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "    sub = epoch_merged[epoch_merged['stage'] == stage]\n",
    "    n = len(sub)\n",
    "    if n < 30:\n",
    "        print(f'  {stage}: n不足 (n={n})')\n",
    "        continue\n",
    "    rho, pval = spearmanr(sub['CHI'], sub['SpecSlope'])\n",
    "    epoch_corr_records.append({'stage': stage, 'n_epochs': n, 'rho': rho, 'p_value': pval})\n",
    "    print(f'  {stage:<5}: rho={rho:+.3f}  p={pval:.2e}  n_epochs={n:,}  '\n",
    "          f'(参考: 被験者数={sub[\"subject_nr\"].nunique()})')\n",
    "\n",
    "# 全ステージ・全条件プール (構造的結合仮説: ステージに依らず一貫するはず)\n",
    "rho_all, p_all = spearmanr(epoch_merged['CHI'], epoch_merged['SpecSlope'])\n",
    "print(f'\\n  全ステージ・全条件プール: rho={rho_all:+.3f}  p={p_all:.2e}  n_epochs={len(epoch_merged):,}')\n",
    "\n",
    "epoch_corr_records.append({\n",
    "    'stage': 'ALL_POOLED', 'n_epochs': len(epoch_merged), 'rho': rho_all, 'p_value': p_all\n",
    "})\n",
    "\n",
    "df_epoch_corr = pd.DataFrame(epoch_corr_records)\n",
    "epoch_corr_path = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'epoch_level_chi_specslope_correlation.csv')\n",
    "df_epoch_corr.to_csv(epoch_corr_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n結果保存: {epoch_corr_path}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('解釈の目安 (pseudoreplicationのためp値ではなくrhoの大きさ・一貫性で判断):')\n",
    "print('  全5ステージで同程度・同符号のrho (目安: |rho|の範囲が0.2以内に収まる)')\n",
    "print('    → CHIとSpecSlopeの関係は睡眠段階・薬効・被験者に依らない構造的/数学的結合')\n",
    "print('      である可能性が高い。N1固有の現象という解釈は退けられる。')\n",
    "print('  ステージ間でrhoの大きさが大きく異なる (特にN1でのみ突出)')\n",
    "print('    → 構造的結合だけでは説明できず、N1固有の測定要因という6eの結論を維持できる。')\n",
    "\n",
    "stage_rows = df_epoch_corr[df_epoch_corr['stage'] != 'ALL_POOLED']\n",
    "if len(stage_rows) == 5:\n",
    "    rho_range = stage_rows['rho'].max() - stage_rows['rho'].min()\n",
    "    same_sign = (np.sign(stage_rows['rho']) == np.sign(rho_all)).all()\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "    print(f'  5ステージ間のrho範囲: {rho_range:.3f}  (全ステージ同符号か: {bool(same_sign)})')\n",
    "    if rho_range < 0.2 and same_sign:\n",
    "        print('  -> ステージ間で一貫した中〜強程度の負の相関。構造的結合仮説を支持。')\n",
    "        print('     Discussion: SpecSlopeはCHIの独立した比較対象 (negative control) として')\n",
    "        print('     不適切であった可能性が高く、Step 6の「orthogonality」評価から除外/再定義を検討。')\n",
    "    elif rho_range >= 0.2:\n",
    "        print('  -> ステージ間でrhoの大きさに無視できない差がある。N1固有の要因の関与も')\n",
    "        print('     引き続き検討対象とすべき。')\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "aux_step6g_epoch_level_other_metrics"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6g: 他の非線形指標 (SampEn/PermEn/LZC) の\n",
    "#                    エポックレベル構造的結合チェック\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 背景:\n",
    "#   Step 6fでSpecSlopeについては、5ステージ全てでrhoが-0.48〜-0.56の\n",
    "#   狭いレンジに収まり (範囲0.071)、CHIとの構造的/数学的結合であることが\n",
    "#   示された。SpecSlopeにはDFAスケーリング指数との理論的対応関係\n",
    "#   (β ≈ 2α−1, Eke et al.) があるため、この結果自体は驚くべきものではない。\n",
    "#   一方 SampEn (Sample Entropy) / PermEn (Permutation Entropy) /\n",
    "#   LZC (Lempel-Ziv Complexity) には、CHIとの間にそのような事前の理論的\n",
    "#   対応関係は想定されていない。Step 6のもともとの目的 (CHIが他の非線形\n",
    "#   指標に対して冗長か直交か) を正しく評価するには、これら3指標についても\n",
    "#   Step 6fと同じ論法でエポックレベルの構造的結合の有無を確認しておく\n",
    "#   必要がある。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 方法: Step 6fと同一。df_all (CHI) と df_nl (SampEn/PermEn/LZC) を\n",
    "#        subject_nr/condition/epoch_idxでマージし、被験者・条件をプールした\n",
    "#        エポックレベル相関をステージ別・全体プールで算出する。\n",
    "# 注意: pseudoreplicationのためp値は参考値。判断はrhoの大きさ・一貫性で行う。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "OTHER_METRICS = ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC']\n",
    "\n",
    "epoch_merged_others = pd.merge(\n",
    "    df_all[['subject_nr', 'condition', 'epoch_idx', 'stage', 'CHI']],\n",
    "    df_nl[['subject_nr', 'condition', 'epoch_idx'] + OTHER_METRICS],\n",
    "    on=['subject_nr', 'condition', 'epoch_idx'],\n",
    "    how='inner'\n",
    ")\n",
    "epoch_merged_others = epoch_merged_others[epoch_merged_others['stage'].isin(VALID_STAGES)]\n",
    "\n",
    "epoch_corr_records_others = []\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric in OTHER_METRICS:\n",
    "    print('=' * 70)\n",
    "    print(f'エポックレベル CHI-{metric}相関 (被験者・条件をプール, 参考値)')\n",
    "    print('=' * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "    sub_all = epoch_merged_others.dropna(subset=['CHI', metric])\n",
    "    print(f'総エポック数: {len(sub_all):,}')\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "\n",
    "    stage_rhos = []\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "        sub = sub_all[sub_all['stage'] == stage]\n",
    "        n = len(sub)\n",
    "        if n < 30:\n",
    "            print(f'  {stage}: n不足 (n={n})')\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        rho, pval = spearmanr(sub['CHI'], sub[metric])\n",
    "        stage_rhos.append(rho)\n",
    "        epoch_corr_records_others.append({\n",
    "            'metric': metric, 'stage': stage, 'n_epochs': n, 'rho': rho, 'p_value': pval\n",
    "        })\n",
    "        print(f'  {stage:<5}: rho={rho:+.3f}  p={pval:.2e}  n_epochs={n:,}')\n",
    "\n",
    "    rho_all, p_all = spearmanr(sub_all['CHI'], sub_all[metric])\n",
    "    epoch_corr_records_others.append({\n",
    "        'metric': metric, 'stage': 'ALL_POOLED', 'n_epochs': len(sub_all),\n",
    "        'rho': rho_all, 'p_value': p_all\n",
    "    })\n",
    "    print(f'\\n  全ステージ・全条件プール: rho={rho_all:+.3f}  p={p_all:.2e}  '\n",
    "          f'n_epochs={len(sub_all):,}')\n",
    "\n",
    "    if len(stage_rhos) == 5:\n",
    "        rho_range = max(stage_rhos) - min(stage_rhos)\n",
    "        same_sign = all(np.sign(r) == np.sign(rho_all) for r in stage_rhos)\n",
    "        mean_abs_rho = float(np.mean(np.abs(stage_rhos)))\n",
    "        print(f'\\n  5ステージ間のrho範囲: {rho_range:.3f}  (全ステージ同符号か: {same_sign})')\n",
    "        if rho_range < 0.2 and same_sign and mean_abs_rho >= 0.3:\n",
    "            print(f'  -> {metric}もCHIと構造的に結合している可能性が高い (ステージ非依存)。')\n",
    "        elif mean_abs_rho < 0.15:\n",
    "            print(f'  -> {metric}はCHIとほぼ無相関。直交性 (incremental validity) の根拠として支持される。')\n",
    "        else:\n",
    "            print(f'  -> 中間的な関連。ステージごとの値を個別に確認すること (自動判定は非推奨)。')\n",
    "    print()\n",
    "\n",
    "df_epoch_corr_others = pd.DataFrame(epoch_corr_records_others)\n",
    "epoch_corr_others_path = os.path.join(\n",
    "    NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'epoch_level_chi_other_metrics_correlation.csv'\n",
    ")\n",
    "df_epoch_corr_others.to_csv(epoch_corr_others_path, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'結果保存: {epoch_corr_others_path}')\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- 4指標横断サマリー (SpecSlopeはStep 6fの結果 df_epoch_corr を利用) ---\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('4指標横断サマリー: CHIとのエポックレベル構造的結合 (全ステージプールrho)')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "if 'df_epoch_corr' in dir():\n",
    "    specslope_pooled = df_epoch_corr[df_epoch_corr['stage'] == 'ALL_POOLED']['rho'].values\n",
    "    if len(specslope_pooled) > 0:\n",
    "        print(f'  SpecSlope : rho={specslope_pooled[0]:+.3f}  (Step 6f; DFA-PSD理論的対応関係あり)')\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print('  (df_epoch_corr未定義: Step 6fを先に実行してください)')\n",
    "\n",
    "for metric in OTHER_METRICS:\n",
    "    row = df_epoch_corr_others[\n",
    "        (df_epoch_corr_others['metric'] == metric) & (df_epoch_corr_others['stage'] == 'ALL_POOLED')\n",
    "    ]\n",
    "    if len(row) > 0:\n",
    "        print(f'  {metric:<10}: rho={row[\"rho\"].values[0]:+.3f}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('この4指標横断表が、Step 6の本来の問い')\n",
    "print('(「CHIは他の非線形指標に対して冗長か、独立した情報を持つか」)への')\n",
    "print('最終的な回答表となる。|rho|が小さい指標のみを、真にincrementalな')\n",
    "print('比較対象としてDiscussionで扱うこと。')\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": null,
   "metadata": {
    "id": "aux_step6h_stage_demeaned_pooled_corr"
   },
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 6h: Stage-demeaned プール相関\n",
    "#                    (ステージ主効果を除去した真の「ステージ内」相関)\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 背景:\n",
    "#   Step 6gで、SampEn/PermEn/LZCはステージ間でCHIとの相関の符号自体が\n",
    "#   反転した (例: PermEn W=+0.231 vs N3=-0.462)。にもかかわらず全体プール\n",
    "#   相関 (PermEn: -0.644) はどの単一ステージのrhoよりも絶対値が大きく、\n",
    "#   これはステージ間の平均値差 (CHI・各指標とも睡眠深度で系統的に変化する)\n",
    "#   がプール相関を底上げした集約バイアス (Simpsonのパラドックスと同型) で\n",
    "#   ある可能性が高い。SpecSlope (Step 6f) はステージ内rhoが一貫していた\n",
    "#   ため問題にならなかったが、SampEn/PermEn/LZCについては、この\n",
    "#   「ステージ主効果」を除去した上で、真にステージ内で存在する平均的な\n",
    "#   関係を再評価する必要がある。\n",
    "#\n",
    "# 方法: 3つの推定量を横並びで比較する。\n",
    "#   (a) naive pooled rho        : Step 6f/6gで既に算出済み (集約バイアスを含みうる)\n",
    "#   (b) n加重ステージ内平均rho   : 各ステージのrhoをエポック数で加重平均\n",
    "#                                  (Simpsonバイアスを含まない素朴な参照値)\n",
    "#   (c) stage-demeaned pooled rho: 各エポックからステージ内平均を引いた残差\n",
    "#                                  同士のプール相関 (fixed-effect除去の簡易版、\n",
    "#                                  カテゴリカル共変量=stageとする偏相関に相当)\n",
    "#   (b)(c)が(a)と大きく乖離する指標は、naive pooled rhoがステージ主効果由来の\n",
    "#   集約バイアスであったことを意味する。\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "\n",
    "def stage_demeaned_pooled_corr(df, x_col, y_col, stage_col='stage'):\n",
    "    d = df[[stage_col, x_col, y_col]].dropna().copy()\n",
    "    d['x_dm'] = d[x_col] - d.groupby(stage_col)[x_col].transform('mean')\n",
    "    d['y_dm'] = d[y_col] - d.groupby(stage_col)[y_col].transform('mean')\n",
    "    rho, p = spearmanr(d['x_dm'], d['y_dm'])\n",
    "    return rho, p, len(d)\n",
    "\n",
    "# --- ステージ別rhoを4指標分、統一形式でまとめる (n加重平均の計算用) ---\n",
    "stage_rho_lookup = pd.concat([\n",
    "    df_epoch_corr.assign(metric='SpecSlope')[['metric', 'stage', 'n_epochs', 'rho']],\n",
    "    df_epoch_corr_others[['metric', 'stage', 'n_epochs', 'rho']],\n",
    "], ignore_index=True)\n",
    "stage_rho_lookup = stage_rho_lookup[stage_rho_lookup['stage'] != 'ALL_POOLED']\n",
    "\n",
    "def n_weighted_mean_rho(metric_name):\n",
    "    rows = stage_rho_lookup[stage_rho_lookup['metric'] == metric_name]\n",
    "    if len(rows) == 0:\n",
    "        return np.nan\n",
    "    return float(np.average(rows['rho'], weights=rows['n_epochs']))\n",
    "\n",
    "METRIC_SOURCE = {\n",
    "    'SpecSlope': (epoch_merged, 'SpecSlope', df_epoch_corr, None),\n",
    "    'SampEn':    (epoch_merged_others, 'SampEn', df_epoch_corr_others, 'SampEn'),\n",
    "    'PermEn':    (epoch_merged_others, 'PermEn', df_epoch_corr_others, 'PermEn'),\n",
    "    'LZC':       (epoch_merged_others, 'LZC', df_epoch_corr_others, 'LZC'),\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('3推定量の比較: naive pooled / n加重ステージ内平均 / stage-demeaned pooled')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "\n",
    "summary_records = []\n",
    "for metric, (df_src, col, corr_table, metric_filter) in METRIC_SOURCE.items():\n",
    "    rho_dm, p_dm, n_dm = stage_demeaned_pooled_corr(df_src, 'CHI', col)\n",
    "\n",
    "    if metric_filter is None:\n",
    "        naive_rho = corr_table[corr_table['stage'] == 'ALL_POOLED']['rho'].values[0]\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        naive_rho = corr_table[\n",
    "            (corr_table['metric'] == metric_filter) & (corr_table['stage'] == 'ALL_POOLED')\n",
    "        ]['rho'].values[0]\n",
    "\n",
    "    wmean_rho = n_weighted_mean_rho(metric)\n",
    "\n",
    "    summary_records.append({\n",
    "        'metric': metric,\n",
    "        'rho_naive_pooled': naive_rho,\n",
    "        'rho_n_weighted_stage_mean': wmean_rho,\n",
    "        'rho_stage_demeaned': rho_dm,\n",
    "        'p_stage_demeaned': p_dm,\n",
    "        'n': n_dm,\n",
    "    })\n",
    "    print(f'\\n{metric}:')\n",
    "    print(f'  naive pooled          : {naive_rho:+.3f}')\n",
    "    print(f'  n加重ステージ内平均    : {wmean_rho:+.3f}')\n",
    "    print(f'  stage-demeaned pooled  : {rho_dm:+.3f}  (p={p_dm:.2e}, n={n_dm:,})')\n",
    "\n",
    "df_summary_6h = pd.DataFrame(summary_records)\n",
    "summary_path_6h = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, 'stage_demeaned_pooled_correlation.csv')\n",
    "df_summary_6h.to_csv(summary_path_6h, index=False)\n",
    "print(f'\\n結果保存: {summary_path_6h}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "print('最終判定: CHIと各指標の「真の」構造的結合 (stage-demeaned rho基準)')\n",
    "print('=' * 70)\n",
    "for _, row in df_summary_6h.iterrows():\n",
    "    abs_rho = abs(row['rho_stage_demeaned'])\n",
    "    if abs_rho >= 0.3:\n",
    "        verdict = '構造的に結合 (CHIとほぼ冗長)'\n",
    "    elif abs_rho < 0.15:\n",
    "        verdict = '直交性の根拠あり (incrementalな比較対象として妥当)'\n",
    "    else:\n",
    "        verdict = '中間的 (弱い関連あり、要個別検討)'\n",
    "    print(f'  {row[\"metric\"]:<10}: stage-demeaned rho={row[\"rho_stage_demeaned\"]:+.3f}  -> {verdict}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('注記: naive pooled rhoとstage-demeaned rhoが大きく乖離する指標は、')\n",
    "print('      naive pooled rhoがステージ主効果由来の集約バイアスであったことを意味する。')\n",
    "print('      Discussion/論文用サマリーで報告する数値はnaive pooledではなく')\n",
    "print('      stage-demeaned rhoを用いること。')\n"
   ]
  },

    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 7: 比較図の生成\n",
    "# ステージ別 Δ(Temazepam − Placebo) を4指標について並置表示\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "NL_METRIC_LABELS = {\n",
    "    'SampEn':    'Sample Entropy',\n",
    "    'PermEn':    'Permutation Entropy',\n",
    "    'LZC':       'Lempel–Ziv Complexity',\n",
    "    'SpecSlope': 'Spectral Slope (naive aperiodic)',\n",
    "}\n",
    "\n",
    "fig_nl, axes_nl = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(14, 10), facecolor='#FFFFFF')\n",
    "axes_nl = axes_nl.flatten()\n",
    "\n",
    "for ax, metric in zip(axes_nl, ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC', 'SpecSlope']):\n",
    "    ax.set_facecolor('#FFFFFF')\n",
    "    delta_means, delta_sems, sig_labels = [], [], []\n",
    "\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",

    "        delta_means.append(sub.mean() if len(sub) > 0 else np.nan)\n",
    "        delta_sems.append(sub.sem() if len(sub) > 0 else np.nan)\n",

    "\n",
    "    colors_bar = [STAGE_COLORS[s] for s in STAGE_ORDER]\n",
    "    x = np.arange(len(STAGE_ORDER))\n",
    "    ax.bar(x, delta_means, yerr=delta_sems, color=colors_bar, alpha=0.8,\n",
    "           edgecolor='white', lw=0.5,\n",
    "           error_kw=dict(ecolor='#5A6470', capsize=4, lw=1.2))\n",
    "\n",
    "    for i, (dm, sig) in enumerate(zip(delta_means, sig_labels)):\n",
    "        if not np.isnan(dm):\n",
    "            y_off = delta_sems[i] if not np.isnan(delta_sems[i]) else 0\n",
    "            scale = abs(dm) if dm != 0 else 1\n",
    "            ax.text(i, dm + y_off + 0.02 * scale, sig, ha='center', va='bottom',\n",
    "                    color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=9)\n",
    "\n",
    "    ax.axhline(0, color='#F0E68C', ls=':', lw=0.8)\n",
    "    ax.set_xticks(x)\n",
    "    ax.set_xticklabels(STAGE_ORDER, color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "    ax.set_ylabel(f'Δ{metric} (T−P)', color='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "    ax.set_title(NL_METRIC_LABELS[metric], color='#1A1A1A', fontsize=10)\n",
    "    ax.tick_params(colors='#1A1A1A')\n",
    "    for spine in ax.spines.values():\n",
    "        spine.set_edgecolor('#CCCCCC')\n",
    "    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.15)\n",

    "# ============================================================\n",
    "# 補助解析 Step 8: 論文用サマリー出力\n",
    "# ============================================================\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "print('補助解析: CHI vs 他の非線形指標 比較 — 結果サマリー')\n",
    "print('='*70)\n",
    "print()\n",
    "\n",
    "print('─── ステージ別 Wilcoxon検定 (Temazepam vs Placebo) ───')\n",
    "print(f'{\"Metric\":<12}{\"Stage\":<6}{\"Δ mean±SD\":>20}{\"p\":>10}{\"sig\":>5}')\n",
    "print('─' * 55)\n",
    "for metric in ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC', 'SpecSlope']:\n",
    "    for stage in STAGE_ORDER:\n",
    "        row = df_stat_nl[(df_stat_nl['metric'] == metric) & (df_stat_nl['stage'] == stage)]\n",
    "        if len(row) == 0:\n",
    "            continue\n",
    "        r = row.iloc[0]\n",
    "        d_str = f'{r[\"delta_mean\"]:+.4f}±{r[\"delta_sd\"]:.4f}'\n",
    "        print(f'{metric:<12}{stage:<6}{d_str:>20}{r[\"p_value\"]:>10.4f}{r[\"sig\"]:>5}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('─── CHIとの被験者間相関 (冗長性 vs 直交性チェック) ───')\n",
    "print(df_corr_nl.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('─── SpecSlope 陰性対照 (W / N1 / REM; gain confoundチェック) ───')\n",
    "if 'df_negctrl_specslope' in dir() and len(df_negctrl_specslope) > 0:\n",
    "    print(df_negctrl_specslope.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print('  (Step 6b未実行 — chi_vs_specslope_negctrl_W_N1_REM.csv を参照)')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('─── ゲイン交絡の直接検証 (SD比 vs ΔCHI / ΔSpecSlope) ───')\n",
    "if 'df_gain_corr' in dir() and len(df_gain_corr) > 0:\n",
    "    print(df_gain_corr.to_string(index=False))\n",
    "else:\n",
    "    print('  (Step 6c未実行 — gain_proxy_vs_chi_specslope_correlation.csv を参照)')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('─── 解釈のためのチェックリスト ───')\n",
    "print('1. CHIのみがN2/N3選択的に有意')\n",
    "print('   → 選択的感度の面でCHIが優位 (既存指標では検出できない変化を捉えている)')\n",
    "print('2. 他指標もN2/N3選択的に有意 かつ ΔCHIと強く相関 (|rho|>=0.5)')\n",
    "print('   → CHIは既存指標と冗長 (新規性が乏しい可能性)')\n",
    "print('3. 他指標が有意だが ΔCHIとの相関は弱い (|rho|<0.3)')\n",
    "print('   → CHIは他指標と直交した情報を捉えている (増分的価値の根拠)')\n",
    "print('4. 他指標がいずれのステージでも非有意')\n",
    "print('   → CHIの感度の高さを支持する追加根拠')\n",
    "print('5. SpecSlopeとの相関が陰性対照 (W/N1/REM) でも同程度に強い')\n",
    "print('   → N2/N3の相関はテマゼパム薬理効果ではなく、録音条件(アンプゲイン等)')\n",
    "print('     由来の一般的な技術的共変動である疑いが強く、Limitationsへの明記が必要')\n",
    "print('6. SD比 (ゲイン交絡の代理変数) がΔSpecSlopeとは相関するがΔCHIとは相関しない')\n",
    "print('   → ΔCHI-ΔSpecSlope相関はSpecSlope側のゲイン感受性に由来する可能性が高く、')\n",
    "print('     CHI自体はゲイン交絡から独立しているという主張を直接的に補強する')\n",
    "\n",
    "n_sig_nl_by_metric = df_stat_nl[df_stat_nl['p_value'] < 0.05].groupby('metric')['stage'].apply(list)\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('各指標で nominal p<0.05 だったステージ:')\n",
    "for metric in ['SampEn', 'PermEn', 'LZC', 'SpecSlope']:\n",
    "    stages_sig = n_sig_nl_by_metric.get(metric, [])\n",
    "    print(f'  {metric:<10}: {stages_sig if len(stages_sig) > 0 else \"なし\"}')\n",
    "\n",
    "print()\n",
    "print('結果ファイル:')\n",
    "for f in ['all_epochs_nonlinear.csv', 'nonlinear_within_subject_wide.csv',\n",
    "          'wilcoxon_results_nonlinear.csv', 'chi_vs_nonlinear_correlation.csv',\n",
    "          'chi_vs_specslope_negctrl_W_N1_REM.csv',\n",
    "          'gain_proxy_vs_chi_specslope_correlation.csv',\n",
    "          'nonlinear_comparison_by_stage.png']:\n",
    "    p = os.path.join(NLCOMPARE_OUTPUT_DIR, f)\n",
    "    exists = '✓' if os.path.exists(p) else '✗'\n",
    "    print(f'  {exists} {p}')\n"
